DhPr_1.1–1.2	sūtra abhidharma vinayāḥ sugatasya vācaḥ bādhā vinā adbhuta tayā satatam jayanti ābhānti darpaṇaḥ iva pratibimbitāni tattvāni yatra sakalasya padārtha rāśeḥ śrī dharma kīrtti abhimukhāni jagat hitāni dharma uttarasya vipulāni padāni amūni samyak prakāśya sukṛtam samupārjayāmi tena api duḥkha jaladheḥ jagat uddharāmi mātsarya ādi mala upetaiḥ śakyam na guṇa darśanam yatas hema parīkṣāyāḥ santaḥ hi nikaṣa upalāḥ 
DhPr_1.3	 nyāya binduṭīkām cikīrṣuḥ eṣa dharma uttaraḥ bhagavat pūjā puṇyayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvam atīndriyam īdṛśi viṣaye gati antara virahāt abhyupeya prāmāṇyāt āgamāt avagamya puṇyasya ca apuṇya virodhi tvāt apuṇya phala vidhna ādi abhāvaḥ vyāpaka viruddha vidhinā sambhavī tena avidhnena grantha karaṇa tad samāptau tad adhyayane ca bhagavat guṇa gaṇa śravaṇa janita atiśaya viśeṣa āsādita puṇyasya tathā eva avidhnena jijñāsita śāstra artha tattva avagamaḥ bhaviṣyati dṛṣṭa śiṣṭa ācāra upi anupālitaḥ bhaviṣyati iti abhisandhāya vāc vijaya ākhyāna dvārām bhagavataḥ pūjām stuti mayīm ārabhate 
DhPr_2.1	 syāt etat pūjāyāḥ puṇya upajanana mātra prayojanasya sampādaka tvāt āripsita ārambhāt prāk kāya mayīm eva iṣṭa devatā pūjā māracayya kim iti na tadā ārabhyate atha ucyate tad pūrvikāyām api pravṛttau stuti pūjā eva pravṛtti puraḥsarī kinna kṛtā iti ca udyam āpadyeta tathā ca aśoka vanikā codya sadṛśam idam iti na anuvādyam api viduṣām iti asat etat evam hikāya pūjāyāḥ āracane stuti padāni prayuñjān asyā atad vyākhyāna bhūtasya asya ślokasya aprakṛtasya karaṇam na āpadyeta kāya pūjā tu sukha āsana upadeśana ādīti karttavyatā sthānīya tvāt na aprakṛta karaṇa codyena upadrūyate iti 
DhPr_2.2^1	 atra ucyate syāt eva etat yadi sva artham uddiśya stutiḥ īdṛśī pūjā vidhīyate kim tarhi śrotṛ jana artham uddiśya api bhagavataḥ guṇa kīrttane kṛte śrotṛbhiḥ antatas kāvya guṇa jijñāsayā api ślokaḥ avaśyam jñātavyaḥ tad jñānāt tathāgata guṇāḥ tāvat kālam tāvat śotṛ santānam adhyāsate tatra ye tāvat bhagavati prāc ati prasanna manasaḥ teṣām evaṃvidha guṇa atiśaya śālini sthānaḥ eva asmākam manaḥ prasannam iti niścinvatām sthemānam āsādayati cittam ye ca madhyasthāḥ teṣām evaṃbhūta guṇa ratna alaṅkṛte mahataḥ mahīyasi cittam āvarjayitum ucitam sva hita avahitaiḥ tat vayam iyantam kālam pramādyante eva udāsmahe smaḥ iti nirvidyamānānām cittam atimattam pratiṣṭhate 
DhPr_2.2^2	 ye api anatiprasannāḥ teṣām api evaṃvidha guṇa niketane kim asmābhiḥ akasmāt vidviṣyate iti mananā anma nāgāvarjanam mādhyasthyam vā syāt iti atiprasanna madhya sthayoḥ puruṣayoḥ citta prasāda sthairya manaḥ prasāda upajananābhyām puṇya atiśayaḥ jāyate tṛtīyasya api manāgauvarjanepi puṇya prasavaḥ mādhyasthye tu bhagavat vidveṣa upacaya upaneya narakeṣu anatipatanam vidveṣa upaśamāt bhavati asatyām tu stuti maya pūjāyām ittham trividha śrotṛ jana prayojanam yat tat na kṛtam syāt iti sva para artha uddeśena stuti mayī pūjā vidhīyate iti sthitam 
DhPr_2.3–2.6	 tatra anena ślokena bhagavān sva artha sampadā para artha sampad u pāya sampadā para artha sampadā ca stūyate tāsām tisṛṇām api sampadām avaśya vaktavya tvāt tathā hi cira kāla abhyāsa sātmyī kṛta mahā kṛpasya bhagavataḥ para artha sampad pradhānam prayojanam itarada pradhānam ānuṣaṅgikam tathāgata tvam api iti sā tāvat avaśya abhidheyā tat āha bhaṭṭa varāhasvāmī sākṣātkṛta aśeṣa jagat svabhāvam prāsaṅgikam yasya tathāgata tvam iti sā ca upāya sampadam antareṇa asambhavinī iti tad abhidhānam api āvaśyakam iyañcān adhigata svātha sampadaḥ na sidhyati iti tad abhidhānam api niyatam āpatitam tat āha saḥ eva 
DhPr_2.7	 tatra sva artha sampannasya para artha sampādana upāya sampad tad sādhyā ca para artha sampādana sampad iti prathamam jāti ityādinā sugatasya iti antena sva artha sampattiḥ uktāḥ anupāyasya para artha sampattiḥ na sampadyate iti tadanu vācaḥ iti anena para artha upāya sampad uktā īdṛśam vastunaḥ rūpam idañcā anuṣṭheyam ityādi rūpeṇa dharma deśanā eva hi bhagavataḥ jagat hita avagamana lakṣaṇa para artha sampādana upāya sampad vaidya varasya iva vyādhi svarūpa pratīti śakti bhaiṣajya upadeśaḥ roga upaśama sampādana upāya sampad tad anantaram tad upāya sampatti sādhyā para artha sampadanyena padena uktā 
DhPr_3.1	 tatra vācaḥ jayanti iti sambandhaḥ avivakṣita karma tvāt akarma tvam vācaḥ sūtra abhidharma vinaya lakṣaṇāḥ jayanti utkṛṣyante prakṛṣṭāḥ bhavanti utkarṣaḥ ca sajātīya apekṣayā iti sāmarthyāt īśvara ādi vacanebhyaḥ prakṛṣṭāḥ bhavanti iti arthaḥ yat vā jayanti abhibhavanti abhibhavaḥ ca pratiyogi gocaraḥ iti arthāt tīrthika śāstra abhibhavam kurvanti iti arthaḥ pramāṇa upapanna artha pratipādaka tvāt āsām teṣām tu tad vaiparītyāt iti buddhi siddham kṛtvā kevalam etat atra uktam viniścaya ṭīkāyām punar anena yukti prabhāva ityādi hetu bhāvena viśeṣaṇam upāttam 
DhPr_3.2	 kasya tāḥ iti ākāṅkṣāyām āha sugatasya iti su śabdaḥ ayam artha traya vṛttiḥ draṣṭavyaḥ praśastam gataḥ sugataḥ praśastam yathā bhavati tathā gataḥ saṃsārāt prakrāntaḥ katham tathā gamanam tasya nairātmya darśanena saṃsāra atikramāt tasya ca prajñā niśrayāt athavā gati arthānām jñāna artha tvāt api praśastam gataḥ jñātavān iti arthaḥ praśaḥ tañca tat tattvam nairātmya lakṣaṇam tattva rūpa tvañca tasya pramāṇa upapanna tvāt dṛṣṭaḥ ca ayam su śabdaḥ praśasta artha vṛttiḥ surūpā rūpājīva iti yathā apunarāvṛttyā vā gataḥ sugataḥ gataḥ prayātaḥ saṃsārāt punarāvṛtti śabda vācyayoḥ janma doṣayoḥ ātma darśana bīja upaghātena bhagavatā sa mūla ghātam nihata tvāt etad arthepi su śabdaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sunayaḥ jvaraḥ iti yathā niḥśeṣam vā gataḥ sugataḥ niḥśeṣam yāvat gantavyam tāvat gataḥ prāptaḥ akleśa nirjara kāya vāc buddhi vaiguṇya lakṣaṇa śeṣa lakṣaṇa prahāṇena muneḥ tad pada prāpteḥ evaṃvṛttiḥ api su śabdaḥ dṛśyate su pūrṇaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti yathā 
DhPr_3.3	 tasya sugatasya kimbhūtasya iti āha vijetuḥ abhibhavituḥ kasya asau vijetā iti āha jagataḥ jīva lokasya vijayaḥ ca jagat apekṣayā parama pada prāptyā tasya prakṛṣṭa tvam draṣṭavyam atas eva jagat abhibhūtam bhavati tasya tad vaiparītyāt na punā rāja vijayaḥ iva rāja antara apekṣayā kāya ādi tiraskāraḥ abhibhavaḥ avaseyaḥ 
DhPr_3.4	 jagataḥ kīdṛśasya jāyate saṃsarati anayā iti jātiḥ tṛṣṇā vyasyate vividhena prakāreṇa itaḥ tatas asyatekṣipyate anena iti asyati iti vā vyasanam jātiḥ eva vyasanam iti antar nīta niyamaḥ samāsaḥ karttavyaḥ tṛṣyan= eva hi prāṇī tat tat ācarati yena saṃsāre saṃsarati tatas tayā eva asau itas tatas utpāda dvāreṇa vyastaḥ kṣiptaḥ bhavati iti sā eva vyasanam yuktam athavā jātau utpattau nikāya viśiṣṭāyām vyasanam āsaktiḥ vidyādharaḥ aham bhūyāsam devaḥ aham bhūyāsam iti ādi ākāraḥ abhiniveśaḥ yat vā jāti āśritāni vyasanāni duḥkhāni roga śoka ādīni prāktana vyākhyāne tasya antim avyākhyāne teṣām prabandhaḥ pravāhaḥ tat eva vā prakṛṣṭaḥ bandhaḥ pravāha pakṣe prabandhena bandha pakṣe prabandhasya prasūteḥ kāraṇasya evañca prabandha prasūti śruti sahitam hetu padam upādadānaḥ paramata nirākaraṇañca abhipraiti tathā hi evam abhidhāne sati ayam tātparyāthaḥ jagat eva ananya sattvanā iyam svayam eva tathā tat tat ācarati yena tathā saṃsāre saṃsarati na tu para preritam yathā anye manyante 
DhPr_4.1–4.2	 itarathā jāti vyasana āśrayasya iti tad anya viśeṣaṇa sahitam eva brūyāt iti kimbhūtasya sugatasya rāga ādīnām kleśānām arāteḥ śatroḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi vigamena tena teṣām sva santāne sa mūlam unmūlita tvāt yatas eva bhagavān rāga ādi arātiḥ jagat ca jāti vyasana prabandha prasūti hetuḥ atas eva asau tatas prakṛṣṭaḥ bhavati vijetā tasya athavā rāga ādi arāteḥ iti jagataḥ viśeṣaṇam rāga ādayaḥ arātayaḥ pratipakṣā nityam upaghātakāḥ yasya iti kṛtvā tadā tu tad vijetā bhagavān sugata tvāt eva boddhavyaḥ jagataḥ ye rāga ādayaḥ teṣām arāteḥ iti ādi vyākhyānam tu kliṣṭa tvāt na uktam 
DhPr_4.3–4.4	 kiṃviśiṣṭā vācaḥ iti āha manaḥ ityādi sat asat artha viveka vibandhaka tvāt tamaḥ iva tanaḥ ajñānam avidyā tat ca manasaḥ vikalpa vijñānasya kayācid vyapekṣayā dharmaḥ iva bhinnaḥ kathyate vastutas tu kliṣṭam eva jñānam avidyā yat vā kliṣṭam manaḥ eva tamaḥ iva tamaḥ pūrvavat kecid tu manaḥ tamaḥ iti śabda samudāyam ajñāna artha vācakam ācakṣate 
DhPr_4.5	 tasya tānavam tanu tvam mandībhavanam iti arthāt tat ādadhānāḥ kurvāṇāḥ tān avagrahaṇena ca idam ācaṣṭe na bhagavataḥ vācaḥ sarvathā jagat ajñānam upadhnanti tad śravaṇa mātreṇa moha hānyāḥ mukta tvāt mārga bhāva nā vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt kintu kiyantam kālam ālā ucyamānāḥ samudācārataḥ mohasya māndya āpādanena tam tanūkurvanti iti 
DhPr_4.6–4.7	 athavā anyathā vyākhyāyate tāḥ vācaḥ tamaḥ jayanti abhibhavanti moha pracāram ādadhānāḥ śeṣam samānam pūrveṇa yat vā manasi tamaḥ yasya sa manaḥ tamā mūḍhaḥ uktaḥ tasya bhāvaḥ manaḥ tamaḥ tāḥ tasyāḥ anavaḥ niṣṭhā tathā hi nūtiḥ navaḥ tad viruddhena tam ādadhānāḥ mūḍha tva pravarttanāt śeṣam samānam pūrveṇa iti vyākhyātaḥ ślokaḥ 
DhPr_4.8–5.1	 kevalam idam ālā ucyatām tathāgatam abhistuvatā dharma uttareṇa asya eva vijayaḥ mukhya vṛttyā kim na kathitaḥ kim punar dharmi viśeṣaṇa tvena anuṣaṅgataḥ pratipāditaḥ iti atra samādhīyate ācāya śrī dharma kīrttinā bhagavat pravacana artha samarthana prakṛta tvāt vijayaḥ mukhyatas pratipādyate yat vā yasya vācaḥ eva tathā jayanti tasya vijayaḥ daṇḍāt jaya nyāyena atiśayena pratipāditaḥ sūcitaḥ ca asau vijetṛ padena athavā aagamikānām matena nirupadhi śeṣe nirvāṇa dhātau parinirvṛtaḥ bhagavān parinirvṛtasya asya pravacana mayam eva vapuḥ vidyate iti āgamikaḥ vāc vijayam eva pratipādayate sma iti 
DhPr_5.2	 samyak jñāna ityādinā prakaraṇasya yat prayojanam samyak jñāna vyutpattiḥ tasyāḥ yat prayojanam puruṣa artha siddhi rūpam tat ucyate na ca samyak jñāna vyutpatteḥ samyak jñāna parijñānam prayojanam na puruṣa artha siddhiḥ iti śakyam abhidhātum vipratipatti nirākaraṇena svarūpa pratipattiḥ arā iva hi samyak jñānasya vyutpattiḥ sā katham ātmanaḥ eva prayojanam bhavet iti abhiprāyeṇa vyākhyātavantau vinīta deva śānta bhadrau tat vyākhyānam avamanyamānaḥ abhidheya prayojanam ucyate iti vyācaṣṭe avajñāne ca ayam āśayaḥ asya idam prayojanam iti khalu anvaya vyatirekābhyām avadhāryate na anyathā iyañca svarūpā puruṣa artha siddhiḥ samyak jñāna vyutpattim antareṇa api gopāla aṅganā ādīnām bhavantī sati samyak jñāne satyām api tad vyutpattau asati samyak jñāne manīṣiṇām abhavantī na tad vyutpatteḥ anvaya vyatirekau= anuvidhatte kintarhi samyak jñānasya iti tasya eva prayojanam bhavitum arhati iti 
DhPr_5.3–5.4	 samyak jñāna ityādinā vākyena karaṇena prakaraṇa abhidheyasya samyak jñāna lakṣaṇasya prayojanam dṛṣṭam puruṣa artha siddhi lakṣaṇam ucyate vārttika kṛtā kartrā iti arthāt nanu ca yatra abhidhā vyāpāraḥ samāpyate sa vākya arthaḥ na ca asau puruṣa artha siddhau viśrāmyati kim tarhi śrotuḥ samyak jñāna vyutpattau tat katham sā vākya artha tvena ucyate ucyate yadi api śabda abhidhā vyāpāra apekṣayā tat samyak jñānam vyutpādyate śiṣya iti śiṣya samyak jñāna viṣayā vyutpatti kriyā prādhānyāt vākya arthaḥ tathā api asya tātparya artha sambhave tad nirūpaṇena idam ucyate tathā hi tad vyutpattim eva asau kim ati kāryate yatas samyak jñāna pūrvikā sarva puruṣa artha siddhiḥ mucyate yatra punar abhidhā viṣaye eva arthaḥ sambhavī na tu tātparyārthaḥ statra saḥ eva vākya arthaḥ kalpyate dvitaya sambhave tu yat param vākyam tathā ca tasya arthaḥ iti a arthena nyāyena abhidheyasya prayojanam puruṣātha siddhiḥ vākya artha tvena ucyate iti vyākhyāyate iti 
DhPr_5.5^1	 kecid punar idam dharma uttarīyam vākyam anyathā vyācakṣate na atra prayojana śabdena phalam abhipretam kintu prayujyate pravarttyate anena iti prayojayati iti vā prayojanam tat ca puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam abhidheyasya hi samyak jñānasya puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvena prayuktaḥ puruṣaḥ pravarttate iti uttaratra api prayojanam idam eva vivakṣitam atas eva atra ca ityādi vākye sarva puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam prayojanam pravarttakam uktam iti spaṣṭīkaraṇam ghaṭataḥ iti tat ca na ati śliṣṭam utpaśyāmaḥ 
DhPr_5.5^2–6.1	 tathā hi atra ca prakaraṇa abhidheyasya samyak jñānasya puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam prayojanam uktam iti vakṣyamāṇena vyaktīkṛta tvāt iha api abhidheyasya prayojanam iti ṣaṣṭhī tatpuruṣaḥ avaśya kāryaḥ tathā ca ayam asamarthaḥ pada vidhiḥ bhavet tat hi puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam na abhidheyasya samyak jñānasya pravarttakam api tu puruṣasya tat katham abhidheya padena samasyeta prayojana padam na ca kenacid rūpeṇa abhidheya sambandhi tva asya samarthayoḥ eka arthībhāvaḥ bhavati iti na hi yajñadatta putraḥ bhṛtya tva ādinā rūpeṇa devadatta sambandhī bhavan devadatta putraḥ iti ṣaṣṭhī samāsasya viṣayaḥ bhavitum arhati atha bhāva pradhāna tvāt nirdeśasya prayojanam prayojaka tvam iti arthaḥ tat ca āśritasya prayojaka tayā bhavati sambandhi iti samartha vidhiḥ kalpyate 
DhPr_6.2	 nanu yadi samyak jñāna gatam puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam prayojanam prayojaka tvam tarhi samyak jñānam prayojanam iti āpannam yatas na prayojana tvam eva prayojanam bhavitum arhati na ca samyak jñānena prayuktaḥ pu ṣaḥ samyak jñāne pravarttate kintu puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvena tat katham prayojanam bhavitum arhati kiñca vṛddha vyavahāraḥ hi śabda artha vyavahāra bhūmiḥ na ca vṛddhaiḥ prayojakaḥ sati api prayojayitṛ tve prayojanam ucyate anyathā samyak jñānam vyutpadyamānānām ātmānam vyutpādakam karttum pravarttamānaḥ ācāryaḥ prayojakaḥ iti samyak jñāna vyutpatteḥ prayojanamucyeta yaḥ api kaṭam kurvantam karttum prayuṅkte saḥ api tat prayojanamucyeta iti evaṃvādī na laukikaḥ na parīkṣakaḥ iti upekṣaṇīyaḥ eva 
DhPr_6.3	 api ca kim etat anyathā na upapadyate eva yena evam mṛtvā śīrtvā upapādyeta na ca evam anyathā api sūpa pāda tvāt prayojaka tvam iti nirddeśe ca dharma uttaraḥ kim gauravam paśyati yena evam avācakam ācakṣīta kathañca prakaraṇasya iti durupapādam prayuñjīta kiñca yadi īpsañji hāsan vā puruṣaḥ pravarttate tad upādāna parityāgābhyām pravarttitaḥ bhavati yathā āha akṣapādaḥ yam artham adhikṛtya pravarttate tat prayojanam iti adhikṛtya uddiśya iti arthaḥ na ca samyak jñānasya bhinnam sat api puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam īpsan jihāsan vā pravarttate kintarhi hita ahita prāpti parihārau= uddiśya iti tau= eva prayojane yukte kiñcid ajihāsoḥ anupāditsoḥ artha nirīhasya sati api puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tve apravarttanāt smaraṇāt abhilāṣeṇa vyavahāraḥ pravarttate iti alam śabda mātra samarthana dṛṣṭeḥ artha tattvān avagāhinaḥ vacane andha ādareṇa 
DhPr_6.4–6.5	 atha abhidheya prayojanam pravarttakam iti samasyate tatas ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced tad avadyam na hi puruṣātha siddhi hetu tvena prayuktaḥ puruṣaḥ samyak jñāna lakṣaṇe abhidheye pravarttate kintu prakaraṇe pravarttate grantha śravaṇa lakṣaṇām pravṛttim anutiṣṭhati atha granthasya śabda artha svabhāva tvāt evam api asau śabde abhidheye ca samudāye pravṛttaḥ bhavati tat granthasya prakaraṇasya iti ṣaṣṭhī katham atha punar ayam arthaḥ asya prakaraṇasya abhidheye arthāt abhidhāna abhidheya samudāye prayojanam pravarttakam iti tathā ca prakaraṇasya prakaraṇe pravarttakam iti asaṅgatam uktam syāt yadi ca uktayā vyutpattyā prayojana śabdena prayojakam tathābhūtam asya bubodhayiṣitam bhavet tadā samyak jñāna pūrvikā ityādinā abhidheya prayojanam ucyate iti uktam syāt mukhyaḥ ca sambandhī puruṣaḥ puruṣasya iti darśitaḥ syāt na ca evam tasmāt prayojana śabdena phalam eva asya abhipretam atra uttaratra api 
DhPr_6.6	 atha ucyate phala arthī ced pratipattā phalaḥ eva kim na pravarttate ki śramaḥ samyak jñānaḥ iti heya upādeyayoḥ hāna upādāna lakṣaṇa phala arthitā eva tad nibandhanam jñānam mṛgayate anyathā visaṃvādanam ātmīyam āśaṅkamānaḥ iti kā kṣatiḥ phala pakṣe tu puruṣa pravṛtti upayogi ca asya abhidheyam iti tat darśitam bhavati 
DhPr_7.1	 nanu ca na ayam pratyasta mita avayava arthaḥ saṃjñā śabdaḥ kim tarhi prayujyate anena iti prayojayati iti vā vyutpattyā phale api varttate tat katham etat vyākhyāyate iti ced satyam etat kevalam na puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam samyak jñānasya ātmanaḥ eva prayojakam kintu puruṣasya tatra ca uktā doṣa mātrā abhidheye prayojanam iti vigrahe ca bhūyān doṣaḥ darśitaḥ tasmāt tathābhūta vyutpattinā api prayojana śabdena atra na tathābhūtam prayojakam vācyam api tu phalam eva iti sarvam avadātam 
DhPr_7.2	 nanu ca prakaraṇe śrotṛt pravivarttayiṣuḥ ayam abhidheya prayojanam abhidhatte tad anena asya eva tat ākhyātum ucitam tat ca yathāsvam abhidheya pratyāyana lakṣaṇam iti āśaṅkya āha dvividham hi ityādi hiḥ yasmāt dvi prakāram prakaraṇasya śarīram svabhāvaḥ tat uktam kāvya alaṅkāre śabda arthau sahitau kāvyam iti tasmāt abhidheya prayojanam ucyate iti 
DhPr_7.3–7.4	 katham dvaividhyam iti āha śabdaḥ iti caḥ śabdena saha artham prakaraṇa śarīra tvena samuccinoti etat uktam bhavati śabda arthayoḥ avacchedyāvacchedaka tvena sthitayoḥ prakaraṇa tvam na anyathā iti ubhaya svabhāva tvāt prakaraṇasya abhidheya prayojana abhidhāne prakaraṇasya eva abhihitam bhavati iti yadi evam śarīra tva aviśeṣāt abhidheyasya iva abhidhāna ātmanā upi tat kinnā ucyate kiñca na niṣkṛṣṭa rūpe abhidheye puruṣaḥ pravarttate kintu granthaḥ eva śravaṇa lakṣaṇām pravṛttim ācarati abhidheya jñānāya tat asya eva prayojanam vācyam iti pūrva pakṣa dvitayam paśyan= āha tatra iti nirdhāraṇe ca etat na anyat iti puruṣa pravṛtti upayogi 
DhPr_7.5	 ayam asya āśayaḥ na hi śabdasya sva artha pratyāyana lakṣaṇam phalam asti iti śabda sandarbhaḥ ārabhyate śrūyate vā tasya kāka danta parīkṣā sādhāraṇa tvena agaṇyamāna tvāt kintarhi tad arthasya sa prayojana tvena atas kim anena uktena api iti tarhi abhidheyasya api tat kim ucyate iti āha abhidheyam tu ityādi turabhidhānāt abhidheyam bheda vat darśayati api śabdaḥ na ārambhaṇīyaḥ iti asmāt paraḥ draṣṭavyaḥ tat ayam arthaḥ tad pratipattaye śabdānām sandarbhaḥ na ārambhaṇīyaḥ api syāt kim punar śravaṇīyaḥ iti 
DhPr_8.1–8.3	 yathā iti sāmānyena uktasya arthasya viṣaya upadarśane yathā etat darśitam tadvat sarvam draṣṭavyam iti yathā śabda arthaḥ tad parīkṣeti īkṣa ittham itthañcā iti karma upadeśaḥ pada saṃhatiḥ iti ca buddhi stham parīkṣaṇam vā parīkṣā vimṛṣya avadhāraṇam tādarthyāt śāstram api tathā nanu niṣprayojana abhidheyam mārambhi vacanena tu anena kim kriyate iti āha tasmāt ityādi yasmāt niṣprayojana abhidheyam na ārabhyate tasmāt ārambhaṇīya tvam darśayatā ārambha yogyam eva idam mayā ārabhyate iti prakāśayatā ārambhaṇīya tve ca darśite śravaṇīya tvam api nimitta sāmyāt darśitam bhavati iti te pravarttitāḥ bhavanti 
DhPr_8.4^1	 nanu ca samyak jñāna pūrvikā sarva puruṣa artha siddhiḥ iti anena eka deśena abhidheya prayojanam uvatam na samuditena tat katham anena vākyena ucyate iti ucyate ucyate vākyam hi nāma ekasmin= arthe prādhānyena pratipādye guṇa guṇi bhāvam anubhavatām artha dvāreṇa anyonya apekṣiṇām sambaddhānām padānām samūhaḥ ucyate tatra yadi sarveṣām padārthānām prādhānyam syāt tadā parasparān upakārāt sambandhaḥ eva padānām na syāt iti vākya rūpa tā eva hīyeta iti sūktam anena iti abhidheya prayojana abhidhānam eva asya samyak jñāna ityādi pada samūha ātmakasya yathā tathā yasmāt ityādinā kaṇṭha uktam karoti 
DhPr_8.4^2	 tasya samyak jñānasya pratipattaye śiṣyasya iti arthāt etat ca tat vyutpādyate iti asya sāmarthya avasthita artha kathanam draṣṭavyam itinā vākya arthasya svarūpam idamā ca buddhi siddha tvena tat eva aṅgulī vyapadeśa yogyam iva darśayati anena ca puruṣa artha siddheḥ upeya tvāt prādhānyam pratipādyamānasya ca samyak jñānasya tad upāya tvāt aprādhānyam atas eva ca arthena nyāyena puruṣa artha siddheḥ vākya artha tvam śābdyā tu vṛttyā śiṣya samyak jñāna viṣayā vyutpatti kriyā vākya arthaḥ iti darśitam 
DhPr_8.5	 nanu samyak jñāna ityādinā vākyena samyak jñānasya puruṣa artha siddhau hetu bhāvaḥ param pradarśitaḥ na punar idam tasya prayojanam iti darśitam tasya eva prayojanam anena ucyate iti ca uktam tat katham yujyate atha ca etāvatā api na jñāyate kasya kim tad abhidheyam kiñca tasya prayojanam iti āśaṅkya āha atra ca ityādi 
DhPr_8.6	 atha samyak jñānasya puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam prayojanam iti avadyam mūla virodhāt yukti virodhāt ca tathā hi puruṣa artha siddhim eva ācāryī iyam samyak jñāna ityādi vacanam prayojanam anujānāti na tu puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam avayava artha vyākhyāne tasya tām eva prayojana tayā vyaktīkariṣyati na ca hetu tvam hatoḥ bhinnam iṣyate yujyate vā tat katham asya eva samyak jñānasya prayojanam bhaviṣyati na ca atra prayojanam prayojakam vācyam ukta nyāyāt iha api pravṛtti sambandhinaḥ upādāna prasaṅgāt ca na ca rāja śāsanam sāmānyam kiñcid asti yena bhāva pradhānaḥ prayojana śabdaḥ kalpyeta tat iṣṭau pūrva uktam dūṣaṇam parāvartteta iti 
DhPr_9.1–9.2	 satyam na puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam samyak jñānasya prayojanam abhipretam kintarhi puruṣa artha siddhiḥ eva aśābdikā asau katham ucyatām iti ced ucyate caśabdaḥ atra yasmāt arthe tatas yasmāt prakaraṇa abhidheyasya samyak jñānasya puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam uktam tasmāt prayojanam uktam iti dvis āvartanīyam tad ca atra arthāt puruṣa artha siddhiḥ eva avatiṣṭhate samyak jñānasya tām prati hetu tva uktau ca sā prayojana muktā iti kim sākṣāt vācakena padena kriyate iti bhāvaḥ etāvatā eva tāvat idam samādhīyate bahavaḥ punar atra āyāsyanti 
DhPr_9.3–9.4	 sarvā puruṣa artha siddhiḥ yatas hetu tvāt tat sarva puruṣa artha siddhi tathāvidham hetu tvam yatra prayojanam tat tathā tat ca puruṣa artha siddhiḥ eva iti anayā vyutpattyā anena śabdena sā eva uktā kasya tādṛśam iti apekṣāyām idam uktam prakaraṇa abhidheyasya samyak jñānasya iti kecid prattipadyante anye tu arśā ādi tve prayojanam asya asti iti matu arthīya matam vidhāya pradhāna vat nirdeśam vivakṣitvā prayojanavat tvam iti pratijānate evam ca artham samarthayanti yatas eva puruṣa artha siddhiḥ samyak jñāna sādhyā tatas eva sā prayojanam tasya api yat eva tām prati hetu tvam tat eva prayojanavat tvam iti 
DhPr_9.5–9.7	 eke tu yatas samyak jñāne sati puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam vyavasthāpyate tatas pramāṇa phala vat vyavasthāpya vyavasthāpana bhāvam āśritya it am uktam tatas na kiñcid avadyam iti manyante apare tu caśabdam bhinnakramam kṛtvā puruṣa artha siddhi hetu tvam uktam prayojanam ca uktam iti yojayanti itare tu puruṣa artha siddhi hetu śabdena kāraṇe kāryam upacarya puruṣa artha siddhim eva abhidadhati ananya upāya sādhya tā darśana artham ca upacāra karaṇam samādadhate 
DhPr_9.8–9.10	 kecid tu nibandha kṛtaḥ kathañcid api idam samarthayitum anīśānāḥ sahita śabda pātāt pramāda pāṭhe eva iti varṇayanti atra sāra asāram santaḥ eva vivecayiṣyanti syāt etat yathā pravṛtti aṅgatayā abhidheya prayojanam ucyate tadvat sambandha ādikam api kim na ucyate iti āha asmin= ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe katham punar anyasya uktau= anyat uktam bhavati iti āha tathā hi iti nipāta samudāyaḥ ca ayam yasmāt iti asya arthe sarvatra varttate 
DhPr_10.1–10.4	 puruṣa arthaḥ heya upādeya hāna upādāna lakṣaṇaḥ upayogaḥ vyāpāraḥ saḥ asya asti iti tathā evam sati kim siddham iti āha tasmāt iti tad śabdena anantara uktaḥ vākya arthaḥ pratyavamraṣṭavyaḥ abhidheya bhāgaḥ aṅgaḥ eka deśaḥ sambandha ādi bhāga apekṣayā sambandha ādi ityādi grahaṇena abhidheya prayojanayoḥ saṃgrahaḥ uktāni iti uktāni iva uktāni prakāśitāni na tu tatrā abhidhā asya sambhavinī 
DhPr_10.5–10.6	 atha abhidheya prayojanam yathā vākyena sākṣāt ucyate tathā sambandha ādīni api kinna ucyante iti āha na tu iti turavadhārayati viśinaṣṭi vā ayam āśayaḥ yadi sarvepadārthāḥ prādhānyam aśnu vīran vākyam eva tadā viśīryeta anyonyā avyapekṣā bhāvena eka artha apratyāyanāt tatas vākyam eka artham abhidheya tayā upādātum kalpyate na anekam 
DhPr_10.7	 yadi sākṣāt na samartham katham na asamartham atha asamartham eva na sākṣāt samartham iti tarhi na vācyam iti āha ekam tu iti turatra api vat grāhyaḥ sākṣāt vācya tvena ekam vyavacchinatti darśayati prakāśayati tatra vākyasya abhidhā vyāpāra asaṃbhavāt atas eva uktāni iva uktāni iti tathā asmābhiḥ vyākhyātam anyathā tat anena virudhyeta 
DhPr_10.8	 nanu yadi nāma abhidheya ādikam vākyasya prakāśyam na abhidheyam tathā api padārthena tena avaśyam bhāvyam tathā ca kasya kim vācakam padam iti āśaṅ kyāha tatra ityādi teṣu abhidheya ādiṣu tat iti dvitīya antam etat yatas vyutpādyate iti atra lakāraḥ prayojya karmaṇi vihitaḥ na prayojya kriyā karmaṇi iti vākye api loke padyate gamyate anenā arthaḥ iti vyutpattyā pada prayogaḥ dṛśyate tatas vyutpādyate iti prayojana padam iti āha anyathā pada vṛndam idam na padam yat vā vyutpādyate iti atra iti draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_11.1–11.3	 nanu uktam prayojanam puruṣa artha siddhiḥ tat kim punar cintyate kathañca tat anyathā ucyate iti āha prayojanam ca atra iti caḥ vaktavya antara samuccaye tat ayam arthaḥ na uktam prayojanam iti cintyate kintu guṇa bhūta artha prayojaka padasya vyutpādyate iti asya prayojanam tad vyutpattiḥ kriyate iti ṇicaḥ kim prayojanam iti praśne tasya prayojanam cintyate iti yāvat atra iti guṇa bhūta artha nirūpaṇe prakaraṇa karaṇam eva vyāpāraḥ nanu kasmāt iyam āśaṅkā vaktrā kimartham kriyate śrotṛbhiḥ ca kimartha śrūyate iti tau khalu evam eva pravartteyātām iti āśaṅkya āha tathā hi iti yasmāt 
DhPr_11.4	 atha katham ubhayoḥ vyutpādanam prayojanam ucyate yadi atas vyutpadyate tasya vyutpattiḥ prayojanam yaḥ tu vyutpādayati tasya vyutpādanam iti na etat asti prayojaka vyāpāravatī hi vyutpattiḥ prayojanam iṣṭa iti ubhayoḥ vyutpādanam eva prayojanam kevalam ekaḥ anyathā pravarttate anyaḥ ca anyathā katham nāma mad vyāpāra vaśena śrotṛ santāna varttinī vyutpattiḥ bhūyāt iti ācāryaḥ pravarttate atas eva sva prayojaka vyāpāra adhiṣṭhitā śrotṛ santāna varttinī vyutpattiḥ karttuḥ prayojanam evam eva asau vyutpādakaḥ bhavati śrotā tu katham nāma etat ācārya vyāpāra vaśena mad saṃtāna vartinī vyutpattiḥ bhūyāt iti pravartate 
DhPr_11.5–12.1	 atas eva ācārya vyāpāra adhiṣṭhitā vyutpattiḥ śrotuḥ api prayojanam evam eva asau tad vyutpādyaḥ bhavati tatas vyutpādanam prayojaka vyāpāra vaśa varttinī vyutpattiḥ dvayoḥ api prayojanam iti iti śabdam hetu padam kṛtvā upasaṃharan= āha prakaraṇa karaṇa śravaṇayoḥ prayojanam vyutpādanam iti nanu ca ṇici kṛte vyutpādanam katham ubhayoḥ prayojanam ittham iti praśna visarjane syātām tena eva tāvatā darśitena kim prayojanam samyak jñāna vyutpattau kathañcid nimitta mātrāt dadhi bhojana ādeḥ ācāryasya asādhāraṇa kāraṇa tā pratipattiḥ prayojanam ayam arthaḥ asti prayojaka vyāpāra pradarśane samyak jñāna vyutpattau= upayogi tva mātreṇa svāsthya ādinā sāmyam ācāryasya darśitam syāt asti ca asya tad vyutpattau= upadeśa lakṣaṇaḥ asādhāraṇaḥ vyāpāraḥ sa katham nāma pratīyeta iti ṇicāḥ nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ iti 
DhPr_12.2–12.3	 atha bhojana ādeḥ tad vyutpattau sākṣāt vyāpārā asambhavāt ācārya vyāpāraḥ pratipatsyate iti ced na etat evam hi vyākhyātṛṇām idam pratipādana kauśalam syāt na karttuḥ iti nyāyyaḥ ṇicāḥ nirdeśaḥ nanu uktam abhidhānasya prayojanam na nirūpyate iti tat kim idānīm tat eva vyāja antareṇa nirūpyate satyam kevalam vākya artha tvena na nirūpyate iti abhisandhinā tat na nirūpyate iti uktam na tu padārtha tvena api iti kim virodhaḥ 
DhPr_12.4–12.7	 samyak jñānam vyutpadyamānānām iti asādhuḥ ayam śabdaḥ vyutpatti arthasya padeḥ akarma tvāt iti bhāga vṛtti kāraḥ tat na ati śliṣṭam jñāna arthasya padeḥ sa karmakasya vyutpannaḥ saṅketaḥ ityādau bahuśas prayoga darśanāt yathā avādi pramāṇa vārttike vārttika kṛtā manaḥ vyutpanna saṃketam asti tena sa ced mataḥ iti yadi abhidheya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ sambandhaḥ tarhi kasya padasya arthaḥ iti āha sambandha ityādi sāmarthyāt iti na abhidhāvyā pāreṇa eva kāreṇa padasya api abhidhām apohati tuśabdaḥ kevalam iti asya arthe 
DhPr_12.8–13.1	 katham sāmarthyāt iti āha prekṣāvatā iti upāyaḥ kāraṇam upeyā samyak jñāna vyutpattiḥ sādhyāḥ tayoḥ bhāvaḥ yad vaśena upāya upeya jñāna abhidhāne bhavataḥ eva kāraḥ upāya śabdāt paraḥ draṣṭavyaḥ pratiyoginā upāyā yogasya eva śaṅkita tvāt tad anya yogasya ca śaṅkiṣyamāṇa tvāt anartha āśaṅkā upasthāpita ani ayoga nirāse tu karttavye sāmarthya gamyam avadhāraṇa antaram kāryam na tu idam eva vācyam na anyaḥ iti ca na anyaḥ eva iti avaseyam evaṃrūpasya sambandhaḥ vyutpādyate iti prayojana abhidhānāt eva darśitam tat uktam 
DhPr_13.2	 abhidheya ādi prakāśana dvāreṇa ādi vākyam pravarttakam iti asahamānaḥ āha nanu ca iti nipāta samudāyaḥ ca ayam codayāmi abhimukhaḥ bhavaḥ iti asya arthasya dyotakaḥ śravaṇa anantaram teṣām pratīyamāna tayā pramāṇa abhāva asiddheḥ śravaṇāt prāk iti āha ayam pūrva pakṣa vādinaḥ abhiprāyaḥ śravaṇāt prāk śabda āśrayeṇa pravarttamānam anumānam anyat vā śabdasya arthanā antarīyatāyām pravarttayitum arhati asambandha nibandhanāyāḥ parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ prāmāṇya ayogāt sā ca śabdasya asambhavinī ācāryasya ca āpta bhāvaḥ durbodhaḥ yena āpta upadeśa tayā śabdaḥ artha tathā tvam pratyāyayet iti ārabhyate iti ārambhaḥ prakaraṇam tasya pradeśaḥ eka deśaḥ sāmarthyāt tad ādiḥ 
DhPr_13.3–13.4	 sat codye satyam iti āha yadi satyam idam kim artham tarhi te kathyante iti ukteṣu iti turanukta pakṣāt ukta pakṣasya viśeṣam darśayati anena etat āha sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāve yena ṛte byāhārāt pratiniyata adhikaraṇaḥ yauktaḥ saṃśayaḥ bhavitum arhati iti api nyāyataḥ sambhāvanām darśayati atiśayam vā anyathā kim sa pramāṇakeṣu api saṃśayaḥ jāyate yena apiśrutiḥ saṃgacchet nanu pravṛtti phalam ādi vākyam pravṛttiḥ ced na asti kim saṃśayena utpāditena api iti āha saṃśayāt ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe 
DhPr_13.5	 atha ye tāvat madāḥ śraddhayā vā aacāryam upasannāḥ te tad vacanāt artham niścitya eva pravarttamānāḥ na saṃśayāt pravarttante ye api tad viparītāḥ saṃśerate teṣām api na saṃśayāt pravṛttiḥ pravṛttau vā prekṣāvat tva hāniḥ iti āśaṅkya āha artha saṃśaya upīti na kevalam artha niścayaḥ iti apiśabdena āha śakya niścaye hi niścayam antareṇa pravarttamānāḥ prekṣāvat tāyāḥ hīyeran yatra tu artha saṃśayena arthitayā pravarttamānāḥ na upālambham arhanti iti bhāvaḥ yadi ca yuktā dvitīya ākāra anupraveśena saṃśayān asya na kvacid pravṛttiḥ tarhi na kasyacid vacanāt kvacid pravarttitavyam iti bhūyān vyavahāraḥ vilupyeta 
DhPr_13.6–14.1	 nanu nivṛttiḥ anartha niścaya nibandhanā anartha niścayaḥ ca pramāṇāt tat ca iha na asti nivṛtti itaraḥ tu pravṛtti vyātiḥ ekī prakāraḥ na asti tatas athatna siddhā pravṛttiḥ tat kim tad arthena ādi vākyena iti āha anartha ityādi na kevalam anartha niścayaḥ api iti api śabdaḥ yadi avaśyam vaktavyāni abhigheya ādīni tarhi vyākhyātāraḥ eva tāni vakṣyanti tat kim śāstra kṛtaḥ vyāhāreṇa iti āha śāstra kāreṇa eva na vyākhyātṛbhiḥ 
DhPr_14.2	 atha ucyate pravṛtti aṅga tvāt ca vyācakṣate abhidheya ādi anabhidhāne tu pravṛtteḥ eva asambhavāt katham sambhavinaḥ vyākhyātāraḥ yena āśaṅkya teṣām vyāhāra mayam nirasyati iti atra ucyate na sarvathā abhidheya ādi prakāśanam kenacid na karttavyam eva iti codyam pravṛttam kintvādi vākyam tad artham na karttavyam iti abhisandhinā tatra ye tāvat sākṣāt ācārya upasanna arateṣām tad vacanāt eva tad pratītau pravṛtti jñānayoḥ sambhavāt sambhavi vyākhyātṛ tvam tebhyaḥ api tad upasannānām iti kim avadyam 
DhPr_14.3	 nanu ca na śāstra kṛt vacanam api prasahya pravarttayati kim tarhi prayojana ādi abhidhānena pravṛtti viṣaya upadarśanāt tat ca vyākhyātṛ vacane api sambhavati iti kim ucyate śāstra kāreṇa eva iti atas āha vyākhyātṝṇām hi iti hiḥ yasmāt arthe śāstra kāreṣu api idam samānam iti āha śāstra kṛtām iti tunā vyākhyātṛbhyaḥ śāstra kṛtām vaidharmyam āha viparītam ca tad abhidheya ādi abhidhānam ca iti vigrahaḥ athavā viparītam ca tad asatya tvāt abhidheyañca abhidheya tayā prakāśanāt tasya abhidhānam iti vigrahītavyam utpaśyāmaḥ utprekṣāmahe anena etat āha teṣām api tathā abhidhāne kim asmākam bādhakam pramāṇam kevalam eṣām mahīyasā aaśayena śāstram praṇetum icchatām para artha pravṛttānām na etat sambhāvayāmaḥ iti 
DhPr_14.4–15.1	 prakaraṇasya prārambhaḥ ādau etat ca prayojana ādi abhidhāna niyata sannidheḥ yathā bhūta artha cintā vidhāna viṣayasya kālasya nirdeśaḥ na tu prakaraṇasya madhye avasāne vā tat sambhavati sa prayojanam ca iti athayadi evaṃvidhā pravṛttiḥ śāstra kṛtām dṛśyate tvayā api asya kim na sambhāvyate iti āha na api iti apiḥ aprayojana apekṣayā samam pravṛtti darśanam samuccinoti tat eva utpaśyāmaḥ iti sambadhyamānam iha paśyāmaḥ iti āsya arthe sambandhavyam paśyāmaḥ iti vā adhyāhāryam anena etat āha tathā api sambhāvayāmaḥ yadi teṣām īdṛśī paśyāmaḥ na tu evam iti atas hetoḥ teṣu abhidheya ādiṣu yat vā teṣu śāstra kāreṣu vaktṛṣu satsu tad ukteṣu abhidheya ādiṣu iti prakaraṇāt saṃśayaḥ artha unmukhaḥ iti draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_15.2–15.3	 nanu sati api artha saṃśaye arthitva abhāve pravṛttiḥ na asti tad nimittā tu sā saṃśaya mātrāt api bhavati tad mātrañca sādhaka bādhaka virahāt api arthe siddham tat kim tad utpāda arthena vākyena iti āha anukteṣu iti turukta avasthāyāḥ anukta avasthām bhedavatīm darśayati nirgatam prayojanam yasmāt niṣka antam vā prayojanāt kāka dantāḥ hi abhidheyāḥ te ca na kvacid puruṣa arthaḥ upayujyante sa prayojanam vā abhidheyam aśakya anuṣṭhānam sambhāvyeta kiṃvat iti āha jvara ityādi jvaram harati iti jvara haraḥ takṣaka ākhyasya nāga rājasya cūḍā śikhā tasyāḥ ratnam ratim tanoti iti viśiṣṭam vastu tena alaṅkaraṇam alaṅkāraḥ jvara haraḥ ca asau= evaṃbhūtaḥ ca iti vigrahaḥ saḥ upadiśyate yena granthena tadvat 
DhPr_15.4–15.5	 satoḥ vā sa prayojana śakyā anuṣṭhāna tvayoḥ asya prayojanam anabhimatam eva āstikānām sambhāvyeta mātuḥ vivāhasya kramaḥ paripāṭiḥ upadiśyate yena pārasīka śāstreṇa tadvat pārasīka śāstreṇa hi mṛte pitari mātā prathamam agrajena putreṇa pariṇetavyā tadanu tad anujena iti upadiśyate atas vā prakaraṇāt laghuḥ alpa granthaḥ prayojanasya samyak jñāna vyutpatti lakṣaṇasya anupāyaḥ eva animittam eva 
DhPr_15.6	 catvāraḥ api vā śabdāḥ pūrva pūrva apekṣayā pakṣa antaram avadyotayanti sambhāvanā ca sarvā varṇitā anartha unmukhā pratipattiḥ yuktyā dvitīya ākāra anupraveśāt ca saṃśaya pada abhilāpyā pratyetavyāḥ sarvatra iva ākāra antarasya pratiyoginaḥ samudācārataḥ adarśanāt tathāvidhā anartha sambhāvanāyāḥ ca bījam idam asti ādi vākye yadi asya prayojana ādikam bhavet bahubhiḥ anyaiḥ iva anena api ādau= uktam bhavet na ca anena kiñcid avādi iti matiḥ 
DhPr_15.7–15.8	 kāmam amūra nartha sambhāvanāḥ bhavantu kā naḥ hāniḥ iti āha etāsu iti na kevalam sarvāḥ iti apiśabdena āha prayojana ādi anabhidhānaḥ iva yadi abhidhāne api bhavanti tāḥ tadā kim abhidheya ādibhiḥ abhihitaiḥ api iti āha abhidheya ādiṣu iti turukteṣu iti asya anantaram draṣṭavyaḥ anukta pakṣāt ca viśeṣasya dyotakaḥ atha katham anayoḥ artha anartha sambhā vanayoḥ virodhaḥ yatas sambhāvanā saṃśayaḥ ucyate sa ca ubhayām śāva lambanaḥ iti anyonyasya āmanyākāraḥ asti iti kutas saha anavasthānam ucyate ekasyām anartha aṃkāraḥ udriktaḥ anubhūyate yukteḥ tu dvitīya ākāra anupraveśaḥ itasyām tu udriktaḥ arbha ākāraḥ anubhūyate yukteḥ tu anartha ākāra anupraveśaḥ iti ubhayoḥ api anyonya vaiparītyena anubhavāt katham avirodhaḥ 
DhPr_16.1	 bhavatu evam tathā api katham asya abhidhāne anartha āśaṅkā nirastā iti ced ucyate puruṣa artha siddhi rūpa abhidheya prayojana abhidhānenā aadimā anartha sambhāvanā nirastāḥ abhidheya tad prayojanayaḥ rūpa nirūpaṇena ca dvitīya tṛtīye niraste antimā api sāmarthya gati sambandha pratipādanāt nirastāḥ turīyām tu parama viveka śālinaḥ ācāryasya prakaraṇa ārambha sāmarthyān nirasyate tathā hi na samāne api upāya antare sambhavati mahataḥ mahān ayam prekṣā pūrva kārī prakaraṇam īdṛśam ārabhate kim aṅga punar laghūni iti 
DhPr_16.2	 atha syāt sama samaya sambhavī deśa antara vartī ca kaścid etat agratas laghu upāya antara granthaḥ syāt tat katham tad praṇīta laghu upāya antara nirāsaḥ atra api tat prekṣā vat tā eva mahatī nibandhanam prekṣā pūrva kāri tvāt eva tathābhūtāt tena asmin= āryāvarte anyatra vā loke neda āni intanena etad artham prakaraṇam praṇītam iti bahudhā anusarttavyam anusṛtya dṛṣṭvā tad laghuḥ upāyaḥ iti ca niścitya idam praṇetum ucitam na anyathā iti sarvatra eva prakaraṇe satya ādi vākye laghu upāya antara nirāse gatiḥ iyam eva nahi anyatra api abhidheya tad prayojana ādi prakāśanam antareṇa laghu upāya antara nirāsa abhidhānam asti iti kim na anumanyate 
DhPr_16.3	 yadi evam itarāsām api anartha sambhāvanānām evam eva astu nirāsaḥ tad kim ādi vākyena na etat na hi sūcī praveśa eti eva mūsala praveśaḥ tathā hi asatya ādi vākye prekṣā pūrva kāri prayukta tvam eva prakaraṇasya na śakyate kalpayituma pratyuta aprekṣā pūrva kāri prayukta tvam eva śakya kalpanam dṛśyante hi prekṣā pūrva kāriṇaḥ prakaraṇa ādau sarvatra prayojana ādi abhidhāyakam ādi vākyam praṇayantaḥ na ca anena ādi vākyam tad artham akāri tasmāt na ayam prakaraṇa kāraḥ prekṣā pūrvakārīti saṅkalpāt na upādadīta 
DhPr_16.4	 nanu ca pravṛtti arthaḥ ayam prayāsaḥ sā ced na asti kim tayā utpannayā api iti āha tayā iti yadi artha sambhāvanā prakaraṇe puruṣasya pravarttayitrī tarhi kim abhidheya ādi abhidhīyate iti āha iti iti yasmāt artha sambhauvanayā pravarttante itiḥ tasmāt artha sambhāvanām karttum kimbhūtām pravṛteḥ aṅgam nimittam aṅga ādi śabdānām asati bahuvrīhau para liṅga agrahaṇāt su a liṅgena nirdeśaḥ itiḥ evam arthe sthitam niścitam 
DhPr_17.1–17.2	 evam anena pravandhena samyak jñāna ityādi vākyasya samudāya artham vyākhyāya avayava artham idānīm avisaṃvādakam ityādinā vyācaṣṭe atra ayam pūrva pakṣaḥ kim idam samyaktvam jñānasya abhipretam yat yogāt samyak jñānam ucyate yadi evam vastu tattva grahaṇam samyaktvam atha api gṛhīta vastu prāpaṇam ubhayathā api anumānam avastu grahaṇāt asamyak jñānam agṛhīta prāpaṇāt vā samyak jñāna tve jala jñānam api upadarśita marīcikāḥ prāpayati iti na kiñcid samyak jñānam na syāt iti 
DhPr_17.3	 siddhānta vādi api amīṣām pakṣāṇām anabhyupagamena nirāsam manyamānaḥ avisaṃvādaka tvam samyaktvam vivakṣitam iti darśayati avisaṃvādakam saṃvādakam ucyate viśabdaḥ hi saṃvādaka pratiṣedhe varttate tat pratiṣedhasya vidhi rūpa tvāt saṃvādakaḥ eva avatiṣṭhate iti saṃvādaka arthaḥ avisaṃvādaka śabdaḥ tat ayam arthaḥ avisaṃvādakam pravṛtti viṣaya vastu prāpakam samyak jñānam iti 
DhPr_17.4	 syāt etat vṛddha vyavahāraḥ hi śabda artha niścaya bhūmiḥ tatra ca saṃvādaka śabdaḥ na upadarśita artha prāpake varttate kim tarhi satya vādini na ca jñānasya tādrūpyam asti tat kutas tatra saṃvādaka śabdaḥ iti āha loke ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe api śabda arthe vā loke vyavaharttari jane ayam āśayaḥ yathā loke satya vādi śabda pravṛtti nimittasya upadarśita artha prāpaṇasya puruṣe sambhavāt saṃvādaka śabdaḥ pravarttate tathā jñāne api tad sambhavāt iti 
DhPr_17.5–17.6	 atha ucyate na upadarśita artha prāpaṇa nimittakaḥ puruṣe saṃvādaka śabdaḥ kintu pratijñāta artha prāpaṇa nimittakaḥ tat katham iha nimitta sambhavaḥ iti tad avadyam tatra api pratijñayā upadarśanasya upa lakṣaṇāt tat eva tu upadarśanam kvacid vacanena kvacid adhyavasāyenā pi kvacid vastu pratibhāsa pūrvakeṇa kvacid anyathā vṛttena iti viśeṣaḥ saṃvādaka śabda pravṛtti nimittam tu sarvatra samānam iti prāpayan iti lakṣaṇa hetvoḥ iti hetau śatuḥ vidhānāt prāpaṇāt iti arthaḥ evam uttaratra api avaseyam 
DhPr_18.1	 nanu upadarśita artha prāpakam saṃvādakam iti bruvatā jñānasya ekasya upadarśaka tva prāpaka tve pratijñāte pravṛttim antareṇa prāpteḥ anupapatteḥ arthataḥ pravarttaka tvam api na ca ekasya ete vyāpārāḥ sambhavanti yatas anyat pradarśati yena jānīte anyat pravarttayati yad anantaram pravṛttim ācarati anyat ca prāpayati yatas prāptyā abhisambaddhyate puruṣaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha pradarśite ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe 
DhPr_18.2	 pravarttaka tvam eva prāpaka tvam bruvataḥ ayam abhiprāyaḥ yadi api artham sākṣātkṛtya anurūpam niścayam janayat pradarśakam kiñcid aparam pradarśayat vā bāhyāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ kāraṇam bhavat pravarttakam itarat pravarttana dvāreṇa bāhyāyāḥ prāpteḥ nimittam bhavat prāpakam vyapadiśyate tathā api saḥ eva bāhya pravṛtti kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pravartayitṛ tva ādi prayojaka vyāpāra rūpaḥ jñānasya puruṣa preraṇena artha jananena ca pravarttana prāpaṇayoḥ asambhavena pradarśanāt anyaḥ na upayujyate iti vastutas sarvasya eva jñānasya niścaya anugatasya adhigamāt na aparau pravarttana prāpaṇa vyāpārau atas eva tatra ādyam eva jñānam pramāṇam vyavasthāpyate tatas vastutas pradarśaka tva ādīnām abhedaḥ vyāvṛtti nibandhanaḥ tu bhedaḥ asti eva atas eva ete pradarśaka pravarttaka prāpaka śabdāḥ kṛtaka tva anitya tva ādi vat na paryāyāḥ iti 
DhPr_18.3	 syāt matam kim punar prayojanam yena prarvattanāt nā aparaḥ prāpaṇa vyāpāraḥ jñānasya adhigamāt ca na anyat pravarttana prayatnena sādhyate yadi uttara jñānasya prāmāṇya niṣedha artham tadā gṛhīta grāhitā eva tat niṣetsyati iti kim tad arthena prayāsena iti atra ucyate yadi pravarttayitṛ tvam prāpayitṛ tvam ca pradarśaka tvāt paramārthataḥ anyat syāt tadā gṛhīta grāhitā eva na śakyate pratipādayitum iti kena prāmāṇyam niṣedhyeta tathā hi na tat jñānam gṛhītam gṛhṇāti api tu gṛhīte pravarttayati aparam tu gṛhītam prāpayati tathā akāriṇoḥ ca bhinna upayoga tvāt prāmāṇyam katham apākriyate yadā tu pravarttanāt na aparaḥ prāpaṇa vyāpāraḥ jñānasya pradarśanāt ca na anyat pravarttanam prathamena eva ca pratyakṣa anumāna kṣaṇena artha kriyā samarthaḥ vastu santānaḥ pravṛtti viṣayīkarttum niścayāt śakyate tadā uttareṣām tad santāna bhāvinām abhinna yogakṣema tayā prāmāṇyam apāsyate iti 
DhPr_18.4	 etena tat api pratyuktam yat kenacid abhyadhāyi dharma uttare yadi upadarśaka tvam eva prāpaka tvam tarhi yat uktam upadarśitam artham prāpayat saṃvādakam iti tasya ayam arthaḥ syāt upadarśitam upadarśayat iti na ca etat yuktam artha bheda abhāvāt tathā hi yadi paramārthataḥ artha abhedaḥ ucyate tadā na kiñcid avadyam atha tadā api na evam vaktavyaḥ atyalpam idam ucyate kṛtaka tvam anitya tvam pratipādayati iti api na vaktavyam artha abhedāt iti api kim na ucyate atha śabda pravṛtti apekṣayā artha abhedaḥ ucyate tadā asau= asiddhaḥ vyāvṛtti bhedasya darśita tvāt tena ayam arthaḥ upadarśitam sākṣātkṛtya janita anurūpa niścayam artham pravarttana dvāreṇa bāhyāyāḥ prāpteḥ sākṣāt yogyatayā vā nimitta tām gacchat saṃvādakam iti vāstavaḥ tu pravarttaka prāpakayoḥ prameya adhigati lakṣaṇāt pradarśana vyāpārāt anyaḥ vyāpāraḥ na asti iti na pravarttayitṛ tvam prāpayitṛ tvam ca prayojaka vyāpāraḥ anayoḥ bhinnaḥ iti 
DhPr_19.1	 syāt matam yadi adhigatiḥ eva uttareṣām api phalam syāt tadā upayoga antara abhāvāt bhavet aprāmāṇyam yāvatā pravarttakasya pravṛttiḥ phalam prāpakasya prāptiḥ iti phala bheda niṣpatteḥ bhinnaḥ vyāpāraḥ iti āha atas eva iti yatas na artha janana dvāreṇa artha prāpaṇam jñānasya yatas ca na prasahya preraṇena pravarttanam atas eva asmāt eva kāraṇāt arthasya adhigatiḥ paricchittiḥ phalam na pravṛtti ādi 
DhPr_19.2	 nanu tat pramāṇasya phalam vyavasthāpyate yasmin sati tad vyāpāraḥ parisamāpyate na ca adhigatau= api pravṛtti prāptyoḥ abhāve sa parisamāpyate iti āha adhigate ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe yasmāt yena arthaḥ samyak jñānena darśitaḥ tatra tena apravarttitaḥ api puruṣaḥ pravṛtti yogya upadarśanāt tad gatasya ca vyāpāra antarasya abhāvāt pravarttitaḥ iti ucyate satyarthi tve pravarttanam eva jñānena tāvat pravṛtti yogyaḥ kṛtaḥ iti yāvat 
DhPr_19.3^1	 astu puruṣaḥ tathā pravarttitaḥ arthaḥ tu na prāpitaḥ tathā ca vyāpāra antaram anya adhīnam asti iti āha prāpitaḥ iti caḥ pūrvavat arthaḥ api asau= aprāptaḥ api śakya prāptikaḥ darśitaḥ iti prāpitaḥ ucyate atas eva prāpaṇa śaktiḥ eva jñānasya prāmāṇyam sā ca prāpyāt arthāt ātma lābha nimittā iti yatas yena pravarttate tat api prāpaṇa yogyam eva śakti niścayaḥ tu artha kriyā nirbhāsasya sarvasya anumānasya ca svatas eva pravarttaka adhyakṣasya ca kasyacid svatas eva yat abhyāsena paritas nirasta vibhrama āśaṅkam yad nidrā ādi anupaplutam sat āsanna deśam anāśaṅkya vyañjaka adhīnā anyathā abhivyavita ca vastu gṛhṇāti tad rūpa saṃvedanāt eva satya artham niścīyate 
DhPr_19.3^2	 kasyacid tu paratas artha kriyā nirbhāsa ātmakāt svatas pramāṇāt anyatas vā yatas kutaścid na antarīyaka artha darśanāt madhya kāla vartti bhrānti śaṅkā apanodena niścīyate iti prāpitaḥ ca artham iti kvacid pāṭhaḥ sa tu yukta rūpaḥ pravṛtti yogyīkaraṇāt pravarttitaḥ prāpya artha upadarśanāt prāpitaḥ artham iti eka vākya tayā upadarśanāt evam uttaratrā api eṣa eva pāṭhaḥ avadātaḥ iti tathā ca sati tasmin= ca prakāre sati samāptaḥ paryavasānam gataḥ tasmāt adhigamasya phala tvam yuktam iti bhāvaḥ yatas adhigamāt anyat phalam na upapadyate jāte ca tasmin samāpyate vyāpāraḥ atas asmāt kāraṇāt anadhigataḥ jñāna antareṇa aparicchinnaḥ viṣayaḥ arthaḥ yasya tat pramāṇam bhavati 
DhPr_19.4	 nanu adhigata viṣayam udīcīnam jñānam tatra arthe kiñcid adhikam ādadhānam pramāṇam bhaviṣyati na hi viṣaya bhedāt eva pramāṇa bhedaḥ api tu upayoga bhedāt api iti āha yena eva iti hiryaramāt pūrvāt yogyatayā pravarttitaḥ prāpitaḥ iti ca uktam tatra eva pūrva jñānāt adhigate kim adhikam atiriktam kāryam karttavyam na kiñcid ādyena eva karttavyasya kṛta tvāt iti bhāvaḥ atas asmāt hetoḥ idha gataṣiyam tat adhigantṛ sajātīyam vijātīyam vā na pramāṇam tena pramāṇasamplavaḥ nāma na asti eva iti prakāśitam 
DhPr_20.1	 nanu ca prabandhena anena pravṛtti viṣaya upadarśakam samthak jñānam iti darśitam vakṣyamāṇayā nītyā pratyakṣa anumāna nāmanī dve samyak jñāne tatra yadi samānam anayoḥ pravṛtti viṣaya upadarśanam tat idam pratyakṣam sat pramāṇam idam anumānam sat iti bhedaḥ na syāt atas tad anayoḥ asa māna viṣaya tvam eva kathitavyam evam ca kasya katham tat iti vaktavyam iti āha tatra iti tayoḥ pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ madhye dṛṣṭa tvena jñātaḥ niścitaḥ yadi jñātaḥ iti eva kriyate tadā anumeyaḥ api niścitaḥ san pratyakṣeṇa pravṛtti viṣayīkṛtaḥ prasajyeta iti dṛṣṭa tvena iti kṛtam atha yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti kim na ucyate na ucyate kṣaṇika tva ādeḥ api dṛṣṭa tvena pratyakṣa viṣaya tvāt anumāna avatāra abhāva prasaṅgāt iti 
DhPr_20.2	 nanu na pratyakṣasya niścayanāt grahaṇam api tu pratibhāsāt tat kim ucyate jñātaḥ niścitaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha yasmāt iti vikalpena anugamyate anustriyate adhyavasīyate paśyāmi iti ākāreṇa tasmāt dṛṣṭa tvena jñātaḥ iti ucyate vikalpena iti tad pṛṣṭha bhāvinā anurūpeṇa iti draṣṭavyam ananurūpa vikalpa anugata vyāpārasya tatra aprāmāṇyāt kṣaṇikatvaḥ iva evam bruvataḥ ca ayam abhiprāyaḥ sāṃvyavahārikasya pramāṇasya idam lakṣaṇam ucyate tatas vastu vṛttyā prakāśamānam api anurūpa vikalpena aviṣayīkṛtam sat apratibhāsamānam na atiśete vyavahāra ayogya tvāt evam tat grāhakam api tathāvidha vikalpena ananugamyamāna vyāpāram vyavahārayitum aparyāptam sat tṛṇasya api kubjīkaraṇe asamartham agrāhakam na ativarttate tena yat uktam pradarśaka tvam eva pravarttaka tva ādi iti yat ca uktam adhigatiḥ eva phalam iti tad anurūpa niścaya anugata vyāpāram anurūpa niścaya anugatau= iti draṣṭavyam evam yatra yatra ucyate pratyakṣam vastu upadarśakam vastu grāhakam ityādinā śabdena tatra sarvatra anurūpa niścaya anugata vyāpāram eva boddhavyam 
DhPr_20.3–21.1	 atha evam sati vikalpasya api prāmāṇyam prasajyeta iti ced etat svayam eva dharma uttareṇa āśaṅkya nirākariṣyate iti na iha ucyate yadi pratyakṣam evam pravṛtti viṣayam upadarśayati anumānam api evam tadā katham bheda vyavasthā iti āha anumānam tu iti tuḥ pratyakṣāt anumānasya vaidharmyam āha pratyakṣam na svayam niścinvat pravṛtti viṣayam darśayati kintu niścāyayat anumānam tu svayam eva niścinvat iti katham apratibhāsamānam niścetum īṣṭe tat iti āha liṅga darśanāt iti liṅgasya sādhyāvinābhūtasya dhūma ādeḥ darśanāt darśanam ca svarūpa grahaṇa pūrvakam sarvatra idam sādhyāvinābhūtam iti jñānam sarvatra sādhya avinābhūtam iti smaraṇa puraḥsaram vā kvacid svarūpa grahaṇam iha vivakṣitam 
DhPr_21.2^1	 nanu ca pratyakṣa anumāna jñāna vat anyasya api jñānasya yathā pravṛtti viṣaya pradarśanam tathā kim na pradarśyate atha aprāmāṇyāt na upadarśyate katham punar aprāmāṇyam anyasya aniyata pravṛtti viṣaya pradarśaka tvāt iti ced tarhi pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ api tathātvena prāmāṇyam na syāt iti āgūrya jñāna antarāda bhedam anayoḥ darśayan= āha tathā ca iti tasmiḥ ca pratyakṣasya sva vyāpāra anusāri vikalpa upajananena niścayanāt pravṛtti viṣaya pradarśana prakāre manyadāḥ liṅga darśanāt svayam niścayena pravṛtti viṣaya pradarśana prakāre pratyakṣam jñānam pratibhāsamānam svarūpeṇa prakāśamānam niyatam artha kriyā kṣame bhāva rūpaḥ eva vyavasthitam darśayati tena na anartham na api aniyatam darśayati iti ākūtam anumānam ca niyatam artham darśayati 
DhPr_21.2^2	 caḥ pratyakṣeṇa samam anumānam niyata pradarśaka tvena samuccinoti liṅga sambaddham iti hetu bhāvena viśeṣaṇam tat ayam arthaḥ yasmāt liṅgam vijātīya vyāvṛtte arthekriyā kāriṇi tādātmyena tad utpattyā vā sambaddham āyattam tasmāt tat prabhavam api anumānam niyatam darśayati adhyavasyati iti tena anumānam api na anartham na api aniyatam bhāva ātmani abhāva ātmani vā darśayati iti prakāśitam iyān= tu viśeṣaḥ anumānam sambandha grahaṇa kāla dṛṣṭa sādhāraṇam rūpam āśritya udayamānam sva lakṣaṇa madhyavasyat api na santāna antara asādhāraṇa madhyavasyati iti pravṛtti viṣaya apekṣam api sāmānya viṣayam eva pratyakṣam tu pravṛtti viṣaya apekṣam api asādhāraṇa viṣayam eva santāna antara asādhāraṇena eva rūpeṇa viṣayasya niścāyanāt iti 
DhPr_21.3	 idānīm yasya ayam āśayaḥ astu pratyakṣam niyata artha darśakam arthasya sākṣātkaraṇāt anumānam tu parokṣa arthasya asākṣātkaraṇāt katham niyatam darśayati tasmāt na dvayoḥ niyata artha pradarśaka tvam api tu ekasya eva iti tam sāmastya niṣedha vādinam pratyupasaṃharan= āha atas iti yasmāt vastu prakāśāt pratyakṣam niyatam darśayati parokṣasya antarā sākṣāt anavabhāse api tad sambaddha tayā ca anumānam kārya svabhāva jam ekānta niyatam bhāvam anupalambha jam ekānta niyatam abhāvam tathābhūtam darśayati atas asmāt hetoḥ ete dve api tathārūpe tatas anena sāmastya niṣedhasya niṣedhaḥ upasaṃhṛtaḥ anyathā vyākhyāyamāne tu yatas tu niyatam artham pradarśayataḥ atas ete niyata artha upadarśake iti arthaḥ syāt etat ca parisphuṭasya eva skuṭīkaraṇam anarthakam āpadyeta iti 
DhPr_22.1–22.2	 bhavatām ete niyata artha upadarśake pramāṇe tu katham iti āha tena iti tena niyata artha pradarśaka tvena niyata artha pradarśaka tva abhāvāt kila aprāmāṇyam anayoḥ śaṅikatam sati api tasmin katham tat syāt iti bhāvaḥ anayoḥ pravṛtti viṣaya pradarśana prakāra upadarśane tad anyasya jñānasya ca tad apradarśane yat buddhi stham āsīt tat idānīm na anyat ityādinā abhivyanakti na anyat vijñānam pramāṇam iti vacana vipariṇāmena sambandhaḥ yadi evam jñāna tva aviśeṣāt amū api pramāṇe mā bhūtām iti āha prāptum iti ādarśayat iti hetau śatuḥ vidhānāt hetu padam etat tena ayam arthaḥ yatas prāptum śakyam artham ādarśayati tena pratyakṣa ādikam prāpakam iti bhavatu prāpakam pramāṇam tu kasmāt iti āha prāpaka tvāt ca iti caḥ avadhāraṇe 
DhPr_22.3	 nanu ābhyām anyena api darśitaḥ arthaḥ śakya prāpaṇaḥ eva tatas tad upadarśakam api kim na prāpakam prāpaka tvāt ca kim na pramāṇam iti āha pramāṇābhyām iti caḥ yasmāt atyanta grahaṇena saṃśaya jñāna viṣayāt viśeṣam darśayati tathāvidhaḥ api kim na prāpya ita iti āha sa ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe niyata upadarśaka tve api anartha upadarśaka tvāt aprāmāṇyam asya darśitam yadi kaścid īdṛśaḥ tad anya jñāna viṣayaḥ anyādṛśaḥ bhaviṣyati tat upadarśakam ca pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti atas āha kaścid iti saṃśaya arthaḥ saṃśaya ālambanaḥ sthāṇuḥ vā puruṣaḥ vā aiti hi pratyayaḥ sthāṇum ullikhya puruṣaḥ vā iti ālambayan= tad abhāvam ullikhati tatas sthāṇu abhāva avyabhicāriṇam puruṣam puruṣa abhāva avyabhicāriṇam ca sthāṇu mavasyan= a bhāve na api abhāve niyatam sthāṇam puruṣam vā darśayati iti bhāva abhāvayoḥ aniyatam darśayati yatas eva ayam ekānta niyatam darśayitum anīśānaḥ dolāyate tatas eva saṃśayaḥ iti upapadyate iti 
DhPr_22.4–22.5	 atha viparyaya arthaḥ asattvāt na prāpyatām ayam tu kasmāt na prāpyate iti āha na ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe nanu bhavatu saṃśaya viparyayayoḥ aprāmāṇyam kim naḥ chinnam etat atiriktam pratyakṣa anumānābhyām anyat pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti āśaṅkya āha sarveṇa ca ityādi caḥ yasmāt sarvānte rgata tvāt anumānasya api tathātvam syāt iti āha aliṅgena iti na asya liṅgam utpādaka tvena vidyate iti aliṅgam yadi aliṅgena sarveṇa tat karaṇīyam tadā pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ api vikalpasya tadā aayātam iti āha niyāmakam iti viṣaya adhīnaḥ hi niyata artha parigrahaḥ jñānasya iti arthaḥ niyāmakaḥ tam adṛṣṭvā 
DhPr_23.1	 nanu kim pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvi api niyāmakam artham dṛṣṭvā pravarttate yena tādrūpya virahāt anyeṣām vikalpānām tathā atvam āśaṅkyate ucyate pravarttena iti atra antarbhūtaḥ ṇijarthaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ tatas ayam arthaḥ niyāmakam adṛṣṭvā pravarttitena iti tathā ca sati pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvī vikalpaḥ niyāmakam dṛṣṭvā eva pratyakṣeṇa pratyayena pravartti ate iti tathā tvena parihṛtaḥ bhavati itare tu aliṅga vikalpāḥ yena pravartti ante jāyante na tena sākṣāt niyāmakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti teṣām tathā tva anuṣaṅgaḥ 
DhPr_23.2	 anye tu anumāna nivṛtti artham aliṅgā iti yojayitvā katham punar avasāya ātmakena api aliṅgena tena evam karaṇīyam iti āśaṅkya niyāmakam adṛṣṭvā iti asya tu hetu bhāvena viśeṣaṇa tvāt niyāmakam adṛṣṭvā pravṛtta tvāt iti arthaḥ iti vyākhyāya tātparya artham api darśayanti yadi api śabda ādi janmānaḥ vikalpāḥ na ubhaya pakṣa saṃsparśena dolāyante tathā api te niyāmakān āśrayeṇa pravarttamānāḥ na yaukta saṃśaya rūpa tām ativarttante iti pūrva vyākhyāne api ayam eva āśayaḥ sarvasya tasya samudācaratorviruddhayoḥ ākārayoḥ abhāve api yuktyā dvitīya ākāra anupraveśāt saṃśaya rūpa tvena bhāva abhāva aniyata artha upadarśaka tvam iti 
DhPr_23.3–23.4	 eke tu niyāmakam vikalpayitavyam vastunā āntarīyakam vastu adṛṣṭvā pravṛttena iti yojayanti aliṅgena iti ca asya eva arthasya hetu bhāvena viśeṣaṇam āhuḥ ubhaye api tu pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvi vikalpena atiprasaṅga manadhigata artha adhigantuḥ vikalpasya prāmāṇya cintā adhikāreṇa nirākurvate tena ayam arthaḥ sarveṇa tena anadhigata artha adhigantṛ tayā abhipretena evam avaśya karaṇīyam iti aniyata artha pradarśakam api tad prāpakam syāt iti āha sa ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe aśakyaḥ iti asya anantaram sa avadhāraṇa arthaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ saḥ aniyataḥ arthaḥ na prāptum śakyaḥ aśakya tvāt iti bhāvaḥ 
DhPr_23.5	 nanu ca tādṛśam sarvam mā bhūt prāpakam pramāṇam tu kasmāt na bhavati iti āśaṅkya pūrva uktam eva upasaṃharati tasmāt iti yasmāt prāpaka tvāt eva pramāṇam tasmāt arthasya aśakya prāpaṇa tve atyanta viparīta tvāni tva aniyata tve hetū hetu bhāvena anayoḥ viśeṣaṇa tvāt caḥ aprāptika artha samuccaye kaścid atyanta viparyastaḥ kaścid aniyataḥ iti ādeḥ yathākramam upasaṃhāraḥ anyat jñānam iti na anyat jñānam iti asya 
DhPr_24.1	 syāt etat śakya prāptika artha upadarśakam eva samyak jñānaṃna anyat iti nirnimittam idam tathā ca anyat api kim na parīkṣyate iti āha artha kriyā arthibhiḥ iti caḥ yasmāt arthasya dāha ādeḥ kriyā niṣpattiḥ tām arthayantā ati tathā etaiḥ artha kriyāyām śaktasya vastunaḥ prāpteḥ yad nimittam tat mṛgyate anviṣyate artha kriyā arthi tvāt eva ca tad anveṣaṇam eṣām avaseyam taiḥ ca prekṣāvadbhiḥ iti prakaraṇāt draṣṭavyam itaratha artha kriyā arthibhiḥ api aprekṣāvadbhiḥ mithyājñānam api nibhālyate iti tad parīkṣā api āpatet 
DhPr_24.2	 yadi nāma taiḥ tat mṛgyam tathā api tat itarat api jñānam kim na parīkṣyate iti āha yat ca iti caḥ avadhāraṇe vicāryate parīkṣyate īdṛśam tat samyak jñānam pravarttakam yat anusaranti bhavantaḥ iti vibhajya pratipādyate ayam asya āśayaḥ na vyasanitayā aacāryeṇa jñānam vicāryate kintarhi artha kriyā arthi jana anurodhena te tathābhūtam eva jñānam mṛgayante na anyat iti tat eva vicāryate iti tat eva iti ca mukhya vṛtti abhiprāyeṇa uktam na tu mithyājñānam śāstre asmin na vicāryate eva prasaṅgāt tu tasya api kalpanā prabhṛtau vicāra sambhavāt iti 
DhPr_24.3	 nanu śakya prāpaṇa artha upadarśakam eva samyak jñānam kutas vyavasthāpyate na anyat iti praśne kim idam aprakṛtam ucyate iti āha tatas iti yatas artha kriyā arthinām prekṣāvatām na anyat mṛgayaṇīyam tad anveṣaṇīyam eva vicāraṇīyam vyasani tayā vicāra asambhavāt tatas artha kriyā samarthasya vastunaḥ pradarśakam samyak jñānam na anyat iti arthāt 
DhPr_24.4	 astu samyak jñānam īdṛśam eva tat punar anyat upadarśya anyat prāpayat api kim na samyak jñānam sat pramāṇam vyavahriyate tathā ca pītaśaṅkha ādi jñānam api prāmāṇyāt na apaiti āha yat ca iti caḥ avadhāraṇe anena pītaśaṅkha ādi jñānam api aṃśe saṃvādāt pramāṇam iti yat kaiścid iṣṭim tat api samyak jñāna vyavacchedyam iti darśayati 
DhPr_24.5	 nanu ca anukta samam idam pīta śaṅkha ādi jñānena anupadarśitasya api śukla śaṅkhasya jala jñānena anupadarśitasya api marīcikā nicayasya prāpaṇa darśanāt na etat asti yatas na tad jñāna pūrvikā sā prāptiḥ tasyāḥ ajñāta vastu viṣaya tvāt na ca tena śukla śaṅkha vastu marīci vaḥ tu vā jñātam yathā tu jñāna antarāt eva tathāvidha artha prāptiḥ na tatas tathā anena eva prāmāṇya parīkṣāyām nirloṭhitam iti na iha ucyate 
DhPr_25.1–25.2	 tat eva tena prāpaṇīyam iti kutas etat iti āha artha adhigama iti hiḥ yasmāt uktam iti pradarśana ādīnām vastutas abhedam pratipādya atas eva artha adhigatiḥ eva pramāṇa phalam iti anena prakāśita tvāt na tu sākṣāt abhihitam yadi anyat adhigamya anyat prāpayet tadā pradarśana prāpaṇayoḥ bhedaḥ eva syāt abhedaḥ ca pratipāditaḥ iti bhāvaḥ katham punar adhigatiḥ eva phalam iti anena tathā atvam asya uktam yatas prāpaka tvam prāmāṇyam phalam ca tat avyatiriktam iti athavā prāptum śakyam artham ādarśayat prāpakam iti anena evam uktam tathā hi tādṛśam artham ādarśayat iti paricchindat iti arthaḥ paricchedaḥ ca prāpaka tvāt na bhidyate iti 
DhPr_25.3	 bhava tu upadarśita artha prāpaka tvam eva samyak jñānam yat tu tat eva prāpya vastu śaṅkha ādikam pīta rūpa tayā pradarśayati tat katham asamyak jñānam iti āha tatra iti tatra iti vākya upakṣepe ca etat pradarśitāt rūpāt bhinna ākāra ādi sat vastu anyat iti anya tvam vidheyam ākāra ādi bhinnam api na tatas anyat tat eva idam iti adhyavasāyāt iti a āha viruddhā iti hiḥ yasmāt yadi viruddha dharma adhyāsāt anya tvam na tarhi deśa ādi bhedāt iti āha deśa iti caḥ yasmāt arthe bhavatu evam tathā api ākāra ādi bhinna grāhi jñānam ākāra antara ādi yogini vastuni kim na pramāṇam iti āha tasmāt iti yasmāt samyak jñānena yat eva hi darśitam tat eva prāpaṇīyam ākāra ādi bhinnam ca tatas anyat tasmāt kim iva kva na pramāṇam iti āha yathā iti bhinna deśa grāhiṇaḥ kā vārtā iti āha deśa antarā iti kiṃvat na pramāṇam iti āha yathā iti avapavaraka śabdena deśa viśeṣaḥ layana udara ādi śabda vācyaḥ ucyate apavaraka śabdasya api etad arthasya bhāvāt apavaraka deśa sthaḥ iti pāṭhe api na doṣaḥ 
DhPr_25.4^1	 bhinna kāla grāhiṇaḥ kā vyavasthā iti āha kāla antarā iti upadarśana kālāt anyena kālena vyāvahārikeṇa yuktam sambaddham tat grāhi bhinna kāla vastu grāhi iti yāvat caḥ pūrvavat pūrveṇa saha idama prāmāṇyena samuccinoti tat udāharan= āha yathā iti ayam asya arthaḥ adharātre nidrāṇasya madhyāhna kāla pratibhāsam anubhavataḥ vaṇijyā gata suta vastu darśana hṛṣita romṇa eva jhaṭiti bodhe kākatālīya nyāyena ca sati api putra upalambhe tat jñānam na pramāṇam tat khalu parama arthena ardharātra kāla sambaddham madhyāhna kāla akalitam ca pratītam iti madhyāhna kāla tvena avabhāsanāt eva ca madhyāhna kālam tat vastu uktam 
DhPr_25.4^2	 ardharātraḥ kālaḥ āgamana kālaḥ yasya tasmin na pramāṇam athavā yaḥ ardharātre suptaḥ ahnaḥ madhyam udgate savitari putram āgatam dṛṣṭavā prabhātāyām rātrau sampanne madhyandine tasmin= eva ca deśe tam eva sutam prāgatam prabuddhaḥ api paśyati tasya tat jñānam saṃvāda mātra bhāj api na pramāṇam yatas ardharātre madhyāhnam tadānīm anāgatam api putra vastu āgatam tena avagatam na ca ardharātre deśa kāla niyatasya putrasya tasya ca kālasya asti sadbhāvaḥ tadā tu ardharātraḥ paramārthataḥ pratibhāsa kālaḥ yasya madhyāhna kāla yukta vastunaḥ iti yojyam 
DhPr_26.1–26.2	 etena suptasya kenacid paṭhyamānam grantham śṛṇvataḥ jñānam asatya artham vyākhyātam avaseyam yasmāt deśa kāla bhinna ātmānam śrotāram grantham ca śrotavyam paśyati nidrā upahataḥ na ca tad deśa kāla sambaddhau staḥ yad deśa kālau ca staḥ tathā na gṛhṇāti iti anayā eva ca diśā vāji svapnaḥ api vyākhyātaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ yatas tatra api ghoṭaka svapne yad kāla darśana viṣayāḥ bhāvāḥ dṛśyante na tathā santi yad kālāḥ ca santi tad kālāḥ na dṛśyante ardharātra ādiṣu hi svapna darśanam sūrya udaya ādi sambaddhāḥ ca te bhāvāḥ dṛśyante tasmāt svapne keṣāñcid anubhūtānām atyantam abhāvāt artha kriyāyāḥ na asti sattvam kecid tu artha kriyā kāritayā abhimatāḥ satya svapne viṣayāḥ dṛṣṭa kāla bheda vyabhicāriṇaḥ na santi eva iti prakaraṇa arthaḥ 
DhPr_26.3	 idam īdṛś viśiṣṭam svapna jñānam udāha rataḥ dharma uttarasya ayam āśayaḥ evaṃvidhasya svapna jñānasya sat artha tva abhimānaḥ keṣāñcid satya svapna vādinām asti iti tad abhimāna śamanāya idam mayā udāha raṇīkṛtam na tu asmāt anyasya svapna jñānasya kaścid viśeṣaḥ sarvasya eva svapna jñānasya nirālambana tayā mithyājñāna tvāt iti 
DhPr_26.4	 idānīm paricchidyamānasya yad kālam paricchedanam tad kālam eva prāpyamāṇasya prāpaṇam abhimatam evam bruvate iti matvā asya arthasya anupapattim codayati nanu ca iti deśe niyatam ākāre niyatam ca śakyam prāpayitum iti abhidadhānaḥ anayoḥ avi pratipattim āha idam tu na sambhāvyate iti āha yad kālam tu iti tunā anantara uktābhyām vidhābhyām vaidharmyam āha yaḥ kālosya paricchedanasya tat yathā bhavati tathā paricchinnam sa kālaḥ yasya prāpaṇasya tat yathā bhavati tathā na śakyam prāpayitum yasmin kāle paricchinnam tasmin kāle na śakyate prāpayitum iti arthaḥ evam ca bruvatā anena kāla antara grāhi iti yat uktam tat ayuktam iti darśitam sarvasya eva jñānasya evaṃśīla tvāt iti 
DhPr_26.5	 na ucyate ityādinā siddhānta vādī ca udakasya anukta upālambham āha anena api na kiñci tkāraṇam uktam tat kim tvayā evam na ucyate iti pārśva stham pratyasya eva abhiprāyam prakāśayati anyaḥ hi iti hi iti yasmāt yadi evam na ucyate tarhi kim nāma ucyate iti āha kintu iti nipāta anipāta samudāyaḥ ayam kevalam iti asya arthe 
DhPr_27.1^1	 nanu asaṅgatam idam vākyam na hi yat eva paricchinnam iti asti yena evamucyeta yad kālam tu paricchinnam tad kālam iti tu yuktam vaktum na tat eva iti satyam etat kevalam bodhe yatnaḥ karaṇīyaḥ yad kālam iti anena hi tad kālam iti prāptam tat eva iti tad śabdena vastu viṣayaḥ yat śabdaḥ ākṛṣyate tatas ayam arthaḥ yad kālam paricchinnam yat vastu tad kālam tat eva vastu prāpaṇīyam iti aho gaḍu praveśe akṣi tārā niḥ gamaḥ jātaḥ evam khalu vākyam syāt samarthitam pūrva pakṣāt punar asya aviśeṣaḥ prāptaḥ asti viśeṣaḥ mahān kevalam bhavatā na samīcīnam nirūpitaḥ tathā hi pūrva pakṣa avasthāyām yad kālam tad kālam iti ca atra bahuvrīhiṇā paricchedana lakṣaṇā prāpaṇa lakṣaṇā ca kriyā abhidhīyate 
DhPr_27.1^2	 idānīm punarvastutas na ayam arthaḥ yat vastu yena kālena sambaddham paricchinnam tat eva tena kālena sambaddham svarūpeṇa prāpaṇīyam tadā anyadā vā paricchedasya yādṛśaḥ kālaḥ tasmin kāle yat vidyamānam tat eva prāpaṇīyam iti yāvat tatas ca pariccheda kālā asataḥ yat grāhakam tat na pramāṇam iti avatiṣṭhate na ucyate yasmin kālaḥ ityādinā ca yat etat uktam tat bāhya prāpaṇa abhiprāyeṇa draṣṭavyam paramārthataḥ tu jñānasya pradarśanāt anyaḥ prāpaṇa vyāpāraḥ na asti iti yasmin= eva kāle paricchidyate arthaḥ tasmin= eva kāle prāpyate iti etat ca anantaram eva anena eva vistareṇa pratipāditam iti sva vacana vyāghātaḥ anyathā asya syāt iti 
DhPr_27.2	 nanu evam api pariccheda kāla varttinaḥ prāpaṇam na sambhavati eva sarvasya eva viṣayasya kṣaṇika tvāt tathā ca upadarśita artha prāpaka tvam nāma kasyacid api jñānasya na asti iti asambhavitā eva samyak jñāna tva lakṣaṇasya syāt iti āśaṅkya āha abheda iti abhedena eka rūpa tvena tat eva idam iti ākāreṇa adhyavasāyāt upādāna upādeya kṛtakṣaṇa prabandhaḥ santānaḥ tad gataḥ tad āśritaḥ 
DhPr_27.3	 ayam asya bhāvaḥ sāṃvyavahārikasya iha pramāṇasya lakṣaṇam ucyate tena na ekāntena vastu sthitiḥ apekṣyate tatra yadi api vastu sthityā paricchinna prāpyayoḥ nānātvam tathā api vyavaharttāraḥ nirantara apara apara utpatteḥ avidyā vaśāt ca hetu phala rūpam kṣaṇa pracayam tat eva idam iti eka tvena adhimuñcanti tatas pariccheda kāla bhāvinaḥ prāpaṇam sambhavati eva itiḥ samyak jñāna pada vyākhyāna parisamāptau 
DhPr_27.4–28.1	 tat anena prabandhena samyak jñāna padam vyākhyāya adhunā pūrva śabdam vyāci khyāsuḥ tena sārdham asya vigraham āha samyak jñānam iti nanu puruṣa artha siddhiḥ samyak jñānasya prayojanam kāryatvena tathā ca samyak jñāna kāraṇikā iti vaktum ucitam tat kim evam uktam iti āha kāryāt iti anena vyavasthā vācī san= ā iva pūrva śabdaḥ kāraṇe varttate iti darśayati 
DhPr_28.2	 bhavat iti lakṣaṇa hetvoḥ kriyāyāḥ iti hetau śatuḥ vidhānāt hetu padam etat yadi evam kāraṇa śabdaḥ eva kriyatām iti āha kāraṇa iti ayam bhāvaḥ karoti iti kāraṇam ucyate na tu akurvat rūpam akurvati punar kāraṇa vyapadeśaḥ kāraṇa kāraṇa tvādī pa cārikaḥ na ca mukhye sambhavati amukhye pratyayaḥ yujyate tatas yat eva jñānam avyavadhānena puruṣa artha siddheḥ nibandhanam tat eva kāraṇa śabdena pratīyeta iti yadi pūrva grahaṇe api evam pratyayaḥ tadā kaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti āha pūrva śabdaḥ iti tuḥ kāraṇa śabdāt viśeṣam asya āha pūrva mātram iti sākṣātkāraṇam itarat ca 
DhPr_28.3	 nanūbhayoḥ sambhave sākṣātkāraṇa parihāreṇa itara grahaṇāya pūrva śabdaḥ śobhate na ca evam asti sarvasya eva puruṣa artha siddhim prati sākṣātkāraṇa tvāt iti āha dvividham ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe katham dvaividhyam iti āha artha kriyā iti nirbhāsate asmin= iti nirbhāsaḥ artha kriyāyāḥ nirbhāsaḥ yasmāt tat tathā yatas sādhana jñānāt anantaram dāha ādi pratibhāsa jñānam utpadyate tat evam ucyate 
DhPr_28.4	 kecid tu kṣaṇena kārya kāraṇa vyavahārasya arvāk darśanena karttum aśakyatvāt dāha ādi pratibhāsam eva jñānam evam bruvate artha kriyāyāḥ nirbhāsaḥ asmin= iti kṛtvā aparam artha kriyā samarthe ca pravarttakam yat pravṛtti samadhigamya artha kriyā gocaram tat evam uktam caḥ artha kriyā nirbhāsa apekṣayā samuccaye anayoḥ kim parīkṣyate iti āha tayoḥ iti pravarttakam api sākṣāt kāraṇam tat kaḥ anyatra vidveṣaḥ yena idam eva vicāryate kim vā pūrva śabdena iti āha tat ca iti caḥ yasmāt 
DhPr_28.5	 ayam āśayaḥ yatas pravarttante tat sarvam artha prāpteḥ vyavahitam kāraṇam atas ca sambhavat pratibandham tat pravṛtti aṅga tvāt pūrva mātram na tu anantaram kāraṇam iti pūrva mātra abhidhānena sāntaram amum eva draḍhayan= āha na tu iti tuḥ viśeṣa arthaḥ kutas etat iti āha samyak jñānaḥ iti hiḥ yasmāt tasmin samyak jñāne prakaraṇāt sādhana nirbhāse sati smṛti bīja upajanana yogya jñāna jñātasya dāha ādeḥ smaraṇam tatas abhilāṣaḥ tad prāpti icchā tatas pravṛttiḥ pravarttaka jñāna upadarśitam artham prāptu kāmā vyāpāra sahāyā buddhiḥ tasyāḥ ca prāptiḥ upāditsita lābhaḥ yasmāt smaraṇa ādinā vyavadhānam tatas tasmāt na sākṣāt hetuḥ prāpteḥ upāyaḥ puruṣa artha siddheḥ iti prakaraṇāt 
DhPr_29.1–29.2	 yadi paramparayā api prāpti hetuḥ parīkṣyate tarhi sākṣāt hetuḥ atitarām parīkṣaṇīyaḥ iti āha artha kriyā nirbhāsam iti tuḥ pravarttaka adhyakṣāt artha kriyā nirbhāsam bheda vat darśayati yadā prāpti hetuḥ iti pāṭhaḥ tadā artha kriyā nirbhāsam iti asya antya vyākhyāna pakṣe bhinnā santoṣa ādi prāptiḥ loka adhyavasāya siddhā yā tasyāḥ hetuḥ prāpti pāṭhe tu tad vyākhyānān avadya tā pūrva vyākhyāne tu upacārāt prāpti hetuḥ prāpti śabdena vaktavyaḥ karaṇa sādhanaḥ vā prāpti śabdaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ 
DhPr_29.3–29.4	 kasmāt tat na parīkṣyate iti āha yatra eva hi iti hiḥ yasmāt sa āśaṅkāḥ sa sandehāḥ āśaṅka agrahaṇasya upalakṣaṇa tvāt sa viparyāsā iti api draṣṭavyam evam bruvataḥ ca ayam āśayaḥ na vyasanam etat śāstra kṛtaḥ yena jñānam aparīkṣamāṇaḥ svāsthyam alabhamānaḥ parīkṣate kintarhi vyutpādya jana prayojana uddeśena ayam asya ārambhaḥ saṃśaya viparyāsa apasāraṇam ca vyutpādya jana prayojanam tatas yatra eva te tathā apravṛttayaḥ tat eva parīkṣyate iti artha kriyā nirbhāse api te tathā āvṛttayaḥ iti āha artha kriyā iti caśabdaḥ tuśabdasya arthe 
DhPr_29.5–29.6	 kutas na tathā āvṛttayaḥ yena sākṣātkāraṇe asmin sati siddhaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ tena anantaram eva phalasya anubhūyamāna tvāt tadā eva santoṣa ādi gamanāt vā vyākhyāna dvaya ipi artha kriyā nirbhāsa śabda vācya dvaye sthite dvayam etat śaṅkāyāḥ kāraṇam anantara phala adarśanam adhyavasāya siddha bhinna prāpti abhāvaḥ vā tad abhāve tu katham śaṅkeran= iti bhāvaḥ mā bhūvan= tatra sa āśaṅkāḥ tat kim siddham iti āha atas iti 
DhPr_29.7–29.8	 yadi vyavahitam pravarttakam puruṣa artha siddheḥ na kāraṇam tarhi katham uktam kāryāt pūrvam bhavat kāraṇam pūrvam uktam iti asākṣāt kāraṇe ca akāraṇe kāraṇa viśeṣaṇam sākṣāt iti nirarthakam iti āśaṅkya āha tasmāt iti yasmāt sākṣāt kāraṇam āśaṅkān āspadam sat aparīkṣaṇīyam tasmāt yat asākṣāt kāraṇam ata eva ca parīkṣā arham parīkṣā yogyam pravarttakam samyak jñānam ādarśayitum ādarśayiṣyāmi iti kāraṇa śabdam vihāya pūrva grahaṇam kṛtam ācāryeṇa iti arthāt etat uktam bhavati yaḥ ayam kāraṇa śabdaḥ vyavahite kāraṇa kāraṇe varttate na ayam tatra abhidhāyaka tvena varttate karoti iti kāraṇam iti vyutpatteḥ kintarhi tādarthyāt upacārate iti 
DhPr_30.1	 syāt etat sati api kāraṇa grahaṇe vicāra arham eva samyak jñānam pratipatsyate yatas tat vyutpādyate iti arthaḥ sādhya tvāt prātipadikā arthaḥ tu kāraka tvāt guṇaḥ pradhāna anuyāyī tena pradhāna anurodhāt tad śabdaḥ varṇitayā nītyā mukhyasya kāraṇasya samyak jñānasya vyutpatti karma tā a nupapatteḥ tad parityāgena lakṣaṇayā tādarthya bhūtayā pratyāsattyā artha kriyā samartha pravarttakaḥ eva pravarttiṣyate yathā mañcāḥ krośanti iti atra pradhāna anurodhāt mañca śabdaḥ krośana kriyā karttṛ tva anupapatteḥ mukhyam artham tyaktvā lakṣaṇayā tātsthya bhūtayā pratyāsattyā puruṣeṣu varttate iti satyam etat kevalam evam sati vyākhyātṛṇām idam kauśalam syāt na śāstra kṛtaḥ iti sarvam anavadyam 
DhPr_30.2	 idānīm puruṣa artha siddhi padam vivariṣuḥ puruṣa śabdena sārdham artha śabdasya vigraham arthasya ca svarūpam puruṣasya ityādinā ācaṣṭe arthyate iti ācakṣāṇaḥ artha yācñāyām iti atas ṇijantāt karmaṇyacam darśayati arthyate iti asya artham spaṣṭayati kāmyate iṣyate iti anena yāvān eva arthaḥ uktaḥ tāvān eva arthyate iti anena api iti iti yāvat iti asya arthaḥ 
DhPr_30.3–30.5	 kaḥ asau= arthaḥ iti āha heyaḥ iti vā śabdaḥ ca śabdasya arthe arthyamānaḥ iṣyamāṇaḥ arthaḥ na tarhi heyaḥ arthaḥ iti āha heyaḥ iti hiḥ yasmāt heyaḥ hātum tyaktum iṣyate tasmāt arthaḥ ayam āśayaḥ iṣyamāṇaḥ khalu arthaḥ atra yadi api svīkaraṇa icchā na asti tathā api parihāra icchā tāvat asti iti yadi hātum iṣyamāṇaḥ arthaḥ katham upādeyaḥ arthaḥ iti āha upādeyaḥ api iṣyate kevalam upādātum na kevalam heyaḥ iṣyate iti apiśabdaḥ nanu ca na heya upādeyau= arthaḥ api tu anyopi tatas saḥ api kasmāt na pradarśyate iti āha na ca iti ca uvadhāraṇe yasmāt arthe vā nanūpekṣaṇīyaḥ api rāśiḥ asti yatra na pravṛttiḥ yatas ca na nivṛttiḥ tat katham anubhava siddhasya apahnavaḥ iti āha upekṣaṇīyaḥ iti hiḥ yasmāt 
DhPr_30.6	 atra kaścid āha yathā asau= anupādeyaḥ tathā ahaya upi tatra yadi anupādeya tvāt heyaḥ tadā aheya tvāt upādeyaḥ kim na bhavati iti sādhu uktam tena bhadantena kevalam heya śabda artha vicāre manaḥ na praṇihitam tathā hi hīyate tyajyate na svīkriyate iti heyaḥ hānañcāsvīkaraṇam na tu gṛhītvā parityāgaḥ tena ahi viṣa kaṇṭaka ādīnām api hānam tatrā apravṛttiḥ eva sā ca upekṣaṇīye api asti tathā ca yadi tasya svīkāraḥ bhavet tadā aheya tvam siddhim adhyāsīta na ca tat svīkriyate iti vyakta mayam hetuḥ asiddhaḥ tasya na tu asmākam asiddhaḥ anupādeya tvasya asvīkarttavya tvasya siddha tvāt 
DhPr_31.1	 atha anubhava siddhasya tṛtīya rāśeḥ upekṣaṇīyasya asvīkaraṇa mātrāt heyena sārdham aikya pratipādanam ayuktam iti ced priyam uktam priyeṇa na hi vayam api prasiddhayoḥ heya upekṣaṇīyayoḥ arthayoḥ eka svabhāva tām ātiṣṭhāmahe kintu kriyā nimittena heya śabdena eka abhidhānam tathā asvīkaraṇa arthena hāna śabdena upekṣāyāḥ abhidhānam iti kim avadyam etat ca heya upādeya tvam arthasya eka puruṣa eka kāla apekṣayā pratyeyam 
DhPr_31.2–31.3	 adhunā siddhi śabdasya artha padena vigraham bruvan= artham āha tasya iti nanu loke siddhiḥ niṣpattiḥ ucyate yathā odanasya siddhiḥ iti tat katham evam varṇyate iti āha hetu nibandhana iti hetuḥ kāraṇam nibaddhyate asmin= iti nibandhanam pratibandha viṣayaḥ hetuḥ nibandhanam asyāḥ iti vigṛhya hetu pratibaddhā iti arthaḥ vaktavyaḥ 
DhPr_31.4–31.5	 yadi janaka nibandhanā siddhiḥ īdṛśī tarhi jñāna nibandhanā kīdṛśī bhaviṣyati iti āha jñāna iti tuḥ pūrvasyāḥ siddheḥ asyāḥ bhedam darśayati evam ca vyācakṣāṇa artha pada vyākhyāne arthaḥ prayojanam dāha ādi siddhi pada vyākhyāne ca tasya dāha ādeḥ niṣpattiḥ iti yat vinīta deva śānta bhadrau vyācakṣātām tat dvayam api apāsyati yatas sva hetoḥ eva vahni ādeḥ dāha ādeḥ niṣpattiḥ na tu jñānāt tasya tat akāraka tvāt iti nanu yadi siddhiḥ anuṣṭhānam tarhi hānam upādānam ca katham siddhiḥ iti āha heyasya ca iti caḥ hetau avadhāraṇe vā hānam iti asmāt paraḥ draṣṭavyaḥ dvitīyaḥ cakāraḥ samuccaya arthaḥ kim evam sati siddham iti āha tatas iti yatas jñāna nibandhanā siddhiḥ īdṛśī tatas tasmāt kāraṇāt 
DhPr_31.6	 puruṣa artha siddhi śabdānām vigraham artham ca vyākhyāya samprati sarva śabdam vyākhyātum vigraham āha sarvā ca iti evam ca vigṛhṇan yat vinīta devena vyākhyātam sarvaḥ ca asau laukikaḥ lokottaraḥ ca āsanna deśaḥ dūra deśaḥ ca puruṣa arthaḥ ca iti tathā tasya siddhiḥ itiḥ tat dūṣayati evam hi vyākhyāyamāne sarva śabdena puruṣa artha siddheḥ aviśeṣaṇāt mithyājñānāt kākatālīya artha siddhiḥ anivāritā syāt na ca sā sambhavinī yathā ca sā na sambhavati tathā anantaram eva pratipādayiṣyate 
DhPr_32.1–32.2	 yaḥ api śānta bhadraḥ sarvaḥ ca asau puruṣa arthaḥ ca sarveṣām vā puruṣāṇām arthaḥ tasya siddhiḥ iti vyācaṣṭe saḥ api anayā eva dvārā nirākṛtaḥ nanu sarva śabdasya prakārakārtsnya vṛtteḥ api darśanāt na jñāyate kiṃvṛttiḥ atra abhipretaḥ iti āha sarva śabdaḥ iti dravyasya niḥśeṣa tāyām vṛttaḥ pravṛttaḥ vācaka bhāvena yathā sarva utpattimatām īśvaraḥ nimitta kāraṇam iti atra dravya śabdena ca idam tat iti vyapadeśa yogyam grahītavyam na tu vaiśeṣika siddhānta prasiddham pṛthivī ādi tat uktam 
DhPr_32.3	 puruṣa artha siddhiḥ api idam tat iti vyapadeśa yogyā tena sā api dravyam tathā vṛtteḥ asya grahaṇāt anya vṛtti tayā prasiddhasya api pratiṣedham kaṇṭha uktam karoti vṛttaḥ iti varttate yathā pūrve vyācakṣate sarva rasa bhoktā ayam bhikṣākaḥ iti yathā ayam sarva śabdaḥ prakārakārtsnya vācī tadvat atra api iti prakārakārtsnya vṛtteḥ agrahaṇe kaḥ guṇaḥ iti āha tatas iti tatas prakārakārtsnya vṛttasya agrahaṇat tathā api katham ayam arthaḥ bhavati iti ced bhavati hi prakārakārtsnya vacane sarva śabde sati ayam arthaḥ na saḥ asti puruṣa artha siddheḥ prakāraḥ phala lakṣaṇaḥ upādāna lakṣaṇaḥ vā yaḥ na samyak jñāna nibandhanaḥ iti sati ca evam dvi prakārā api siddhiḥ samyak jñāna pūrvikā iti ayam arthaḥ bhavati 
DhPr_32.4–32.5	 nanu ca asmin= api arthe prakāra dvitayasya saṃgṛhīta tvāt kim asaṃgṛhītam nāma yena ayam arthaḥ yatnena mahatā hīyate iti katham na hīyatām kasyāścid tad prakāra antar patitāyāḥ hāna vyakte na hi ṣaṣ api rasa prakārān bhuñjānaḥ kaścid madhura amla ādi rasa vyaktīḥ sarvāḥ eva bhuṅkte na ca tathā akurvan sarva rasa bhoktā na bhavati iti yadi ayam na arthaḥ kaḥ tarhi iti āha api tu iti nipāta samudāyaḥ ayam kintu iti asya arthe sarvatra varttate 
DhPr_32.6^1	 nanu kṛtsnā eva asau samyak jñāna nibandhanā iti ucyamāne mithyājñānāt kākatālīyā api artha siddhiḥ na asti iti darśitam syāt na ca etat yujyate yatas yadi api mithyājñānāt niyamavatī na asti artha siddhiḥ tathā api kādācid kī vidyate eva yathā kaścid dahana uparivarttim maśaka varttim dhūmam avasāya agnim anumāya yadi pravṛttyā agnim āsādayati atas eva ca mithyājñānasya kādācid ka artha siddhi nibandhana tvāt samyak jñānasya tu niyamena artha siddhi nibandhana hetu tvāt samyak jñānam eva yatnataḥ vyutpādyate na tu etāvatā mithyājñānāt na asti eva artha siddhiḥ 
DhPr_32.6^2	 prakāra kārtsnya vṛtta grahaṇe tu na ayam doṣaḥ evam hi samyak jñāna asādhyaḥ para prakāraḥ nirākriyate na tu tad prakāra antar pātinyāḥ kasyāścid siddhi vyakteḥ mithyā jñāna sādhya tvam na ca hāna upādāna vyaktayaḥ pratyekam prakāra śabda vācyāḥ prakāra ānantya prasaṅgāt tasmāt sarva śabdaḥ prakārakārtsnya vṛttiḥ eva grahītavyaḥ iti pūrveṣām matam āśaṅkya āha mithyā iti kāka tālayoḥ saṃyogaḥ iva ākasmikī kākatālīyāḥ kutas na asti iti āha tathā hi iti tatas iti mithyājñānāt tat api prāpayati eva iti āha pradarśitam iti caḥ yasmāt 
DhPr_33.1	 pradarśitam prāpayat api mithyājñānam bhaviṣyati tatas samyak jñānam eva iti avadhāraṇam ayuktam iti āha pradarśitam iti caḥ avadhāraṇe aprāpayat iti atas paraḥ draṣṭavyaḥ lakṣaṇa hetvoḥ iti hetau śatuḥ vidhānāt pradarśita artha aprāpaṇāt eva mithyājñāna miti arthaḥ mithyājñānasya hi idam eva tattvam yat pradarśitāprāpaka tvam nāma prāpake tu mithyājñāna vyapadeśaḥ samāropitaḥ syāt iti bhāvaḥ mā bhūt prāpakam tad artha siddheḥ tu nibandhanam kim na syāt iti āha aprāpakam iti caḥ yasmāt arthe 
DhPr_33.2	 tasmāt ityādinā ukta artha upasaṃhāram karoti yasmāt upadarśita aprāpakam eva mithyājñānam tasmāt yat kiñcit mithyājñānam tatas sarvatas eva na artha siddhiḥ yaḥ punar akasmāt vahneḥ upari maśaka varttim dhūmam avasāya vahnim avasyati saḥ api anumāna kālāt pūrvam yāvat maśaka vartti ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛttam vahni kāryam niyatam dhūma rūpam nirūpya vivecitam tadānīm anumāna kāle na anusarati tad anusaraṇe bhrāntya yogāt tāvat anivarttiṃte saṃśaya hetau tiṣṭhatu tāvat maśaka vartti darśanam satya dhūma darśane api sandigdha vahni kārya tvāt katham niḥśaṅkaḥ nāma sa cetanaḥ tasmāt niścita niyata rūpāt eva dhūmāt vahni niścayaḥ anyasmāt tu eka aṃśa avagrahaḥ api anivartita śaṅkā hetuḥ saṃśayaḥ eva saṃśayaḥ ca bhāva abhāva aniyatasya arthasya aśakya prāpaṇasya darśakaḥ na artha siddheḥ nibandhanam jñāna antarāt eva tu sā prāptiḥ iti asya abhiprāyaḥ evam anyatra api mithyājñāne yathā prāmāṇyam na yujyate yathā ca jñāna antarāt eva sā prāptiḥ tathā dharma uttareṇa eva viniścaya ṭīkāyām vipañcitam iti na iha pratanyate 
DhPr_33.3	 kutaścid artha siddhiḥ api syāt iti āha yatas ca iti caḥ anyasmāt bheda vat rūpam upadarśayati artha siddhi nibandhanam mithyājñānam ācāryasya api na abhimatam iti sāmarthyāt darśayati yadā aaha atas eva iti yatas eva mithyājñānāt artha siddhiḥ na asti samyak jñānāt ca asti eva atas asmāt eva hetoḥ yatna grahaṇam anuṣaṅgeṇa mithyājñāna vyutpādanam darśayati mithyājñānasya api kasyacid vyutpādanāt iti ukta prāyam atas eva iti anena yat eva hetu tvena apekṣitam tat eva yatas ityādinā sukha pratipatti artham kaṇṭha uktam karoti ayam āśayaḥ yadi ācāryaḥ mithyājñānāt api artha siddhim bhavitrīm abhipreyāt tadā na samyak jñānam eva prastāreṇa vyutpādayet tat eva ca tathā vyutpāditavān atas avasīyate na eva tasya idam abhipretam iti 
DhPr_33.4	 nanu samyak jñāna pūrvikā eva iti avadhāraṇe sati mithyājñānāt artha siddhiḥ na asti iti labhyate na ca upāttam avadhāraṇam tat katham ayam arthaḥ labhyate iti āha tatas iti yatas sarva śabde dravya kārtsnya vṛttau sati sarvā kṛtsnā puruṣa artha siddhiḥ samyak jñāna pūrvikā na tu kācid vyaktiḥ asti yā na tad pūrvikā iti ayam arthaḥ labhyate tatas kāraṇāt puruṣa artha siddhiḥ samya jñāna nibandhana eva iti sa avadhāraṇam vākyam yat parimāṇam abhidheyam brūyāt vaktum śaknoti tāvat parimāṇam uktam sarvā samya jñāna pūrvikā iti anena varttatām iti śabdaḥ tasmāt iti asya arthe kva punar yat śabdaḥ asti yena vakṣyamāṇa artha saṅgatiḥ iti āha yat iti caḥ vyaktam etat iti asmin= arthe śabdayoḥ sākṣāt anyonya apekṣā bhāvāt yat tad arthayoḥ iti draṣṭavyam abhisambandhaḥ vyapekṣā evam sati kīdṛśaḥ arthaḥ vyavatiṣṭhate iti āha tat iti 
DhPr_34.1^1	 nanu bahuvrīhau guṇībhūtam samyak jñānam tat katham tasya apradhānasya pradhāna pratyavamarśinā tad śabde parāmarśaḥ syāt iti āha yadi api ca iti yadi api ca iti nipāta samudāyaḥ viśeṣa abhidhāna artha abhyupagame barttate mahābhāṣye ca ayam prāyeṇa dṛśyate samāsaḥ iti samāsa arthaḥ iti arthaḥ vyutpādayitavya tvāt pradhānam iti abhidadhataḥ ayam āśayaḥ dvedhā hi prādhānyam śabdataḥ arthataḥ ca tatra śābdena nyāyena asati api prādhānye samyak jñānasya vyutpādayitavya tayā buddhi antareṇa upasthāpitasya svatantrasyā aarthena nyāyena prādhānyam kaḥ apahastayet iti tad śabdena tasya parāmarśaḥ na viruddhi atas iti evam vyācakṣāṇaḥ vinīta deva vyākhyām tiraskaroti 
DhPr_34.1^2–35.1	 evam hi asau vyācaṣṭe tat iti napuṃsa kaliṅgena nirdeśāt samyak jñānam parāmṛśyate iti samyak jñānasya aprādhānyena parāmarśa anupapattau tad liṅga grahaṇasya eva ayogāt katham asiddhena sādhyatām iti āśayaḥ tatas prādhānyāt tasya eva samyak jñānasya tad śabdena sambandhanam sambandhaḥ svīkāraḥ iti yāvat tatas ayam arthaḥ tat samyak jñānam karma bhūtam vipratipatti nirākaraṇena pratipādyate bodhyate śiṣya janaḥ iti arthāt atas eva tat iti dvitīya antam etat iti sa upapattikam āha samayam smāryate paraḥ iti yathā vipratipatti nirākaraṇena pratipādyate iti bruvatā lakṣaṇam nam virudhyate prasiddhāni pramāṇāni ityādi tat apahastitam veditavyam nanu vārttika ādinā eva samyak jñānasya vyutpādanāt katham asya na vaiyarthyam iti ced saṃkṣipta rucīn prājñān adhikṛtya idam prakaraṇam praṇītam iti adoṣaḥ
