DhPr_108.5–108.7	 tathā svabhāve api hetau bahavaḥ vipratipedire kecid artha antara apekṣiṇī api dharme svabhāvam hetu madhya vasitāḥ kecid tu vastunaḥ dharma viśeṣam āśritam svabhāvam iti tad vipratipatti nirākaraṇa artham tayoḥ lakṣaṇam ākhyātam atra tu kārya tva rūpe na kecid vipratipadyante iti na asya lakṣaṇam uktam iti kārya kāraṇa bhāvena gamya gamaka bhāve sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāva prasaṅga iti ādikāyām vipratipattau= api na kāryasya lakṣaṇe vipratipatti kintarhi tasya gamaka tve sā ca anyatra nirākṛtā atra api prājñaiḥ svayam abhyūhyā prājña jana adhikāreṇa asya prārambhāt iti samprati trirūpāṇi ca trīṇi eva iti asahamānaḥ prāha nanu iti nanu praśnaḥ athaśabdaḥ yadi śabdasya arthe prakārasya svarūpasya bhedāt viśeṣāt bhedaḥ nānātvam evam abhyupagame sati ekasya iti abhinnasya abhinna tvañca asvabhāva hetu tu a vyāvṛtteḥ sarvatra bhāvāt 
DhPr_109.1	 ananta prakāra tvāt iti bruvataḥ ayam bhāvaḥ sa viśeṣaṇa nirviśeṣaṇa vyatirikta avyatirikta viśeṣaṇa tva ādi bhedena ananta svabhāva tvāt iti gamakau= iti vivṛṇvan sādhayate iti sādhanau= iti karttari lyuṭam darśayati atra ca vastunaḥ sādhanau= eva iti avadhāraṇīyam na tu vastunaḥ eva iti itara vyavacchedasya api tābhyām sādhanāt pratipattṛ adhyavasāya anurodhāt tu vidhi sādhana tvam anayoḥ ucyate pratiṣedhasya hetuḥ eva iti avadhāraṇīyam na tu ayam eva iti pūrvābhyām api sāmarthyāt pratiṣedhasya sādhanāt 
DhPr_109.2	 nanu na dṛśya anupalambhena abhāvaḥ sādhyate tasya pratyakṣa siddha tvāt kintu vyavahāraḥ tat katham pratiṣedhaḥ anupalambha sādhyaḥ atha abhāva vyavahāraḥ pratiṣedhaḥ ucyate tarhi vyāpaka anupalambha ādinā vyāpya ādi a bhāve sādhye kena abhāvaḥ sādhitaḥ tatas kim atra pratiṣedha śabdena pratipattavyam iti āśaṅkya āha pratiṣedhaḥ iti itiḥ pratiṣedha śabdam pratyavamṛśati 
DhPr_109.3	 tena pratiṣedhaḥ iti anena śabdena abhāvaḥ abhāva vyavahāraḥ ca uktaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iti arthaḥ ekasya pratiṣedhena iti mukhyayā vṛttyā saṅgrahaḥ anyasya pratiṣedha āśraya tayā gauṇyā vṛttyā iti bhāvaḥ na asti iti jñānam na asti iti abhidhānam niḥśaṅkā atra gamana āgamana lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ vyavahāraḥ sa ca haṭhāt pravarttayitum na śakyate iti tad yogya tā eva sādhya iti draṣṭavyam evam tu svabhāva hetau= antarbhāve api anupalambhasya tatas pṛthak karaṇam pratipad tradhyavasāya vaśāt itya vaseyam 
DhPr_109.4	 nanu vidhi pratiṣedha sādhana tve api amīṣām tri rūpa tvam aviśiṣṭam tattvāt eva ca abhedaḥ coditaḥ tat katham idam uttaram pūrva pakṣam ativartta tām iti āśaṅkya āha tat ayam iti yasmāt idam uttarīkṛtam ācāryeṇa yathāśruti ca pūrva pakṣam na atikrāmati tat tasmāt ayam arthaḥ vākyasya ayam tātparya arthaḥ iti arthaḥ etam eva artham hetuḥ iti ādinā na tu svatas eva iti antena granthena pratipādayati 
DhPr_109.5	 atha katham anyaḥ arthaḥ anyam artham na vyabhicarati yena ete trayaḥ hetavaḥ yathā ca amīṣām sva sādhya sādhanāt gamaka tvam tathā a nyeṣām api akārya svabhāva anupalambha ātmanām kim na bhavati iti manvānaḥ praśnena upakramate kasmāt iti kasmāt iti sāmānyatas hetum pṛcchati punar iti viśeṣataḥ trayāṇām anupalabdhi ādīnām caḥ pūrva nimitta apekṣayā nimitta antara samuccaya arthaḥ anyeṣa āmanīdṛśa ātmanām saṃyogi ādīnām 
DhPr_110.1	 svabhāvena svarūpeṇa sādhanam kṛtāiti pāṇinīya bhāṣya kārasya idam sūtram tena karttṛ karaṇe kṛtā bahulam iti sūtram apanīya galeca upakaḥ ityādi siddhi artha sādhanam kṛtā iti sūtram kṛtam vārttika sūtrikāṇām tu tṛtīyāḥ iti yoga vibhāgāt samāsaḥ avaseyaḥ anena ca tṛtīyā samāsena eva kārya svabhāvayoḥ saṃgrahāt āvṛttyā ṣaṣṭhī saptamī samāsābhyām kārya svabhāvayoḥ saṃgrahaḥ iti yat pūrvaiḥ vyākhyātam tat apavyākhyānam iti khyāpitam 
DhPr_110.2–110.3	 samastasya padasya artham āha svabhāva iti anena pratibandha śabdena pratibaddha tvam āyatta tvam ucyate iti darśayati asya eva artham spaṣṭayati pratibaddhā iti yaḥ sva rūpeṇa kvacid āyattaḥ tasya svabhāvaḥ tatra pratibaddhaḥ āyatta iti artha abhedena pratibaddha svabhāva tvam iti arthaḥ iti spaṣṭīkṛtam nanu pūrveṣām abhimata samāsa vyudāsena tṛtīyā samāsam darśayatā kiṃsvidati yaḥ labdhaḥ kevalam āhopuruṣikā prakāśitā iti āśaṅkya pūrvam buddhi stham eva sphuṭayitum āha kāraṇaḥ iti kasya asau 
DhPr_111.1	 pratibandhaḥ itya kāṅkṣāyām āha kārya svabhāvayoḥ tayoḥ eva prakṛta tvāt aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ dvayoḥ api kārya svabhāvayoḥ atiśaye saṅgrahaḥ svīkāraḥ ayam eva atiśayaḥ iti bhāvaḥ sādhana lakṣaṇaḥ arthaḥ sādhya lakṣaṇam artham gamayet bodhayitum śavanoti yatas evam tasmāt anyeṣām tad vyatiriktānām teṣām svabhāva pratibandha abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ ca teṣām tādātmya tad utpatti abhāvāt tad anyasya ca sambandhasya abhāvāt tādātmya tad utpatti bhāve ca kārya svabhāvayoḥ eva antarbhāvaḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
DhPr_111.2	 tat ityādinā samāsam pradarśya tad apratibaddhasya iti yojayatā dharma uttareṇa mūle tad apratibaddhasya iti pāṭhaḥ darśitaḥ dṛśyate ca bahuśas tad apratibaddha svabhāvasya iti pāṭhaḥ tatra api pāṭhe tad apratibaddhaḥ sādhya apratibaddhaḥ svabhāvaḥ svarūpam yasya liṅgasya iti vigrahaḥ kāryaḥ pratibandhaḥ pratibaddha tvam āyatta tvam yat sādhanasya tasya viṣayaḥ avyabhicāraḥ tena vinā abhavitṛ tvam tasya niyamaḥ avaśyantā 
DhPr_111.3	 nanu tad apratibaddha tve api adyatanaḥ āditya udayaḥ astam ayam apratibandha viṣayam na vyabhicarati iti āśaṅkya āha tat ayam arthaḥ iti yatas evam uktam tat tasmāt ayam tātparya arthaḥ āditya udayaḥ api hi bhaviṣyati na ca tad ahar astamayaḥ mahā ṛṣiṇā anyena vā mahā rdhinā kenacid tasya astamaya vibandha sambhavāt tasmāt ādityasya tasmāt astamaya yoḥyata eva sādhyāḥ ayam āditya udayaḥ astamaya yogyaḥ udaya tvāt śvas tana udaya vat iti sati ca evam svabhāva hetu tvam asya āyātam iti bhāvaḥ 
DhPr_111.4–111.5	 nanu ca avyabhicāra mātreṇa prayojanam tat kim niyamena iti āha avyabhicāra iti caḥ avadhāraṇe hetau vā etat eva kutas iti āha na hi iti hiḥ yasmāt pradīpaḥ vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ api tu kintva vyabhicāri tvena sādhyasya prakṛta tvāt sādhya avinābhāvi tvena niścitam niyama abhāve ca kutas avyabhicāra niścayaḥ iti asya tātparya arthaḥ niścīyatām tat avyabhicāraḥ anyeṣām api pratibandhaḥ tu kasmāt mṛgyate iti āha tatas iti yatas avaśyam avyabhicāraḥ niścetavyaḥ tatas tasmāt anyathā avyabhicāraḥ eva na śakyate niścetum iti arthāt anena darśitam etāvatā api katham gamaka tvam iti āha tatas iti tatas niścitāt avyabhicārāt liṅgasya gamaka tve middhe sādhyasya api gamya tvam siddhyati iti dvayoḥ upayāsaḥ uktam artham upasaṃharan= āha tasmāt iti arthaḥ liṅga lakṣaṇaḥ artham liṅgi lakṣaṇam tat tasmāt iha anumāna anumeya cintāyām svabhāva pratibandha cintāyām vā 
DhPr_112.1	 nanu bhinnayoḥ gamya gamaka bhāve liṅgam tad utpattyā parāyattatvāt pratibaddham sādhyaḥ tu apara āyatta tvāt pratibandha viṣayaḥ tad āśrayaḥ ca sādhya sādhana bhāva niyamaḥ syāt svabhāvayoḥ tu tad bhāve hetoḥ tādātmya pratibaddha tvam tādātmyam ca ubhayoḥ aviśiṣṭam tatas prativaddha tvam pratibandha viṣaya tvam vā dvayoḥ aviśiṣṭam āyāti tad āśrayaḥ ca niyataḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ prasaktaḥ iti āha tatra ayam arthaḥ iti na kevalam artha antara tvaḥ iti apiśabdaḥ yat pratibaddham iti yat sādhya pratibaddha tayā tad āyatta tayā niścitam iti draṣṭavyam pratibandha viṣayaḥ api tattvena niścitaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ 
DhPr_112.2	 nanu tādātmya aviśeṣāt ekaḥ tatra pratibandha viṣaya tayā na tu pratibaddha tayā iti ayam eva vibhāgaḥ kutas iti āha yasya iti yat vā tādātmya anubhāvini dvaye kintatra pratibaddham yat gamakam kiñca pratibandha viṣayaḥ yat gamyam iti aja anantam pratyāha yasya iti caḥ hetau dvitīya pakṣe avadhāraṇe yasya dharmasya vyāvṛtti kalpitasya yaḥ niyataḥ pratiniyataḥ saḥ eva svabhāvaḥ na tad anyaḥ api saḥ iti yasya iti ṣaṣṭhī antena uktaḥ parāmṛṣṭaḥ tat iti yaḥ iti prathama antena uktaḥ pratyavamṛṣṭaḥ tasmin pratibaddhaḥ iti vigrahaḥ niścīyate iti śeṣaḥ prakaraṇa labhyam vā kaḥ punar īdṛśaḥ iti āha yathā iti prayatnaḥ puruṣa vyāpāraḥ tasya anantaram avyavadhānam tatra bhavaḥ iti diś ādi tvāt yat tatas sva arthe kan tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam tadākhyā nāma yasya sa tathā prayatna anantaryaka tvasya hi anitya tvam eva svabhāvaḥ na tu nitya tvam api tatas anitya tve pratibaddham niścīyate 
DhPr_112.3	 īdṛśasya tāvat iyam gatiḥ anyasya tu kā vārttā iti āha yasya iti dharmasya iti anuvṛtteḥ yasya iti dharmasya turviśiṣṭam dharmam darśayati sa ca saḥ api prayatna ānantari ākhyaḥ anyaḥ ca āsaḥ ca aprayatna anantarīyakaḥ vana kusuma ādiḥ api sa pratibandhasya sādhana gata pratibaddha tvasya viṣayaḥ gocaraḥ etat eva vyatireka mukheṇa draḍhayati na tu iti punar arthe tuśabdaḥ kaḥ asau= īdṛśaḥ iti āha yathā iti anitya tva ākhyaḥ prayatna anantaryatva ākhyena pratibaddhaḥ iti yojyam evañca arthāt pratibandha viṣaye ca iti avatiṣṭhate etat ca anitya tvasya tad asat svabhāva tvena aniyata svabhātvam anitya tva sāmānya abhiprāyeṇa uktam anyathā ghaṭa ādi gata anitya tvasya prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam antareṇa kutas avasthānam yena anya svabhāvatayā asya aniyata tvam syāt iti 
DhPr_113.1–113.2	 syāt etat tādātmyam tāvat tayoḥ asti tat kim pratibaddha tva pratibandha viṣaya tva niścayena gamya gamaka tva vyavasthā nibandhanīkṛtena iti āha niścaya iti hi iti yasmāt tad apekṣāyām api kim iti prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam eva gamakam iti āha prayatnā iti caḥ yasmāt arthe yatas tad svabhāvam niścitam atas asmātta deva anitya tve pratibaddham ucyate iti śeṣaḥ yatas tāt ātmya aviśeṣe api yat pratibaddha tayā niścitam tat eva gamakam itarat gamyam tasmāt niyataḥ pratiniyataḥ prayatna āntarīyakam eva gamakam anitya tva ca gamyam eva iti evaṃrūpaḥ viṣayaḥ yasya gamya gamaka bhāvasya sa tathā etat eva vyatireka mukheṇa draḍhayati na anyathā iti nanu ca yaḥ ekasya anyatra pratibandhaḥ tad āyatta tvam sa tau= at na ahetukaḥ kaḥ ca asau hetuḥ iti abhipretya praśnayati kasmāt iti nimitta praśnaḥ ca eṣaḥ tādātmyāt iti maulam uttara vyākhyātum āha yatas iti tatra sādhye svabhāvena pratibandhaḥ pratibaddha tvam liṅgasya iti śeṣaḥ 
DhPr_113.3	 pratijñā sādhya nirdeśaḥ tasyāḥ arthaḥ dharma dharmi samudāyaḥ atra ca sādhya sādhanayoḥ aikātmyasya prastuta tvāt sādhya lakṣaṇasya pratijñā arthasya hetu tvam āsaktam tatas ca sādhya dharma vat sādhana dharmasya api asiddhiḥ siddhau vā hetu vaiyarthyam iti bhāvaḥ yadi paramārthataḥ abhedaḥ katham tarhi bheda nibandhanaḥ gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ iti āha vikalpa iti tuḥ pāramārthikāt abhedāt vaidharmyam āha kaḥ asau vikalpa viṣayaḥ yadi bāhyaḥ tadā tad avasthaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha yat iti tam apekṣate iti tad apekṣaḥ idam sādhanam idam sādhyam iti sādhya sādhana rūpaḥ bhedaḥ nānātvam iti arthaḥ yadi nāma kalpanā nirmitaḥ bhedaḥ tathā api katham gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ iti āha niścaya iti hiḥ yasmāt niścaya apekṣaḥ iti niścaya viṣayīkṛta rūpa apekṣaḥ iti arthaḥ yatas evam tatas tasmāt tayoḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ bhedaḥ nānātvam yuktyā saṅgataḥ yuktaḥ vastunaḥ akṛtrimāt rūpāt āgataḥ vāstavaḥ 
DhPr_114.1	 syāt matam bhedena kalpitayoḥ na tādātmyam gamya gamaka bhāva nibandhanam asti vāstavena ca rūpeṇa eka tvāt na gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ iti katham svabhāva hetoḥ gamaka tvam na ahetu tvam yad darśana dvāra āyātau= etau dharmau tathā apratīyamānau tat tāvat paramārthataḥ tad ātmakam iti ekasya dharma antara avi abhicāraḥ vāstavam tādātmya gatam ca yasya gamaka tvam sa svabhāva hetuḥ ucyate iti kaḥ virodhaḥ 
DhPr_114.2	 ayam prakaraṇa arthaḥ na niścaya sthe samāropite rūpe samāropita tvena adhyavasīyamāne gamya gamake kintu sva lakṣaṇa tvena adhyavasīyamāne tatra tādātmyam asti etat uktam bhavati āropyamāṇam rūpam āropita bhedam āropita sadṛśam ca sva lakṣaṇam tena āropitena rūpeṇa anugamyamānam bhinnam aghī avasīyate tad avadhya vasita bheda nibandhanaḥ gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ tasya svatas ca tādātmyam iti 
DhPr_114.3–114.5	 dvitīyam pratibandha kāraṇam vyākhyātum āha na kevalāt iti caḥ sādhāraṇam nimittam samuccinoti nanu ca samavāya āditas api nimittāt pratibandhaḥ na asambhavī tat katham tādātmyāt tad utpatteḥ eva ca saḥ ucyate iti abhiprāyavān pṛcchati kasmāt iti anya nimittasya anabhidhānāt nimitta dvayāt iti āha atad svabhāvasya ityādi bruvataḥ ca ācāryasya ayam āśayaḥ bhavet eva anyatas sambandhāt pratibandhaḥ yadi samavāya ādiḥ anyaḥ sambandhaḥ pramāṇa bādhitaḥ na bhavet na ca asau na bādhyate tad kutas asa avasannasya nimittam bhavet iti 
DhPr_115.1	 samudāya artham vyācaṣṭe yaḥ yat svabhāvaḥ iti apratibaddha svabhāva tvāt iti mūlasya bhāva pratyayam tyaktvā vigraham āha apratibaddhaḥ iti tasya bhāvaḥ tattvam tasmāt iti tu yojyam amum eva artham yadi ityādinā sphuṭayati kasmāt punar anyatas nimittān na bhavati iti āha pratibaddhā iti hiḥ yasmāt pratibaddha svabhāva tvam eva anyasya anyatra bhaviṣyati iti āha na ca iti caḥ avadhāraṇe hetau vā anyasya sambandhasya abhāvāt tādātmya tad utpatti abhāve ca iti prakaraṇa labhyam kṛtvā na ca anyaḥ kaścid āyatta svabhāvaḥ iti uktam 
DhPr_115.2	 nanu ca asati api tādātmye tad utpattau ca anyatra asvabhāve anutpādake ca anyat pratibaddham yathā ātapaḥ vṛkṣa= chāyāyām tulāyāḥ arvāc bhāga namana avanamane para bhāga unnamana avanam anayoḥ arvāc bhāgaḥ para bhāge rasaḥ rūpe pāṇiḥ pādayoḥ apatat jalam ādhāre balākā salile nadī pūraḥ uparivṛttāyām vṛṣṭau candra udayaḥ samudra vṛddhau kumuda vikāse ca kṛttikā udayaḥ rohiṇī udaye pipilikā utsaraṇam matsya vikāraḥ ca vṛṣṭau śaradi jala prasādaḥ agastya udaye viśiṣṭaḥ megha udayaḥ varṣa karmaṇi adya āditya udayaḥ astamaye śvastana udaye ca kuṣmāṇḍa guḍakaḥ antar sthita bīje parivrājakaḥ daṇḍe santrastaḥ nakulaḥ sarpe kiyat vā śakyate nidarśayitum etāvat tu ucyate yat yena avinābhūtam dṛśyate tat tatra pratibaddham tasya ca liṅgam atas eva trīṇi eva liṅgāni iti saṃkhyā niyamaḥ api ayuktaḥ kevalam liṅgasya rūpāṇi eva vaktavyāni yad darśanāt hetu tvam avasīyate iti 
DhPr_115.3^1	 na eṣa doṣaḥ amīṣām madhye yeṣām pratibandhaḥ asti teṣām tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ anyatara sambhavāt yeṣu ca tad abhāvaḥ teṣām apratibandhāt agamaka tvāt tathā hi vṛkṣasya chāyāyām eka sāmagrī adhīna tayā eva pratibandhaḥ tatas tad pratipattiḥ kārya liṅga jā eva chāyā hi pratibhāsamāna rūpa saṃsthānavatī śaitya ādi artha kriyā kāriṇī vastu eva na tu eva āloka abhāvaḥ sā ca pūrvasmāt āloka upādānāt pūrva vṛkṣa kṣaṇāt vṛkṣa kṣaṇena sārdham utpadyate tathā arvāc bhāga namana avanamane api tulāyāḥ para bhāga unnamana avanamanābhyām eva samam puruṣa prayatnāt eva tathāvidhāt tad upādāna sahakāriṇaḥ utpadyete tathā arvāc bhāga para bhāgayorasa rūpayoḥ api eka sāmagrī adhīna tā eva pāṇiḥ tu apratibaddhaḥ eva vyaṅgasya api sambhavāt 
DhPr_115.3^2	 avyabhicāre ca eka saṃsarga adhīna tā eva nibandhanam tādṛśam ca jalam ādhārasya kāryam eva tādṛśī ca balākā salilasya nadī pūraḥ api tathāvidhaḥ uparivṛṣṭeḥ dṛśya adṛśya samudāyaḥ ca yathāyogam sarvatra dharmī karttavyaḥ nadī pūre ca anyaḥ api prakāraḥ vaktum śakyaḥ nadī dharmiṇī uparivṛṣṭimat deśa sabandhi tvam asyāḥ sādhyam tathāvidha pūra tva mātram hetuḥ evam candra udaya samudra vṛddhi kumuda vikāsānām api ekasām agrī adhīnatā eva ekasmāt eva mahābhūta viśeṣāt kāla vyavahāra viṣayāt etat utpāda apekṣiṇaḥ teṣām utpādāt tathā yaḥ eva kṛttikā udaya hetuḥ mahābhūta viśeṣaḥ kāla saṃjñitaḥ saḥ eva katipaya kāla vyavadhānena rohiṇī udaya hetuḥ iti tad darśanāt hetoḥ tad janana yogya tā dharmaḥ anumīyate eva 
DhPr_115.3^3	 tathā pipīlikā utsaraṇasya matsya vikārasya ca yaḥ hetuḥ saḥ eva katipaya kāla vyavadhānena varṣa karaṇa yogyaḥ tatas pūrvavat hetu dharma anumānam rūpa rasayoḥ iva eka sāmagrī adhīna tayā eva vā tad sama kālika varṣaṇa anumānam tadā tu aśravaṇīya bahis sthita śabda garbha gṛha ādi vyavasthitaḥ anumātā pratyetavyaḥ tathā śarad ādi jala prasādaḥ agastya udayasya kāryam eva atha jala prasādam dṛṣṭvā udeṣyati iti anumīyate tadā tasmāt eva mahābhūtāt kāla saṃjñitāt jala prasādaḥ sa ca katipaya kāla vyavadhānena tad udaya nimittam iti pūrvavat hetu dharma anumānam meghasya api tathāvidhasya atyanta ayogya tā vyāvṛttyā vṛṣṭi karaṇa yogya tā anumeyāḥ na tu bhāvi varṣam vyabhicāra sambhavāt 
DhPr_115.3^4	 sā ca svabhāva bhūtā eva anumīyate iti tādātmyam eva nibandhanam āditya udayasya tu prabhāva atiśayavatā yogi ādinā vibandha sambhavāt na asti eva avinābhāvaḥ anyathā adya gardabha darśanasya api astamaya śvastana udayayoḥ tathātvam syāt evam tu yuktam ayam udetāḥ astamaya śvastana udaya yogyaḥ iti tathā codayatathāvidha yogya tayoḥ tādātmyam eva nibandhanam kuṣmāṇḍasya api bījena ekasāmagrī adhīna tā eva parivrājaka nakulau daṇḍa sarpayoḥ apratibaddhau= eva anyathā api sambhavāt kiyat vā śakyate pariharttum etāvat ucyate asati tādātmye tad utpattau vā kasyacid kvacid pratibandhe tādrūpyeṇa ca gamaka tve sarvam sarvatra pratibaddham tat gamakam prasajyeta iti 
DhPr_116.1–116.2	 kārya svabhāvayoḥ eva tu gamaka tvam katham iti bruvataḥ pūrva pakṣa vādinaḥ ayam āśayaḥ tādātmya tad upattiḥ eva anyasya bhaviṣyataḥ tatas ca gamaka tvam iti kārya svabhāvayoḥ iti dvayoḥ uccāraṇe ca ayam tasya bhāvaḥ bhavadbhiḥ eva anupalambhaḥ anayoḥ antar bhāvitaḥ iti  nupalabdhiḥ iti ukte kutosya pūrva pakṣasya utthānam satyam etat kevalam tat evā miti asyāḥ api anupalabdheḥ pratiṣedha sambhavāt iti abhiprāyeṇa pūrva pakṣa pravṛtteḥ adoṣaḥ eṣaḥ pratiṣedha śabdena vyavahāraḥ abhipretaḥ iti pratiṣedha vyavahāraḥ iti vivṛtam mūle tu api śabdaḥ sādhya antara samuccaye kā asau yathā uktā iti āha yā iti 
DhPr_117.1–117.2	 mūla sāmarthya sthitam abhivyanavita tasmāt anyatas adṛśya anupalabdheḥ novatā pratiṣedha siddhiḥ iti prakṛtena sambandhaḥ yadi adṛśya anupalabdheḥ na bhavati tadā anupalabdhi tva aviśeṣe vivakṣitāyāḥ api mā bhūt iti abhipretya āha tatas tāvat iti tasmāt asambhavāt kāraṇa ātatas iti tatas eva dṛśya anupalabdheḥ iti vivakṣitam itarathā anyasyāḥ api pratiṣedha siddhi kathana prasaṅgāt 
DhPr_117.3	 nanu tatas api asti anyatas api katham punar tatas eva iti niyamaḥ labhyate iti abhiprāyavān āha atha iti athaśabdaḥ praśne anyathā ca iti uttaram vyācakṣāṇaḥ iha evacchedam darśayati caśabdañca yasmāt arthe dṛśya anupalabdheḥ uktāt prakārāt adṛśya anupalabdheḥ anya prakāra tvam anyathātvam vivakṣitam ācārya sya iti darśayan= āha sati iti etasmāt sati vastuni tad sambhavāt mūle tu anyathā ca anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteṣu iti eka vākya tayā eva arthaḥ saṅgacchate nā ya śabda artha vyākhyā na api uttara pada vyākhyāne pūrva pakṣa vacana prayāsaḥ kaścid tathā tu na prakrāntam dharma uttareṇa iti kim atra kurmaḥ kutas etat iti sāmānyena uktvā viśeṣa niṣṭham karoti satyapi iti etat ca vigrahaḥ iti antam sugamam teṣu anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteṣu abhāva niścaya abhāvāt sati api vastuni tasyāḥ anupalabdheḥ bhāvaḥ iṣṭaḥ anena etat āha na asmākam atra pramāṇam asti yat sati eva vastuni sā bhavati iti kintu tasyām satyām api yasmāt pratyayaḥ dolāyate tasmāt evam ucyate iti 
DhPr_118.1–118.2	 samprati niścaya abhāvasya avadhim paryeṣamāṇaḥ āha kasmāt sakāśāt iti para pratyakṣa nivṛtteḥ aśakya niścaya tve tad nivṛtti artham ātma pratyakṣa grahaṇam nanu yadi ayam apādāna praśnaḥ na tu hetu praśnaḥ tadā katham idam āha tasya nivṛtteḥ kāraṇāt niścaya abhāvaḥ iti ced na anya artha tvāt kāraṇa śabdasya niścaya abhāvasya śābdena nyāyena jāyamānasya eṣā prakṛtiḥ kāraṇam janikarttuḥ prakṛtiḥ iti anena labdha apādāna saṃjñakāt asmāt iti arthasya vivakṣita tvāt anyathā tu asamañjasam syāt yasmāt ityādinā uvatam artham upasaṃharati etat ca pratiṣedha siddhiḥ iti etat antam sugamam samprati anupalabdheḥ anumāna jñāna hetu tvāt prāmāṇyam svabhāva viśeṣaḥ vyāpāraḥ ca uktaḥ api kāla puruṣa viśeṣa parigraheṇa vaktum atha ityādinā praśna pūrvam upakramate athaśabdaḥ ārambhe pūrvavat 
DhPr_119.1	 pratyakṣa paricchedya tvāt pratyakṣaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ nivṛtti śabdena ācāryasya anupalabdhiḥ vivakṣitā iti darśayati tasya nivṛttiḥ anupalabdhiḥ iti anupalabdhi śabdena api vivakṣita karttṛ karma dharma upalabdhi paryudāsena anyat eka jñāna saṃsargi vastu tat jñānam ca vivakṣitam etat eva spaṣṭayati tad abhāva svabhāva iti yāvat iti tasya pratiṣedhyasya ghaṭa ādeḥ abhāvaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ bhāvaḥ tad svabhāvāḥ tad abhāva svabhāva śabdena yāvān arthaḥ ukta tad anupalabdhi śabdena api iti iti yāvat iti asya arthaḥ yatas anya upalabdhiḥ eva tad anupalabdhiḥ sā eva ca tad abhāvaḥ na anyaḥ atas eva asmāt eva kāraṇāt abhāvaḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ na sādhyaḥ kutas na sādhyaḥ iti āha svabhāva anupalabdheḥ liṅgāt kutas na sādhyaḥ iti āha siddha tvāt niścita tvāt ghaṭa abhāvasya iti prakaraṇāt 
DhPr_119.2^1	 evam manyate tad eka jñāna saṃsargi vastu tat jñānam ca ghaṭa ādi anupalabdhiḥ tad abhāvaḥ ca tat ca indriya jena pratyakṣeṇa sva saṃvedanena ca siddham iti na liṅgāt abhāvaḥ sādhyate iti nanu avidyamānaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ katham pratyakṣaḥ atha pratyakṣaḥ katham tad anupalabdhiḥ ucyate iti āha avidyamānaḥ api ca iti na kevalam vidyamānaḥ pratyakṣaḥ ucyate iti apiśabdaḥ samagrā samastā sāmagrī kāraṇa kalāpaḥ yasya iti vigrahaḥ śeṣāt vibhāṣā iti kabh na kapi iti hrasva tva pratiṣedhaḥ jñāyamānaḥ niścīyamānaḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ eka jñāna saṃsargiṇi pra tad upalabdheḥ eva iti avadhāraṇīyam pratyakṣa nivṛttiḥ ghaṭa ādi anupalabdhiḥ 
DhPr_119.2^2	 kasmāt tu dvayam tathā ucyate iti āha tatas hi iti hi iti yasmāt yasmāt amū eva dṛśya ghaṭa ādi tuccha rūpa nivṛtti avaseya hetū tasmāt kāraṇāt arthaḥ eka jñāna saṃsargi vaḥ tu antaram jñānam ca tasya eva etat eva vyatireka mukheṇa draḍhayati na tu iti nivṛtti mātram upalabdhi abhāva mātram tasya tathā tve kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha nivṛtti mātrāt iti dṛśya nivṛtti a niścayāt dṛśya abhāva aniścayāt iha nivṛtti mātrasya prasajya pratiṣedha ātmanaḥ niścetum aśakyatvāt na hetu tvam yujyate iti dharma uttarasya āśayaḥ nivṛtti mātrāt dṛśya nivṛtti a niścayāt iti bruvataḥ pūrva pakṣa vādinā tu evam jñātam nivṛtti mātrāt nirviśeṣaṇāt ayam evam pratiṣedhati 
DhPr_119.2^3	 tat aham sa viśeṣaṇam nivṛtti mātram eva darśayāmi iti pramodamānaḥ āha nanu ca iti dṛśya nivṛttiḥ dṛśya abhāvaḥ dṛśya anupalambha āditi atra anupalambha śabdena upalambha abhāva mātram vivakṣitam itarathā pūrva pakṣa vādinaḥ prakṛtam hīyeta anena sa viśeṣaṇam eva upalambha abhāva mātram prasajya prati ṣedha rūpam liṅgam astu na tu nañaḥ paryudāsa vṛttyā tad eka jñāna saṃsargi vastu tat jñānam ca iti pūrva pakṣa vādī darśayati satyam ityādinā pratividhatte kintu eka jñāna saṃsargiṇi bhū tala ādau dṛśyamāne sati dṛśyaḥ sambhāvitaḥ āropitaḥ sa pratiṣedhya iti prakaraṇāt 
DhPr_119.2^4	 tatas dṛśya tva samāropāt dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ dṛśya jñāna abhāvaḥ tuccha rūpaḥ vyavaharttavya mātram niścitā bhavati niścīyatām upalabdhi abhāvaḥ jñeya abhāvaḥ tāvat na niścitaḥ iti tad niścaya artham nivṛtti mātram vyāpariṣyate iti āha dṛśyā iti dṛśya jñāna abhāva niścaya sāmarthyāt anyathā anupapatteḥ caḥ hetau dṛśyasya jñeyasya abhāvaḥ vyavaharttavya eka rūpaḥ sāmarthyam eva yadi ityādinā darśayati hiḥ yasmāt arthe dṛśya anupalambhaḥ iti dṛśya upalambhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ atas asmāt dṛśya anupalambha niścayāt dṛśyasya jñeyasya abhāvaḥ uktāt sāmarthyāt avasitaḥ dṛśya upalambha abhāva niścayaḥ tu eka jñāna saṃsargi vaḥ tu antara upalagbhena iti draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_120.1–120.2	 nanu yadi jñeya abhāvaḥ api avasitaḥ tarhi katham liṅgena sādhyate iti āha na vyavahṛtaḥ iti adṛṣṭānām api sattva śaṅkayā na pratyakṣam vyavahārayitum śaknoti iti bhāvaḥ kena tarhi vyavahriyate iti āha dṛśyānupalambhena liṅga bhūtena  abhāva vyavahāraḥ eva jñānam ca iti cakāraḥ tulya kakṣatām darśayati dvayoḥ ca nivṛtti niścaya hetu tvam jñānam antareṇa yasmāt ayam kevalaḥ pradeśaḥ tasmāt ghaṭa ādiḥ na astiiti adhyavasātum aśakya tvāt tathā viṣayam antareṇa yasmāt kevala pradeśa aparokṣīkaraṇam tasmāt tat jñānam na asti iti niścetum aśakya tvāt iti draṣṭavyam pratyakṣasya ghaṭa ādeni vṛtti niścaya hetu tvāt pratyakṣa nivṛttia spaṣṭam saṃruktam draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_120.3	 nanu ca pratiṣedhyasya ghaṭa ādeḥ asataḥ api tathā astu pratyakṣa tvam yat punar tatra na āsīt eva tasya katham atīta tvam yat ca tatra na asti eva tasya katham varttamāna tvam katham ca tatra anupalabdheḥ vyāpāraḥ iti āśaṅkām apākurvan= āha yathā iti yena prakāreṇa ghaṭaḥ yadi bhavet dṛśyaḥ eva bhavet iti evam rūpeṇa caḥ hetau tasmin= eka jñāna saṃsargiṇī atīte amūḍha smṛti saṃskāre caḥ vaktavya antara samuccaye varttamāne ca samuccaye cakāraḥ tathā tena prakāreṇa yadi tatra pūrvam ghaṭaḥ sthitaḥ yadi syāt upalabdhaḥ syāt na ca upalabhyate iti evam ātmanā ghaṭasya āropāt pratyakṣasya tadānīm asataḥ tad rūpam atīta tvam varttamāna tvañca āropitam āropa siddham itiḥ evam draṣṭavya ākāram darśayati draṣṭavyam jñātavyam iti yojanīyam idam 
DhPr_121.1–121.2	 nanu dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ kasmin kāle pramāṇam kiṃsvabhāvā kiṃvyāpārā ca iti tritayam pṛṣṭaḥ ācāryaḥ tatra anena kim ākhyātam ācāryeṇa iti āśaṅkām apākurvan= āha anena iti anena pratipattṛ pratyakṣasya nivṛttiḥ iti vacanena caḥ avadhāraṇe svabhāva iti asya anantaram draṣṭavyaḥ pratyakṣasya ghaṭasya prasajya pratiṣedha lakṣaṇa nivṛtti niścaya hetu tvāt pratyakṣa ghaṭa nivṛttiḥ pratyakṣa ghaṭa anupalabdhiḥ nañaḥ paryudāsa vṛttyā tad eka jñāna saṃsargi vastu tat jñānam ca dvayam svabhāvaḥ rūpam yasyāḥ dṛśya anupalabdheḥ sā tathā uvatā vyākhyātā iti śeṣaḥ nanu dṛśya anupalabdhi rūpam liṅgam astu paryudāsa rūpam sādhyaḥ tu prasajya pratiṣedha rūpaḥ kim na bhavati iti āha sā iti caḥ yasmāt sā tathāvidhā anupalabdhi uktam ācāryeṇa sā abhāva vyavahāra pravarttanīti anena śabdena iti bhāvaḥ dharma uttareṇa ca atas eva abhāvaḥ na sādhyaḥ iti anena 
DhPr_121.3	 ghaṭa vivikta pradeśa darśanena ahitaḥ āropitaḥ saṃskāraḥ viśiṣṭa śakti yukta vijñāna ātmikā vāsanā na tu para abhimataḥ bhāvanā ākhyaḥ anurūpa smaraṇam janayitum anīśānaḥ mūḍhaḥ iti vyapadiśyate dṛśya ghaṭa anupalambhe dṛśyasya ghaṭasya upalabdhi abhāve tuccha rūpe atas eva ca dṛśye ghaṭe amūḍha smṛti saṃskāra grahaṇam kasmāt na varttamāna viśeṣaṇam iti āha varttamāne tu iti turatītāt varttamānasya vaidharmyam āha atas moha abhāvāt na ghaṭa abhāve vyavaharttavya eka rūpe na api ghaṭa anupalambhe ghaṭa upalabdhi abhāve tuccha rūpe pratyakṣa vat āropāt varttamānasya arthasya ghaṭa ādeḥ atas eva varttamāna grahaṇasya nirviśeṣaṇa tvāt eva 
DhPr_122.1^1	 nanu yathā vikalpena viṣayī kriyamāṇaḥ atītaḥ anupalambhaḥ pramāṇam ucyate tathā vikalpasya avyāhata prasara tvāt anāgataḥ api anupalambhaḥ vikalpyamānaḥ kim na tathā apramāṇam iti āha tat ayam iti yasmāt kevala pradeśa darśana āhitaḥ saṃskāraḥ atīte ghaṭa ādau= amūḍhaḥ gṛhyate varttamāne tu tasmin smṛti saṃskāre mohaḥ na sambhavati eva tat tasmāt ayam tātparya arthaḥ anupalambha niścaya hetu tvāt anupalambhaḥ kevala pradeśa ādiḥ sphuṭaḥ yathā asau kevalaḥ anubhūtaḥ tathā smṛtvā viṣayī kriyamāṇaḥ pramāṇam varttamānaḥ ca tādṛś anupalambhaḥ sphuṭaḥ abhra antena jñānena gṛhyamāṇaḥ iti draṣṭavyam yatas īdṛśaḥ anupalambhaḥ pramāṇam tatas tasmāt kutas na śakyate jñātum iti āha anāgatāyāḥ iti 
DhPr_122.1^2	 tathā tvena niścitaḥ hi hetuḥ gamakaḥ anyathā sandigdha asiddha tā hetu doṣaḥ syāt iti abhiprāyaḥ pratyakṣa nivṛtti śabdena tāvat dṛśya anupalabdheḥ svabhāvaḥ darśitaḥ amūḍha ityādinā tu kim darśitam iti āha kāla iti itiḥ evam arthe tena evam kāla viśeṣaḥ anupalabdheḥ vyākhyātaḥ iti kāla viśeṣaḥ atītaḥ varttamānaḥ ca vyākhyātaḥ kathitaḥ anena iti śeṣaḥ etat ca atīte varttamāne ca kāle anupalabdheḥ prāmāṇya ākhyānam asya upalakṣaṇam draṣṭavyam kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ api tayoḥ kālayoḥ prāmāṇyāt tathā hi āsīt atra vahniḥ dhūmasya upalabdha tvāt asti vahniḥ iha dhūmasya upalabhyamāna tvāt tathā asīt iha pādapaḥ śiṃśapāyāḥ upalabdha tvāt asti iha vṛkṣaḥ śiṃśapāyāḥ upalabhyamāna tvāt iti api bhavati eva 
DhPr_122.2–122.3	 nanu dṛśya anupalambhe bhavatu jñāna abhidhāna lakṣaṇaḥ vyavahāraḥ kāyikaḥ tu katham iti āha ghaṭa iti hiḥ yasmāt pravarttate iti yogyatayā ucyate pravṛtti yogyaḥ tāvat bhavati iti atas eva ca abhāva yogya tā sādhya ucyate tat etasya iti lokoktiḥ eṣā tat ca etat ca iti vigrahaḥ kāryaḥ yat vā yatas abhāva niścayaḥ anupalabdhi nimittakaḥ tat tasmāt apiḥ atiśaye āstām ekasya dvayoḥ vā pravarttanī trividhasya yāvat pravarttanī iti arthaḥ pravartanīti asya dvayam etat vivaraṇam spaṣṭa artham sādhanī pravarttikā iti pravarttayati iti pravarttanī iti yogyatayā uktam sa abhāva tritayam abhāva vyavahāram pravarttayitum yogyā tāvat mātra nimittaka tvāt tasya satyarthi tve puruṣaḥ tān vyavahārān ācaratu mā vā atas eva abhāva vyavahāra yogya tā pradeśa ādeḥ sādhyate dṛśya anupalambhena iti parama arthaḥ 
DhPr_123.1	 nanu yadi na asti iti evam ākāram jñānam anupalabdheḥ liṅgāt bhavati katham tarhi pratyakṣau= asitaḥ abhāvaḥ uktaḥ iti āha yadi api ca iti nipāta samudāyaḥ yadi api śabda vat viśeṣa abhidhāna nimitta abhyupagame varttate abhāva niścaya śabda sāmānādhikaraṇyādayam eva iti nirdeśaḥ caśabdaḥ vaktavyam etat iti asya arthe atra varttate abhāva niścayasya tadā sthairya lābhāt anupalambhāt eva iti uktam draṣṭavyam tathā api iti laukika uktiḥ iyam nigada abhidhāna ārambhe tasmāt śabdena yasmāt śabdaḥ ākṣiptaḥ tena ayam arthaḥ yasmāt kevala pradeśa grahaṇa lakṣaṇa vyāpāra anusārī ghaṭaḥ na asti iti abhāva niścayaḥ tasmāt pratyakṣa kṛtaḥ ucyate iti śeṣaḥ kasya vyāpāra anusārī iti ākāṅkṣāya am uktam pratyakṣasya pramāṇa viśeṣasya iti 
DhPr_123.2	 atha syāt yadi ayam pratyakṣa kṛtaḥ tadā pratyakṣa pravarttitaḥ api tat kim dṛśya anupalambhena kriyate iti āśaṅkya āha kiñca iti vaktavya antara samuccaye tad vivikta pradeśa ādi grāhiṇā pratyakṣeṇa eva abhāvaḥ niṣedhya abhāvaḥ prasajya pratiṣedha ātmā niścitaḥ katham dṛśyasya anupalambhaḥ upalambha abhāvaḥ tuccha rūpaḥ tad niścaya karaṇa sāmarthyāt anyathā anupapatteḥ pūrva uktayā nītyā yuktyā yadi hi dṛśyaḥ tatra bhavet dṛśya anupalambhaḥ na bhavet iti evam ātmikayā yadi pratyakṣam ittham pratiṣedhya abhāvam niścāyayati vyavahārayitum api śaknoti eva iti āha kevalam kintu na śaknoti vyavaharttum iti antarbhū taṇijartha tvāt nirdeśasya vyavahārayitum iti arthaḥ kutas na śaknoti iti āha sattva śaṅkayā iti pratiṣedhya sattvasya svarūpasya sattva śaṅkayā sandehena hetunā 
DhPr_123.3	 nanu adarśane api katham sandehaḥ iti āha adṛṣṭā iti tena pratyakṣeṇa adṛṣṭānām api piśāca ādīnām satvasya sadbhāvasya sambhavāt sambhāvyamāna tvāt nityam śaṅkyamāna anupalambha vyabhicāraḥ hi abhāvaḥ iti bhāvaḥ atas pratyakṣasya tatra aśakta tvāt sā api katham vyavahārayati iti āha dṛśyaḥ iti atas asmāt kāraṇāt kṛtam pratyakṣeṇa iti prakaraṇāt etat eva vyatireka mukheṇa draḍayati na tu iti yasmāt pratyakṣa vyāpāra anusāryabhāva niścayaḥ itiḥ tasmāt abhāva niścayaḥ anupalambhāt pravṛttaḥ api dṛḍhībhūtaḥ api pratyakṣeṇa kevala pradeśa ādi vedinā sāmarthyāt kṛtaḥ utpāditaḥ a nupalambhena dṛśya anupalambhena pravarttitaḥ sādhitaḥ uktaḥ ācāryeṇa abhāva vyavahāra pravarttanīti anena śabdena iti buddhi stham iti ityādinā upasaṃhāraḥ itiḥ evam uktena krameṇa anupalabdhiḥ dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ tasyāḥ eva prakṛta tvāt 
DhPr_124.1–124.3	 kasmāt ityādi varttamānāyāḥ iti antam sugamam anāgatāyāḥ api anupalabdheḥ abhāva niścayaḥ kasmāt na bhavati iti āha anāgata iti hiḥ yasmāt arthe tasyāḥ iti pañcamī antam idam ayam eva ca sāmarthya avasitaḥ maula ūrthaḥ anāgatā hi ityādinā dharma uttareṇaa spaṣṭam sam kāṅkṣa upaśama artham purastāt uktaḥ syāt etat pratiṣedha siddhiḥ ityādinā niścaya abhāvāt iti antena granthena asya arthasya gata tvāt tasyāḥ eva abhāva niścayāt iti ayam ācāryīyaḥ granthaḥ punar uktaḥ iti na punaruktaḥ yatas yathā atīte api kāle ghaṭa ādeḥ tad kāla vartti dṛśya anupalabdheḥ atītāyāḥ smṛti ārūḍhāyāḥ abhāva niścayaḥ tavā a na āgate api kāle ghaṭa ādeḥ abhāva niścayaḥ kim na bhavati iti kena apākṛtam yena ayam punaruktaḥ syāt iti 
DhPr_124.4	 samprati anupalabdheḥ prakārasya svarūpasya bhedam nānātvam prakāra bhedaḥ draṣṭavyam caḥ vaktavya antara samuccaye sā iti mūla anuvādaḥ eṣā iti tasya vyākhyānam ekādaśa grahaṇam ca ācāryasya upalakṣaṇa artham yathā pramāṇa vārttike grahaṇam ṣoḍaśa prakāra iti tu draṣṭavyam etat ca kāraṇa viruddha kārya upalabdhi vyākhyāna anantaram darśayiṣyāmaḥ vivakṣitā anya upalambha eka rūpa tvāt dṛśya anupalabdheḥ katham ayam bhedaḥ upapadyeta iti abhipretya pṛcchati kutas iti prayoga bhedāt iti ācāryīyam uttaram anūdya prayoga śabdam vyācaṣṭe prayogaḥ iti prayukti artham āha śabda iti śabda śabdena prakaraṇāt vācakaḥ śabdaḥ gṛhyate abhidhā artha prakāśanam tatra vyāpāraḥ vyāpṛtiḥ pravṛttiḥ yadvā abhidhā artha prakāśanam tad lakṣaṇaḥ vyāpāraḥ tasya prayogasya bhedāt bhidyamāna tvāt iti tu su bodha tvāt dharma uttareṇa na vyākhyātam 
DhPr_125.1	 nanu śabdasya eva anupalambha vācakasya anupalambhaḥ eva vācyaḥ tat katham prayoga bhedaḥ yena anupalambhasya prakāra bhedaḥ ucyate iti āha śabdaḥ hi iti hiḥ yasmāt sākṣāt avyavadhānena kvacid viruddha upalambha ādau pratiṣedhyāt śīta sparśa ādeḥ artha antaram agni ādi abhidhatte kvacid vyāpaka anupalabdhi ādau vivakṣitāt śiṃśapā ādi pratiṣedhāt pratiṣedha antaram vṛkṣa ādi pratiṣedham abhidhatte yadi artha antara vidhiḥ artha antara pratiṣedhaḥ ca kriyate tarhi dyate iti āha sarvatra iti tuḥ viśeṣa arthaḥ aśabda upāttā sva vācaka pada anupāttā yathā ca aśabda upāttā api sā pratīyate tathā purastāt abhidhāsyate apiḥ avadhāraṇe atiśaye vā itiḥ tasmāt arthe evam arthe atas eva arthīm gatim āśritya uktam na tu śābdīm iti draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_125.2–125.4	 anupalambhasya prakṛta tvāt prakāra bhedān iti mantavyam tasya anupalabdhiḥ pūrva uktayā nītyā tad viviktaḥ pradeśaḥ tat jñānam ca avaseyam evam kārya anupalabdhi ādiṣu dvi rūpa evā anupalabdhi ti nidarśanena nanu kīdṛśī upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ kathañca avidyamānaḥ ayañca iti pūrvasmin= anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa ākhyānaḥ iva ca uyasmāt arthe avadhāraṇa arthe vā pūrvavat iti asya anantaram draṣṭavyaḥ etat ca svabhāva anupalambhasya artha kathanam kṛtam ācāryeṇa na prayogaḥ darśitaḥ asādhana aṅgasya pratijñāyai upādānāt sādhana aṅgasya ca vyāpteḥ apradarśanāt hetoḥ ca anuvādya rūpasya prathama antasya anirdeśāt evam itarāsu sarvāsu eva anupalabdhiṣu boddhavyam prayogaḥ punar īdṛśaḥ yat yatra upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam sanna upalabhyate tat sarvam tatra asat vyavahāra yogyam yathā turaṅgama uttamāṅge śṛṅgam na upalabhyate ca atra upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ dhūmaḥ iti anena sāmānya ādi nirākaraṇe dṛśya anupalambhaḥ prayoktavyaḥ iti darśitam ācāryeṇa tulya nyāyatva āditya vaseyam 
DhPr_126.1	 iha anupalambhaḥ kevala pradeśa ādiḥ abhāva vyavahāra yogya tā ca sādhyāḥ dṛśya anupalambhasya tādātmya lakṣaṇaḥ eva pratibandhaḥ gamya gamaka bhāva nibandhanam iti keṣāñcit matam kecid tu anupalambhā abhāva vyavahāra yogya tayoḥ gamya gamaka bhāve viparyaya tādātmya lakṣaṇaḥ pratibandhaḥ nimittam iti pratipedire atas eva anupalambhaḥ kārya svabhāvābhyām bhedena nirdiṣṭaḥ sva sādhye pratibandha anapekṣaṇāt itarayoḥ ca tad vaiparītyāt iti ca evam ca etat samādadhati iti tathā hi upalabdhi avyabhicārāt tādṛśī anupalabdheḥ eva sattā tatas upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta sattve tad upalambhayoḥ tādātmyāt eva anupalambha asat vyavahārayoḥ gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ yadi tu tad vivikta pradeśa ādi upalambha rūpasya anupalambhasya tat asat vyavahārayā ugtāyāḥ ca yat tāt ātmyam tat nimittamucyeta tadā tasya bhū tala ādeḥ anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptā asat vyavahāra yogya tā api ātma bhūtā eva iti piśāca ādi a bhāva vyavahāram api anupalambhaḥ sādhayet tad pratibandhāt iti 
DhPr_126.2	 nanu kārya abhāvāt kāraṇa abhāvaḥ sādhyatām kim apratibaddha sāmarthyasya iti sādhya dharma viśeṣaṇena iti āha kāraṇāni iti caḥ yasmāt itiḥ tasmāt sādhyaḥ sādhayitum yujyate iti arthaḥ etat eva vyatireka mukheṇa draḍhayati na tu iti turvaidharmya arthaḥ eva kāra arthaḥ vā na anyeṣām kāraṇa kāraṇa tayā upacarita kurvat rūpāṇām 
DhPr_126.3	 atha paripūrṇayā api sāmagryā vidhāraka sambhavāt pratibandhaḥ sambhāvyate tat asambhavi idam viśeṣaṇam iti āha apratibaddhā iti caśabdaḥ tuśabdasya arthe hetau vā kutas etat iti āha anyeṣām iti antyakṣaṇa prāptāni ca kāraṇāni yoginā api pratibandhum aśakyāni itarathā tādrūpyam eva hīyeta atas tathāvidhāni kāraṇāni kārya avyabhicārīṇi kāryeṇa vyāpyante tatas kāryam nivartamānam kāraṇāni tādṛśāni nivarttayati iti draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_127.1–127.2	 iha yadi api anena antya kṣaṇena idam kāryam kṛtam iti na avagatam tathā api vastunaḥ kācid avasthā kāryam kurvatī pratītā eva yad anantaram kāryam upalabdham sā eva ca avasthā atra api niṣidhyate atas eva ayam kṣaṇika akṣaṇika sādhāraṇa avasthā atiśaya niṣedhaḥ nanu kāryasya tāvat dṛśyasya atra anupalambhaḥ hetuḥ upādātavyaḥ tat kim asya sambhavaḥ asti yat kāryam eva dṛśyam na tu kāraṇam yena kārya anupalabdhiḥ prayujyate iti āśaṅkya viṣayam asyāḥ darśayitum āha kāryā iti 
DhPr_127.3–127.6	 kaḥ asau= evaṃvidhaḥ viṣayaḥ iti āha tatra iti vākya upakṣepe yadi punar gṛha aṅgaṇam paśyet dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ eva prayuktā syāt iti abhiprātheṇa āha gṛha aṅgaṇam apaśyan= api iti apiḥ avadhāraṇe aṅgaṇa bhitteḥ paryantam avasānam bhitti paryantena samam tulyam sautrāntikānām ālokatamaḥ svabhāvaḥ evākaḥ śaḥ iti tad matyā āloka saṃjñākam iti uktam atra ākāśe kim pratyetavyam iti āha yat deśa iti yadā yad deśe ca iti pāṭhaḥ tadā yaḥ deśaḥ asya iti vigrahaḥ yadā tu yad deśa sthena iti tadā yaḥ ca asau deśaḥ ca tatra tiṣṭhati iti tad deśa sthaḥ iti sa deśaḥ asya iti vigrahaḥ 
DhPr_127.7	 etāvatā api na jñāyate kaḥ tena pratipattrā dharmī kṛtaḥ iti āha tat gṛha iti sa ca asau gṛha aṅgaṇa deśaḥ ca iti samāsaḥ aṅgaṇasya prakṛta tvāt bhittiḥ tasya eva tayā parikṣiptam paricchinnam dharmiṇam karoti iti sambandhaḥ kim etāvat eva iti āha bhitti iti bhittiḥ aṅgaṇasya eva bhitteḥ ca prāntaḥ vācyaḥ tasyāḥ paryantaḥ avasānam niṣṭhā tena parikṣiptam paricchinnam tena caḥ tulya bala tva samuccaya arthaḥ 
DhPr_127.8	 tasmāt ityādinā upasaṃhāra vyājena loka adhyavasāya siddham dharmiṇam darśayati dṛśya adṛśya samudāyaḥ lokena eka tvena ākalitaḥ tāvān deśaḥ dṛśyamānaḥ kimātmakaḥ deśa avayavaḥ bhāgaḥ yasya sa tathā katham evaṃvidhaḥ dharmī iti āha vahani abhāva iti vahniḥ iti viśiṣṭaḥ dhūma janane avyavadheya śaktiḥ tasya api upalakṣaṇa tvāt anyasya dhūma janane apratibaddhasya abhāva pratītiḥ grahītavyā 
DhPr_128.1–128.2	 ayam arthaḥ lokaḥ tāvat tathāvidha deśe dhūmam anupalabhamānaḥ tāvati deśe tathābhūta vahni abhāvam pratyeti na ca etat evaṃvidham dharmiṇam antareṇa ghaṭataḥ iti sāmarthyam anyathā anupapattiḥ tasmāt āyātaḥ upasthitaḥ atas eva ācāryeṇa api iṣṭam viruddha kārye api deśa kāla ādi apekṣaṇam iti bruvatā evam dharmi iṣṭaḥ eva iti bhāvaḥ nanu apratyakṣasya api dharmi tve katham iha iti idamaḥ ha pratyaya antasya nirdeśaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha iha iti tuśabdaḥ yasmāt arthe itiḥ iha śabdasya nirdiṣṭasya ākāram pratyavamṛśati pratyakṣa vastu pratipādakaḥ nirdeśaḥ tathā uktaḥ 
DhPr_128.3	 nanu yadi dṛśya adṛśya samudāyaḥ dharmīm ghaṭate tadā kārya svabhāva hetvoḥ api kim ayam na sambhavati iti āha na kevalam iti iha eva kārya anupalambhaḥ eva api tu kintu anyatra api kārya viśeṣe svabhāva viśeṣe ca tatra tatra kārya hetoḥ dhūma vākyāt agni pauruṣeya tva ādi siddhau tathāvidhaḥ dharmī su vyaktaḥ iti na tatra darśitaḥ tulya nyāya tayā vā draṣṭavyaḥ 
DhPr_128.4	 katham hetau= api evaṃvidhasya dharmiṇaḥ sambhavaḥ itthā āha śabdasya iti kaścid eva śrūyamāṇaḥ pratyakṣaḥ anyaḥ tu aśrūyamāṇaḥ parokṣaḥ anena avaśyam dṛśya adṛśya śabda samudāyaḥ atra dharmī iti darśitam dṛśya adṛśya ātmanā ca śabdena dharmiṇā bhāvyam iti pratipādya jana saṃśaya āropābhyām āyātam na hi pratipādyaḥ śabdasya anitya tve saṃśayānaḥ viparyasyati arthāt ghaṭa śabdaḥ eva śrūyamāṇaḥ eva ca sandegdhi viparyasyati vā kintu iha ghaṭa paṭa ādi śabde śrūyamāṇe śrute śroṣyamāṇe ca tatas tad anurodhāt pratyakṣa apratyakṣa śabda samudāyaḥ anitya tve sādhye dharmīm prasahya patitaḥ tadvat iha api kārya anupalambhe 
DhPr_128.5–128.6	 amum eva nyāyam anyatra api atidiśan= āha yathā ca iti caḥ avadhāraṇe sādhya pratipatti adhikaraṇa bhūtaḥ iti viśeṣaṇa vyājena dharmiṇaḥ lakṣaṇam uktam kārya anupalabdhi prayogaḥ tu evam karttavyaḥ yatra yasya kāryam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam na upalabhyate tat tu tad janana apratibaddha sāmarthyam na asti yathā kvacid dṛśyamāne aṅkure tathāvidham bījam na upalabhyate ca atra upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ dhūmaḥ iti 
DhPr_128.7	 anena ca kārya anupalambha pradarśanena yat jalpitam jalpa mahā udadhinā niḥśabde deśe śabda mātra abhāve sādhye kaḥ tad eka jñāna saṃsargi vaḥ tu antara upalambhaḥ yena śabda abhāva vyavahāraḥ bauddhānām bhavet iti tat pratyuktam draṣṭavyam tathā hi na iha apratibaddha sāmarthyāni śrotra jñāna kāraṇāni santi śrotra jñāna abhāvāt iti kārya anupalabdhiḥ sphuṭā eva śrotra jñāna anupalambhaḥ ca tad anya jñāna upalambha rūpaḥ saṃviditaḥ asti eva eka jñāna saṃsargi tvam ca anyonya avyabhicarita upalambha tvam iti uktam purastāt prayogaḥ tu anantara vat vijñātavyaḥ iti 
DhPr_129.1–129.2	 vyāpaka an upalabdhim vyākhyātum āha pratiṣedhyasya iti tādātmya aviśeṣe api yathā kaścid eva dharmaḥ vyāpyaḥ itaraḥ vyāpakaḥ ca tathā prāk eva dharma uttareṇa nirṇītam dharmaḥ iti ca dharmī apekṣayā vṛkṣa tva ādi na śiṃśapā iti na śiṃśapā tvam iti arthaḥ vṛkṣasya iti ca dharmiṇā dharmasya vṛkṣa tvasya nirdeśaḥ nanu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya tāvat vṛkṣa tvasya anupalabdhiḥ prayoktavyā tathā ca śiṃśapā tvam api dṛśyam eva niṣedhyam iti dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ eva prayoga arhā iti āha iyam api iti na kevalam pūrvikā viśiṣṭe viṣaye kintu iyam api iti api śabdaḥ śiṃśapātu asya adṛśyasya iti yadi syāt dṛśyam eva syāt iti sambhāvanām ativṛttasya iti arthaḥ evam uttaratra api adṛśya tvam īdṛśam eva draṣṭavyam tasya abhāve sādhyaḥ iti adhyāhāraḥ 
DhPr_130.1	 kaḥ asau= evaṃvidhaḥ viṣayaḥ iti āha tatra iti vākya upanyāse upaśliṣṭau pratyāsannau samunnatau= uccau tarūṇām gahanam gahvaram tena upetaḥ yuktaḥ dvitīyaḥ ekayā śilayā ghaṭitaḥ nirmite eka śilā rūpastūpaḥ iti yāvat tattvena eva ca nirvṛkṣa kakṣakaḥ kakṣaḥ tṛṇam nirgatau vṛkṣa kakṣau yatas iti vigrahaḥ bhavatu evam tathā api katham asyāḥ prayogaḥ iti āha draṣṭā api iti apiḥ avadhāraṇe na vivecayati iti asya anantaram draṣṭavyaḥ tasya tādṛśasya draṣṭuḥ 
DhPr_130.2	 bhavatu draṣṭuḥ tāvat dūra deśa sthāyitayā śiṃśapāyāḥ avivekaḥ tathā api yena eva vṛkṣa abhāvam pratipadyate tena eva śiṃśapā abhāvam api kim na pratipadyate iti āha sa hi iti hiḥ yasmāt katham dṛśya anupalambhāt avasyati iti āha dṛśya tvāt vṛkṣa tvasya iti prakaraṇāt kutas tarhi śiṃśapātvā abhāvam avaitītya āha śiṃśapa iti tuśabdaḥ vaidharmye itiḥ tasmāt arthe abhāva śabdena abhāvaḥ abhāva vyavahāraḥ ca uktaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ evam uttaratra api pratyeyam 
DhPr_130.3–130.5	 prayogaḥ punar īdṛśaḥ kāryaḥ yatra yasya vyāpakam na asti na tat tatra asti yathā asati prameya tve prāmāṇyam na asti ca vṛkṣa tvam śiṃśapātu asya vyāpakam iti anena vyāpaka anupalambhasya vyāpya abhāve gamakatva pratipādanena nityānām artha kriyā kāritva abhāvaḥ krama yaugapadyayaḥ vyapikayoḥ abhāvāt ityādi darśitam draṣṭavyam pratiṣedhya ityādinā svabhāva viruddha upalabdhim vyācaṣṭe mūle tu udāhriyate iti adhyāhāraḥ iti darśayan= āha udāhriyate iti sukha pratipatti artham maula dharmya ādi pravibhāgam darśayan= āha atra iti 
DhPr_130.6–130.7	 etena īśvare api ekopādāna ādi vikalpe sampradāna ādi vikalpa abhāvaḥ viruddha upalabdhi prasaṅgena darśitaḥ vikalpasya vikalpa antareṇa saha asthiti lakṣaṇasya virodhasya sva santāne siddha tvāt tatas ca tasya anirūpya karttṛ tvam āyātam anyathā yugapad dṛṣṭa utpādānām anutpattiḥ prasajyeta anirūpya karttṛ tve cā aadhipatya mātreṇa karttṛ tvam syāt tathā ca karmaṇā siddha sādhana tvam īśvara sādhanānām kāryatva ādīnām ityādi darśitam viruddha kārya upalabdhim vyācakṣāṇaḥ āha pratiṣedhyena iti mūlagamikā vivakṣita abhāva pratipādaka iti vivakṣitam iti darśayitum āha gamikā iti pūrvavat dharmya ādi kathanam 
DhPr_131.1–131.3	 kasmin= iyam prayoktavyā iti āha yatra iti dvayoḥ viruddha śīta sparśayoḥ apiḥ avadhāraṇe tuḥ pūrvasmāt vaidharmye kaḥ punar īdṛśaḥ viṣayaḥ iti āha tatra iti nanu ca pradīpa śikhā prabhave dhūme api na śīta sparśa abhāvaḥ tat katham iyam gamikā iti āha samastā iti apavaraka grahaṇam śīta sthāna upalakṣaṇa artham apavarakāt niryāntam nirgacchantam anyatra ca gamyamānaḥ dhūmaḥ katham anyatra śīta abhāvam sādhayati iti āha iha iti iha viruddha kārya upalabdhau dṛśyamānaḥ ca asau dvāra deśaḥ ca tena sahitaḥ 
DhPr_131.4–131.5	 upapattim āha sādhyeti sādhyasya śīta sparśa abhāvasya pratipattiḥ avabodhaḥ tasya pratipatteḥ anusaraṇam nirūpaṇam tasmāt pūrvavat iti yathāpūrvam kārya anupalambhe vahni ādi abhāva pratīti sāmarthya āyātas tādṛśaḥ dharmī tadvat ayam asya bhāvaḥ śīta sparśa abhāva pratītiḥ eva iyam vimṛśyamāṇā avaśyam evaṃvidha dharmiṇam ākarṣati iti 
DhPr_131.6	 prayogaḥ punar asyāḥ evam karttavyaḥ yatra dhūma viśeṣaḥ tatra śīta sparśa abhāvaḥ yathā mahānasa ādau tathāvidhaḥ ca atra dhūmaḥ iti etat ca atyanta abhyāsāt jhaṭiti dhūma darśanāt śīta sparśa abhāva pratīti udaye viruddha kārya upalambha jam ekam anumānam ācāryeṇa uktam iti draṣṭavyam anabhyāsa daśayā punar ajñāte anumāne kārya liṅga ja viruddha upalambha je bhavataḥ tathā hi yatra dhūmaḥ tatra sarvatra vahniḥ yathā ayaskāra kuṭyām dhūmaḥ ca atra iti kārya liṅga jam ekam atra niyata prāc bhāvi tadanu yatra vahniḥ na tatra śīta sparśaḥ yathā rasavatī pradeśe vahniḥ ca atra iti viruddha upalambha jam dvitīyam iti 
DhPr_132.1–132.3	 pratiṣedhyasya ityādinā viruddha vyāpta upalabdhim vyācaṣṭe pūrvavat sādhya ādi pradarśanam kim uta iti nipāta samudāyaḥ kimpunar iti asya arthe varttate nanu kim ajātasya api vastunaḥ nāśam avaśyam bhāvinam kecid icchanti yena api śabdaḥ samuccaye vyākhyāyate iti na eṣa doṣaḥ ajātasya tāvat aniṣṭa tvāt eva na avaśyambhāvī vināśaḥ jātasya api na avaśyam bhāvī iti ittham mūle api śabdaḥ kevalam kim uta ajātasya iti vyācakṣāṇena dharma uttareṇa ayam arthaḥ na vyaktīkṛtaḥ tatra api kimpunar ajātasya yasya vināśaḥ eva na iṣṭaḥ iti abhiprāyeṇa yojanīyaḥ yat vā prāgabhāvasya anādeḥ ajātasya api nāśam avaśyambhāvinam kecid icchanti iti tad apekṣayā api śabdaḥ samuccaye tad mudgara ādi apekṣate vinaśvaraḥ vinaṃṣṭum iti śeṣaḥ tasya hetu antarasya 
DhPr_133.1	 prayogaḥ punar īdṛśaḥ karttavyaḥ yat yat avasthā prāptau hetu antaram apekṣate na tat avaśyam tad rūpam bhavati yathā vastram rakta rūpa tā āpattau rāga dravya saṃyoga apekṣam na avaśyam raktam bhavati apekṣate ca bhāvaḥ vinaṃṣṭum hetu antaram iti viruddha vyāpta upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ eṣaḥ atas eva mūle api śabdaḥ prasaṅga sādhana tva prasaṅga arthaḥ lakṣyate svatantra sādhanam tu viruddha vyāpta upalambha ākhyam evam draṣṭavyam yaḥ viruddha dharma saṃsargavān na asau= ekaḥ yathā drava kaṭhine viruddha dharma saṃsargavān= ca sāmānyādiḥ iti 
DhPr_133.2–133.3	 nanu ca kaḥ arthayoḥ virodhaḥ kiñca asya virodhasya sādhakam pramāṇam iti āśaṅkām apākarttum āha iha iti nitya tva śabdena avaśyambhāvi tvam anitya tva śabdenā anavaśyabhbhāvi tvam uktam draṣṭavyam anyathā kena nityaḥ vināśaḥ abhyupetaḥ yena asyāḥ anitya tā aapādyeta yat ca pūrvam dhruva bhāvi tva śabdam vivṛṇvatā anena dhruvam avaśyam bhavati iti vivṛtam tat ca vyāhanyeta samprati virodham upapādayati nitya anityayoḥ iti caḥ hetau 
DhPr_133.4	 idānīm paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa virodha vyavasthāpakam dṛśya anupalambham darśayitum āha tathā ca iti katham dṛśyatayā abhyupagatasya niṣedhaḥ iti āha yatas iti evam vakṣyamāṇena prakāreṇa tam eva āha yadi ayam iti na ca na evam nitya rūpaḥ avaśyambhāvi svarūpaḥ dṛśyate pratīyate yadi api evam tathā api dṛśya ātmaka abhyupagamaḥ iti āha evam iti caḥ yasmāt evam anantara uktena krameṇa dṛśyamānasya adṛśyena avastunā a nyonya parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa virodha vyavasthāyām tāvat evam dṛśya anupalambhaḥ upāyaḥ vastunā api adṛśyena tathā tva vyavasthāya āmayam eva upāyaḥ iti darśayitum vastunaḥ api ityādinā upakramate na kevalam kalpitasya avastunaḥ iti apiśabdaḥ itiḥ hetau= evam arthe vā dṛśyasya iti vastu apekṣayā 
DhPr_134.1–134.3	 vā śabda arthaḥ cakāraḥ iti kecid anye tu avastunaḥ adṛśya tvasya siddha tvāt kim tad anuvādena kāryam tatas dvayam api etat vastu apekṣayā yojyam vastunaḥ dṛśyasya ghaṭa ādeḥ adṛśyasya piśāca ādeḥ anyathā piśāca ādi vastunaḥ tathā tvam na uktam syāt prakṛtam ca tat eva iti pratipannāḥ bhavatu evam tatas kim siddham iti āha tathā ca sati iti tadvat ghaṭa vat anyatra anyasmin dṛśyamāne vastuni 
DhPr_134.4	 nanu bhavatu dṛśya anupalambhāt dṛśyamāna iṅgulī ādau sarvasya sumeru ādeḥ tādātmya niṣedhaḥ tathā api uktāsu anupalabdhiṣu kutra ayam antarthavatī iti āśaṅkām apākarttum upasaṃhāra vyājena atideśam api āha evam iti evaṃjātīyakasya evamprakāravataḥ evamprakārasya iti ukte vacana labhyam syāt tatra antarbhāvaḥ darśitaḥ eva iti bhāvaḥ 
DhPr_134.5–134.6	 atha yadi dṛśya anupalambhāt anyatra anyasya dṛśyasya adṛsyaśya vā tādātmya niṣedhaḥ katham viruddha vyāpta upalabdheḥ avatāraḥ iti ced na doṣaḥ virodha pratipatti kāle dṛśya anupalambhasya vyāpārāt tad avagata virodhena tu vyāptam yatra dṛśyate viruddha vyāpta upalambhāt eva vivakṣita abhāva pratītiḥ iti kim avadyam pratiṣedhyasya ityādinā kārya viruddha upalabdhim vivṛṇoti pūrvavat dharmyādi pradarśanam vahneḥ iti śīta nivarttana kṣamāt viśiṣṭāt iti draṣṭavyam anyathā pradīpa ādi ātmanaḥ śīta anivarttaka tvena anaikāntika tā āpatteḥ 
DhPr_135.1–135.2	 kīdṛśi viṣaye asyāḥ prayogaḥ iti āha yatra iti na kevalam pūrvaḥ iti apiśabdaḥ abhāvaḥ abhāva vyavahāraḥ ca abhāva śabdena uktaḥ syāt matam katham punar śīta sparśa śīta kāraṇe adṛśye vahniḥ tu dṛśyaḥ sambhavati yena asyāḥ prayogaḥ ghaṭataḥ iti āha yasmin= iti uddeśe pradeśe pratipattuḥ dūra stha tvāt iti śīta sparśa śīta kāraṇayoḥ adṛśya tve kāraṇam bhāsvara varṇa tvāt iti vahneḥ dṛśya tve nibandhanam bhāsvaraḥ bhāsana śīlaḥ varṇaḥ yasya tad bhāvaḥ tasmāt na kevalam nikaṭaḥ iti apiśabdaḥ tatra tasmin deśe 
DhPr_135.3–135.4	 prayogaḥ punar evam kāryaḥ yatra viśiṣṭaḥ vahniḥ na tatra śīta upajanana apratibaddha śaktīni śīta kāraṇāni yathā kvacid anubhūte pradeśe tathābhūtaḥ ca atra vahniḥ iti etat ca abhyāsāt jhaṭiti vahni darśanena tathābhūta śīta kāraṇa abhāva pratīti janmani ekam kārya viruddha upalambha jam anumānam uktam ācāryeṇa iti draṣṭavyam anyathā tu viruddha upalambha kāryānupalambha je dve ete anumāne tathā hi yatra vahniḥ na tatra śīta sparśaḥ iti svabhāva viruddha upalambha jam ekam anumānam yatra ca yat kāryam na asti na tatra tad kāraṇam tad janana apratibaddha sāmarthyam asti iti kārya anupalambha jam dvitīyam iti 
DhPr_136.1–136.2	 vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhim vyākhyātum āha pratiṣedhya ityādi pūrvavat dharmyādi pradarśanam atra api viśiṣṭāt vahneḥ iti draṣṭavyam asya api prayoga viṣayam āha yatra iti katham tayoḥ adṛśya tvam vahneḥ ca dṛśya tvam katham ca na śīta sparśaḥ eva tuṣāra sparśaḥ iti āśaṅkā tritayam apākurvan= āha dūrā iti caḥ hetau niyame vā tayoḥ bhedam upapādayati tuṣārā iti śīta mātram aśīta vyāvṛtti mātram tatas śīta mātrā abhāvāt śīta viśeṣaḥ ca asau tuṣāra sparśaḥ ca iti vigrahaḥ 
DhPr_136.3	 katham tad abhāva niścayaḥ iti āha śīta viśeṣasya iti eṣa ca vāstavaḥ nivṛtti kramaḥ parāmarśa daśāyām darśitaḥ na tu tad prayoga kālikaḥ tathā tve hi na ekam anumānam idam syāt iti ityādinā upasaṃharati itiḥ evam arthe tasmāt arthe vā etena yat yatra niyata saha upalambham tat tatas na bhidyate yathā ekasmāt candramasaḥ dvitīyaḥ candramāḥ niyata saha upalambhaḥ tu nīla ādiḥ jñānena ityādi darśitam draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_136.4–136.6	 kāraṇa anupalabdhim vivariṣuḥ āha pratiṣedhya iti nanu dvayoḥ api tulya sva jñāna janana yogya tā rūpa tvāt tulya dṛśya tvam iti katham asyāḥ prayogaḥ iti āśaṅkya viṣayam asyāḥ darśayitum yatra ityādinā upakramate nanu manaḥ modaka upayoga mātram etat na punar īdṛśaḥ viṣayaḥ asti yatra agniḥ eva dṛśyaḥ na dhūmaḥ iti katham pūrva ukta atikramaḥ iti āha niṣkampa iti hradaḥ jala ādhāra viśeṣaḥ nirgataḥ kampaḥ calanam yasmāt sa tathā sa ca asau= āyataḥ mahān iti tathā sa ca asau salila pūritaḥ ca iti evam vigrahaḥ kāryaḥ āyata grahaṇena hradasya mahat tvāt bāṣpe bhūyas tvam atas eva dhūmasya tatas bhedena anupalakṣaṇam iti darśayati 
DhPr_136.7	 punar kim viśiṣṭe hemante hemanta saṃjñake kāle ucitaḥ adhikṛtaḥ ca asau bāṣpaḥ ca iti tathā tasya udgamaḥ ūrdhvam gamanam yasmin yasmāt vā sa tathā kāla viśeṣe api asyāḥ prayogaḥ iti darśayati virale sandhyā kāla ucitam tamaḥ sandhyātamaḥ tasmin virale manda pracāre kutra hrade tathāvidhe ca tamasi sati itiḥ tasmāt vahneḥ api tatra iyam gatiḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha vahniḥ tu iti tuḥ pūrvavat ambhasaḥ iti ṣaṣṭhī punar ṣaṣṭhyata sartha ityādinā upari śabdasya ātasartha pratyaya anta tvāt tathā hi ūrdhvaṃrdhva śabdāt upari upariṣṭāt itirit pratyayaḥ nipātitaḥ tena eva sūtreṇa ūrdhva śabdasya upādeśaḥ api 
DhPr_137.1–137.2	 plavamānaḥ avatiṣṭhamānaḥ aneka artha tvāt dhātoḥ gacchan= iti vā sva rūpeṇa jvālā rūpeṇa ādhāra rūpeṇa indhana niviṣṭena itiḥ hetau tatra tasmin sthāna viśeṣe asya kāraṇa anupalambhasya tamisrāyām eva tu rātrau nirādhārake pradeśe kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ prayogaḥ sukaraḥ tatra vahneḥ dṛśya tvāt dhūmasya sataḥ api adṛśya tvāt anena punar evaṃvidham viṣayam parityajya anyam viṣayam upapādayatā kim iti ātmā aayāsitaḥ iti na pratīmaḥ 
DhPr_137.3–137.5	 evam tu prayogaḥ kāryaḥ yatra yasya kāraṇam na asti na tat tatra asti yathā bīja abhāve a ṅkuraḥ na asti ca atra dhūmasya kāraṇam vahniḥ iti etena yatra yatra vijñānasya kāraṇam vijñānam na asti na tatra vijñānam upapadyate yathā upala śakale na asti ca prāk bhavīyam vijñānam kalala avasthāyām iti kāraṇa anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ sūcitaḥ tulya nyāya arthaḥ kāraṇa viruddha upalabdhim vyākhyātum āha pratiṣedhyasya iti pūrvavat dharmyādi pradarśanam udbhedaḥ pulakaḥ iti arthaḥ dantavīṇā adhara upari sthita danta paṅktibhyām satvaram abhihanyamānābhyām kaṭa kaṭa karaṇam ādi śabdena śarīra kampasya grahaṇam sukhāt iti ādi graheṇa harṣa vīra rasayoḥ grahaṇam 
DhPr_138.1–138.3	 kim śīta nivarttanā akṣamaḥ api asti dahanaḥ yena tatas viśiṣyate iti āha kaścid iti sannihitaḥ dahana viśeṣaḥ yasya iti vigṛhṇan sannihitaḥ ca asau dahana viśeṣaḥ ca iti yat anyena vyākhya tam tat apahastayati tadā hi vyadhikaraṇa asiddhaḥ hetuḥ syāt iti kva punar asyāḥ prayogaḥ iti āha yatra iti nanu śīta sparśa roma harṣa viśeṣāṇām adṛśya tve katham vahneḥ dṛśya tvam iti āha rūpā iti hiḥ yasmāt itiḥ evam anantara uktena nyāyena tatra viśeṣe asya kāraṇa viruddha upalambhasya eṣa tu prayogaḥ abhidhānīyaḥ yatra yad kāraṇa viruddham asti na tat tatra asti yathā śleṣma viruddhe pitte na ślaiṣmikaḥ vyādhiḥ asti ca romaharṣa ādi kāraṇa viruddhaḥ vahniḥ atra iti 
DhPr_138.4–138.5	 etat api atyanta abhyāsāt jhaṭiti sannihita dahana viśeṣa tva avagama mātre roma harṣa ādi viśeṣa abhāva pratīti udaye sati ekam ācāryeṇa uktam dharma uttareṇa api tathā vyākhyāyate iti draṣṭavyam anyathā tu viruddha upalambha kāraṇa anupalambha sambhave dve ime anumāne tathā hi yatra vahniḥ na tatra śīta sparśaḥ iti viruddha upalambha jam ekam anumānam yatra śīta sparśa abhāvaḥ na tatra tad kārya romaharṣa ādi iti kāraṇa anupalambha jam dvitīyam iti pratiṣedhyasya ityādinā kāraṇa viruddha kārya upalabdhim vyācaṣṭe pūrvavat dharmyādi pradarśanam 
DhPr_138.6^1	 roma harṣa ādi viśeṣaiḥ yuktaḥ ca asau puruṣaḥ ca iti karmadhārayam kṛtvā sa vidyate yatra sa tat vān iti śāntabhadreṇa vyākhyātam tat ca avadyam yatas karma dhāraya mat tvarthīyāt bahuvrīhiḥ eva lāghavena iti vacanāt romaharṣa ādi viśeṣa yuktaḥ puruṣaḥ yatra iti evam viśiṣṭe pradeśe avagate kim matvarthīyena iti manyamānaḥ mahāvaiyākaraṇaḥ ayam dharma uttaraḥ prāhaḥ yogaḥ yuktam iti bhāve niṣṭhā yadi evam kṛṣṇaḥ sarpaḥ yasmin valmīke lohitaḥ śāliḥ yasmin grāme gauraḥ kharaḥ yasmin= araṇyaḥ iti bahu vrīhiṇā bhavitavyam tatas ca kṛṣṇam arpavān valmīkaḥ lohita śālimān grāmaḥ gaurakhara vat araṇyam iti na syāt 
DhPr_138.6^2	 sādhavaḥ ca amī prayogāḥ tat katham anena evam vyākhyātam iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ yasmāt karma dhārayam atvarthīyāt bahuvrīhiḥ lāghavena iti idam vacanam saṃjñā śabdam varjayitvā veditavyam saṃjñā śabdāḥ ca ete kṛṣṇa sarpa lohita śāli gaura khara śabdāḥ iti sādhu uktam yogaḥ yuktam iti roma harṣa ādi viśeṣa yuktam iti roma harṣa ādi viśeṣa yogaḥ iti arthaḥ tasya tad yuktasya tad yogasya sambandhī sambandhi iti anena sambandha ṣaṣṭhī iyam samasyate iti darśayati yatas ayam roma harṣa ādi viśeṣa yogaḥ sva ātmanā puruṣam vyavacchinatti tatas vyavacchedakaḥ san puruṣam sva sambandhinam upapādayati 
DhPr_139.1–139.2	 kadā ayam prayogaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iti āha trayāṇām iti vahni śīta sparśa roma harṣa ādi viśeṣāṇām apiḥ avadhāraṇe kasmāt evam iti āha romaharṣa ādi viśeṣasya ityādi hi śabda arthaḥ ca atra arthāt draṣṭavyaḥ yatas evam tasmāt ayam iti ayam api iti draṣṭavyam kva punar trayāṇām apratyakṣa tvam dhūmasya tu pratyakṣa tvam iti āha tatra iti vākya upakṣepe vidyamānāḥ api apratyakṣāḥ yadi abhaviṣyan niyatam upālapsyanta iti sambhāvanām ativṛttāḥ dūra sthasya iti hetu bhāvena viśeṣaṇam tatas ayam arthaḥ dūra stha tvāt pratipattuḥ te santaḥ api apratyakṣāḥ iti 
DhPr_139.3–140.1	 tatra sthāne etat kāraṇa viruddha kārya rūpam sādhanam pramāṇam iti anumāna ākhya pramāṇa jana kavāt adūra stha tve tu pratipattuḥ prākāra ādi vyavahita uddeśe ayam prayogaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ dhūma śabdena viśiṣṭaḥ dhūmaḥ vivakṣitaḥ iti darśayati dhūmaḥ tu iti tuśabdaḥ viśeṣa arthaḥ etat eva vyatireka mukheṇa draḍhayan= āha dhūma mātreṇa iti tuḥ pūrvasmāt vaidharmyam āha itiḥ hetau dvitīyaḥ itiḥ evam arthaḥ prayogaḥ punar īdṛśaḥ vācyaḥ yatra yad kāraṇa viruddha kāryam asti tatra tat na asti yathā rudita viśeṣe sati na smita viśeṣaḥ roma harṣa ādi viśeṣa yukta puruṣavat tva kāraṇa śīta sparśa viruddha vahni kāryañca atra dhūmaḥ iti 
DhPr_140.2	 etat api atyanta abhyāsāt jhaṭiti dhūma darśanena roma harṣa ādi yukta puruṣa vattva abhāva pratīti udaye sati kāraṇa virudva kārya upalabdhi jam ekam anumānam uktam ācāryeṇa iti draṣṭavyam anyathā kārya hetu viruddha upalambha kāraṇa anupalambha sambhavāni trīṇi amūni anumānāni tathā hi tadā iyam paripāṭiḥ yatra dhūmaḥ tatra agniḥ iti kārya hetu jam ekam anumānam yatra vahniḥ na tatra śīta sparśaḥ iti viruddha upalambha jam dvitīyam yatra śīta sparśa abhāvaḥ na tatra tad kārya roma harṣa ādi viśeṣa yukta puruṣa bhāvaḥ iti kāraṇa anupalambha jam tṛtīyam iti 
DhPr_140.3	 ete ca prakārāḥ anupalabdheḥ upalakṣaṇam veditavyāḥ anyāsām api vidhāna sambhavāt tathā hi vyāpaka viruddha kārya upalabdhiḥ api asti yathā ātra tuṣāra sparśaḥ dhūmāt iti kārya viruddha kārya upalabdhiḥ api asti yathā na iha apratibaddha sāmarthyāni śīta kāraṇāni santi dhūmāt iti vyāpaka viruddha vyāpta upalabdhiḥ api asti yathā na ayam nityaḥ kadācid kārya kāri tvāt iti pratiṣedhyasya nitya tvasya vyāpakam niratiśaya tvam tasya viruddham sa atiśaya tvam tena vyāptam kadācid kārya kāri tvam iti āsāñca yathāsvam yathāyogam prayogāḥ svayam ūhyāḥ 
DhPr_141.1–141.2	 kecid tu na iha apratibaddha sāmarthyāni vahni kāraṇāni santi tuṣāra sparśāt iti kārya viruddha vyāpta upalabdhim icchanti na atra dhūmaḥ tuṣāra sparśāt iti kāraṇa viruddha vyāpta upalabdhim api iti sā ca prayoga bhedāt ekādaśa prakāra iti yat uktam tat asahamānaḥ codayati yadi iti atra dvau vastu sādhanau= ekaḥ pratiṣedha hetuḥ iti anena ekaḥ pratiṣedha hetuḥ uktaḥ iti codayituḥ āśayaḥ kāryā ityādinā daśagrahaṇasya tātparya artham vyācaṣṭe api śabdaḥ śaṅkāyām sarva grahaṇasya api tātparya artham āha tatra iti vākya upanyāse apiḥ pūrvavat udāhṛtaḥ eva udāhṛta mātrāṇi teṣām anena dravya kārtsnya vṛttaḥ sarva śabdaḥ gṛhītaḥ iti darśitam 
DhPr_141.3	 tarhi sarva grahaṇam eva astu kim daśagrahaṇena iti āha daśa iti prayukta udāharaṇa kārtsnyam gamyeta iti loke sarve padātayaḥ atra yoddhāraḥ ityādau sarva śabdasya upadarśita kārtsnya vṛttasya darśanāt uktam yadi evam daśagrahaṇe api evam kim na syāt iti āha daśagrahaṇāt iti turdaśa grahaṇa rahita pakṣāt vaidharmyam āha atiricyamānam adhikībhavat gata artham sat iti yāvat upadarśita tulya avabodhāya sampadyate 
DhPr_141.4	 syāt etat ime sarve daśa anupalabdhi prayogāḥ iti etāvatā eva kiyatām grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ nirākṛtaḥ eva iti katham kārya anupalabdhi ādi grahaṇam ācāryasya na atiricyate katham ca dharma uttarasya eṣā tātparya artha vyākhyā tat kiyatām api prasaktaḥ āha iti aparyālocita vyākhyānam na bhavati iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ tathā hi prāktana ekādaśa grahaṇasya upalakṣaṇa artha tvena anyeṣām api vyāpaka viruddha vyāpta upalabdhi ādi prayogāṇām abhimata tvāt ādyān kāryā a nupalabdhi ādi prayogān vihāya daśa saṃkhyā pūraṇam kṛtam bhavati eva iti tad āśaṅkā nivṛtti artham kārya anupalabdhi ādi grahaṇam kṛtam ācāryeṇa dharma uttareṇā api tathā vyākhyātam iti na tarhi daśagrahaṇam karttavyam iti ced na asya upalakṣaṇa artha tvāt adoṣaḥ eṣaḥ katham saṅgraham antarbhāvam gacchanti iti āha tādātmyena iti tasyāḥ svabhāva anupalabdheḥ ātmā tad ātmā tasya bhāvaḥ tena svabhāva anupalabdhi tvena anupalabdhi svabhāvāḥ iti arthaḥ iti idam spaṣṭīkaraṇam api svabhāva anupalabdhi smāraka tvena tad svabhāvāḥ iti draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_142.1	 reva kim na śabda ākhyā yatas iti ced na pāramparya grahaṇa vyāghāta prasaṅgāt na sākṣāt ete ityādi vakṣyamāṇa dharma uttarīya vyākhyāna vyāghāta prasaṅgāt ca iti śabdasya vyāpāraḥ abhidhā lakṣaṇaḥ tasya bhede bhidyamāna tve api svabhāva viruddha ādi ityādi grahaṇena kāraṇa viruddha ādīnām grahaṇam kārya anupalabdhi ādi iti ādi grahaṇena vyāpaka anupalabdhi ādīnām grahaṇam artha antara vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām iti mūle karaṇa tṛtīyāt vivacana antam etat iti darśayan= āha artha antara iti caḥ tulya bala tvam samuccinoti bhidyante nānā rūpāḥ bhavanti prayoga antareṣu iti antara śabdaḥ anya vacanaḥ svabhāva anupalabdhi apekṣayā paramparā paripāṭiḥ sā eva pāramparyam iti svārthikaḥ pratyayaḥ etat eva spaṣṭayati praṇālikayā iti 
DhPr_142.2	 nanu yadi amīṣām dṛśya anupalabdhau= antarbhāvaḥ tadā sākṣāt tat abhidhānam tathā tve ca katham pāramparyeṇa iti āśaṅkya āha etat uktam bhavati yadi na abhidadhati tadā na sākṣāt iti na karttavyam saṅgrahaḥ ca katham iti āha dṛśyā iti tuḥ viśeṣa arthe yasmāt arthe vā vidhim agni ādeḥ niṣedham vyāpaka ādeḥ cakāraḥ vā śabda arthe tatas tad avyabhicāri vidhi niṣedha abhidhānāt na sākṣāt na avi avadhānena artha antara vidhi pratiṣedhayoḥ ca dṛśya anupalambhāvi abhicāri tvam kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādi grahaṇa kāla pravṛtta dṛśya anupalambha smāraka ādi draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_143.1–143.2	 eṣa bhedaḥ iti svabhāva anupalabdhi ādi rūpaḥ kasmāt tatra vācyaḥ iti āha śabda iti hiḥ yasmāt śabda bhedaḥ trirūpa liṅga vākya nānātvam yadi api evam tathā api katham tatra vaktavyaḥ iti āha śabdaḥ ca iti caḥ hetau śāstra paripaṭhitānām iti śāstra paripaṭhita dvāreṇa parijñātānām svabhāva ādi anupalabdhi ādi vācakānām vākyānām iti draṣṭavyam upalambhaḥ dvividhaḥ vācya rūpaḥ vācaka rūpaḥ ca atas eva āvarttanam api dvedhā śabda rūpāvarttanam artha āvarttanam ca tatra arthāvarttanam punar punar cetasi niveśanam śabda āvarttanam punar punar uccāraṇam 
DhPr_143.3–143.4	 mūle svayaṃśabdaḥ ātmanaḥ iti ṣaṣṭhī arthe varttamānaḥ gṛhītaḥ iti āśayena āha pratipattuḥ ātmanaḥ iti sva artha anumāna prastāvāt pratipattṛ śabdena yaḥ tri rūpeṇa liṅgena parokṣam artham pratipadyate sa gṛhyate api śabdāt paraḥ api tasmāt pratipadyate iti sambandhanīyam mūle tu na kevalam parasya iti yojanīyam anantara uktena paripaṭhita svabhāva anupalabdhi ādi sūcitena svabhāva anupalabdhi ādi prayoga krameṇa yatas iti śabdaḥ tasmāt arthe tat tasmāt ayam vakṣyamāṇaḥ arthaḥ tasmāt śabdena yasmai cśabdasya anvayāt yasmāt iti uktam anena svabhāva anupalabdhi ādi prayoga lakṣaṇena upāyena pratipadyate iti āśaṅkya pūrvam eva smarayati prayogā abhyāsāt iti 
DhPr_143.5	 syāt matam na svayam uccaritaḥ śabdaḥ tat pratipatteḥ nimittam pratipanne śabda prayogāt anyathā pratiniyata prayoga ayogāt tat katham piṣṭa peṣaṇa kārī śabdaḥ upāya tvena ucyate iti na etat asti yatas liṅga darśanena anyatas vā nimittāt prabuddha vāsanaḥ manda pracāra artha smaraṇaḥ a tyanta abhyasta prayogaḥ tathāvidha prayogam uccārya evam tattvam avagāhamānaḥ tad artham pratipadyate yathā kaścid abhyāsāt sati dharmiṇi dharmāṇām loke cintā pravarttate iti uccārya eva asya artham pratipadyate tadvat trirūpa ākhyānam vākyam uccārya eva kaścid abhyasta prayogaḥ parokṣam artham pratipadyate tatas ayam upāyaḥ bhavati eva 
DhPr_143.6–144.1	 tatas parasya api prati iti udayāt para artha anumānam api syāt iti ced bhavatu kā kṣatiḥ sva pratipatti prayojanam satsva artha anumānam tadā eva ca tena anyaḥ pratipadyate iti para pratipatti prayojanam sat para artha anumānam atas evam aśabdaḥ api kaścid niyataḥ asti iti avācāma iti kecid punar evam vyācakṣate svayam ityādinā granthena vārttika kṛtā idam uktam svabhāva ādīnām anupalabdhyā viruddha ādīnāñca upalabdhyā yathāyogam abhāvam tat vyavahāram ca prayoga nirapekṣaḥ eva pratipattā pratyeti na kevalam prayoga abhyāsāt pratipatti samayaḥ eva prayogam uccārayati na tu tatas apūrvam avagacchati itarathā pratiniyata śabda uccāraṇam na bhavet iti anena upāyena iti ca upāyaḥ iha upāyaḥ tathā śabda uccāraṇa kramaḥ tena iti varṇayanti etena ca anupalabdhi prayoga samarthana nyāyena 
DhPr_145.1–145.3	 anye punar anyathā vyavasthitāḥ svayam api iti ādikam na āvirbhūta prayogam adhikṛtya uktam kintu antar jalpa ākāra pravṛttam sva pratipatti kāla bhāvinam iti atra ca sādhu asādhu vā vyākhyānam sādhubhiḥ eva jñātavyam iti syāt etat yathā prayoga bhedaḥ sva artha anumāne kathyate tathā ca na kiñcid vācyam para artha anumāne syāt iti āśaṅkya āha yat punar iti para pratipattau= eva na tu sva pratipattau= api iti avadhāraṇa arthaḥ 
DhPr_145.4–145.6	 samprati dṛśya anupalabdhau= antarbhāvam sarvān upalabdhīnām asahamānaḥ āha nanu ca iti tathā ca sati kāraṇa ādīnām adṛśyānām niṣedha prakāre sati śiṣṭeṣu pariśiṣṭeṣu abhāvaḥ iti abhāva upīti draṣṭavyam na tu abhāvaḥ eva vyavahārasya api sādhanāt kāraṇa ādi anupalabdhyā ca karaṇa bhūtayā kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādi grahaṇa kāle yā upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca pūrvam āsīt tadvatām pratiṣedhaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ dṛśyānām eva kṛtaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ jñātavyaḥ yathā artha virodha ādi grahaṇa kāle avaśyaṃbhāvinī dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ tathā anantaram eva dharma uttareṇa prasādhayiṣyate 
DhPr_145.7–145.8	 nanu ca kāraṇa ādīnām ca iti anena cakāreṇa avaśyam samuccaya arthena bhāvyam tat katham hetu arthe vyākhyāyate iti āśaṅkya pūrvam buddhi stham spaṣṭayan= āha bahuṣu iti evam manyate samuccaya arthe varttamānaḥ eva ayam hetu arthe varttate na tu evam samuccaya arthaḥ nirākriyate hetūnām paraspara samuccayasya pratīyamāna tvāt tathā sa na hetu arthaḥ bhavati itiḥ evam cakārasya arthaḥ prayojanam 
DhPr_146.1–146.3	 viruddha śabdena pratiṣedhyasya viruddham grāhyam ādi śabdena viruddha kārya ādīnām grahaṇam yeṣām ekadā upalabdhiḥ tebhyaḥ anye anupalabdhāḥ eva kadācid kvacid ajñātāḥ eva vyāpakasya abhāve abhāvaḥ ca vyāpyasya na siddhi iti yasmāt ayam āśayaḥ yadi pūrvam vyāpaka abhimatasya abhāve vyāpya abhimata abhāvaḥ niścitaḥ bhavet tadā vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ siddhyet tadā ca vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ gamikā syāt na anyadā iti ayam atra prakaraṇa arthaḥ prabandhena bhavataḥ yad bhāve yasya abhāvaḥ tasya virodha gatiḥ yat svabhāvaḥ ca yena upalabhyate tena saha kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ api pañca pratyakṣa anupalambha samadhigamyaḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvaḥ api pratyakṣa anupalambha avaseyaḥ iti katham adṛśyasya siddhyanti iti 
DhPr_146.4	 nanu bhavantu te anyatra dṛśyāḥ tatra tāvat adṛśyāḥ eva vaktavyāḥ dṛśya tve dṛśya anupalambha prayogāt tat katham dṛśya anupalabdhau= itarāsām anupalabdhīnām antarbhāvaḥ iti āśaṅkya tathā tatra antarbhāvaḥ tathā darśayitum āha tat iti yasmāt anyatra dṛśya tve api viruddha ādīnām dṛśya anupalambhe antarbhāvaḥ na ghaṭate sa ca ācāryeṇa uktaḥ tat tasmāt ayam arthaḥ sarvatra ca iti ādeḥ vākyasya tātparya arthaḥ katham dṛśya anupalabdheḥ iti amum artham tāvat prasādhayati ekā iti 
DhPr_146.5–147.1	 kārya kāraṇa bhāve kā vārtā iti āha kāraṇa iti yadi evam vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvasya kā gatiḥ iti āha vyāpaka iti nanu ca vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva niścaye tayoḥ eka tvāt kim abhāva niścayena iti āha tatra vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva niścaye karttavye katham abhāva pratītiḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva pratīteḥ nimittam iti āha iha iti āstām sarvatra virodha ādau= abhāva pratītiḥ dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ tu kva upayujyate iti āha abhāva iti caḥ hetau 
DhPr_147.2	 nanu yadi nāma virodha ādi grahaṇa kāle dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ āsīt tathā api na sā viruddha upalabdhi vyāpaka anupalabdhi ādi prayoga viṣaye samprati anuvarttate tat katham viruddha upalabdhi ādīnām tatra antarbhāvaḥ iti āha tasmāt iti yatas abhāva pratītim antareṇa na virodha ādi siddhiḥ abhāva siddhiḥ ca dṛśya anupalabdheḥ tasmāt hetoḥ virodha ādikam smaratā iti viruddha upalambha vyāpaka anupalambha ādi prayoga kālaḥ iti draṣṭavyam tat asmaraṇe hi yatas viruddhādiḥ iha asti yatas ayam vyāpaka ādiḥ na asti tasmāt tat tat na asti iti asyāḥ pratīteḥ ayogāt iti api draṣṭavyam smaratā iti ca tadānīm virodha ādeḥ grahaṇāt gṛhītasya eva vikalpanāt uktam kutas punar avaśya smarttavyā sā iti āha dṛśyā iti 
DhPr_147.3–147.4	 atha syāt prāktanī dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ sadā smaryatām tathā api katham asau vivakṣita abhāva siddhau= upayogam bhajate yena ātmani itarāḥ anupalabdhīḥ antar bhāvayati iti āha virodha iti caḥ yasmāt tasyām niyata smaraṇāyām satyām nanu viruddha upalabdhi kāraṇa ādi anupalabdhi prayoga viṣaye sā na asti tat katham avidyamānā sā eva abhāva pratīteḥ nibandhanam iti āha tatra iti vākya upanyāse samprati idānīm smaryamāṇā sā eva abhāva pratīteḥ nibandhanam viruddha ādi abhāva jñānasya karaṇam 
DhPr_147.5–147.6	 katham tarhi dṛśya anupalabdheḥ viruddha upalabdhi ādīnām bhedaḥ iti āha tatas iti tatas virodha ādi grahaṇa kāla pravṛttāyāḥ dṛśya anupalabdheḥ smaryamāṇa tvāt samprati sā na asti itiḥ tasmāt atra abhāvaḥ sādhyate tena abhāva sādhana tvena tatas bhidyante viruddha upalabdhi ādi prayogāḥ viruddha vidhinā ityādinā uktam artham upasaṃharati viruddha vidhinā iti upalakṣaṇama viruddha kārya ādi vidhinā api dṛśya anupalambha ākṣepāt anyathā tāsām tatra antarbhāvaḥ na syāt 
DhPr_147.7–147.9	 nanu svātantryeṇa tvayā tasyāḥ eva prāc pravṛttāyāḥ abhāva niścayaḥ darśitaḥ tatra ca anupalabdhīnām antarbhāvaḥ na tu ācāryasya ayam abhipretaḥ iti āśaṅkya ācāryasya eva ayam abhipretaḥ arthaḥ iti darśayan= āha tat anena iti anena ime sarve ityādinā vyāpaka bhāva asiddheḥ iti antena yadi sākṣāt tasyām antarbhāvaḥ tadā daśyā anupalabdhiḥ syāt na biruddha upalabdhi ādi bhedaḥ iti āha pāramparyeṇa iti viruddha ādi prayoga kāle na sā asti kevalam prāc pravṛttā sā smaryate iti ayam atra prakaraṇa arthaḥ dṛśya anupalambhasya avaktavya tvena daśānām api anupalabdha ūnām tatra antarbhāvaḥ viruddha ādi a bhāva pratītau= anupayogaḥ ca iti 
DhPr_148.1	 kecid punar atra evam bruvate iha eka jñāna saṃsargi vaḥ tu antara upalambhaḥ anupalambhaḥ na ca śītasya niṣedhe sādhye dūra tvāt vahneḥ bhāsvara rūpa upalabdhiḥ śīta sparśa anupalabdhiḥ yujyate yena anupalabdhiḥ siddhyet rūpa sparśayoḥ eka jñāna saṃsargi tva abhāvāt na ca virodha grahaṇa kāla pravṛtta dṛśya anupalambha smāraka tvena dṛśya anupalambha tvam vācyam prāc pravṛtta pratyakṣa smāraka tvena api pratyakṣa tva prasaṃṅgāt atas eva virodha ādi grahaṇa kāla pravṛtta dṛśya anupalambha smāraka tvena anupalabdhīnām tatra antarbhāvaḥ na yujyate na api smṛtāyāḥ tasyāḥ eva abhāva niścayaḥ vyāpti grāhaka pramāṇa smāraka tvena para artha anumānasya tad pramāṇa antarbhāva prasaṅgāt tatas eva smaryamāṇāt pramāṇāt vivakṣita pratīti prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt sarvatra eva sampratitanaḥ dṛśya anupalambhaḥ darśanīyaḥ tad balena eva abhāva niścayaḥ vācyaḥ na tu prāc pravṛttāt dṛśya anupalambhāt smṛtyā viṣayīkṛtāt abhāva niścayaḥ na api tad smāraka tvena anupalabdhīnām tathātvam iti 
DhPr_148.2	 yadi evam kathaṅkāram sa pradarśyatām iti ced ucyate dūrāt vahne rūpa viśeṣam dṛṣṭvā yatra evaṃvidha rūpa viśeṣaḥ tatra tāvat deśa vyāpakaḥ tuṣāra sparśa viśeṣaḥ asti yathā mahānasa ādau tathāvidham eva rūpam iti ānumānikī viśiṣṭa uṣṇa sparśa pratītiḥ sā eva ca śīta sparśa anupalabdhiḥ uṣṇa śīta sparśayoḥ eka jñāna saṃsargi tvāt vivakṣita upalambhāt anyaḥ upalambhaḥ anupalambhaḥ sa kvacid pratyakṣa ātmā kvacid anumāna ātmā iti na śāstra virodhaḥ na yukti virodhaḥ tatas eva tad dṛśya anupalambhāt śīta sparśa abhāva pratītiḥ 
DhPr_148.3	 āhatya dṛśya anupalabdheḥ anudayāt dṛśya anupalabdheḥ bhedena nirdeśaḥ atas eva ca anumitā anumānam etat kevalam atyanta abhyāsān jhaṭiti tathā apratīti udaye sati ekam anumānam uktam vastutas tu anekam anumānam etat evam vyāpaka viruddha kārya upalabdhi ādau= api sarvam draṣṭavyam tathā ca vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhi ādiṣu aparam anumānam ekam plavamānam avaseyam yayoḥ ca paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇaḥ virodhaḥ tatra dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ sphuṭā eva tena viruddha vyāpta upalabdhi ādiṣu samprati eva dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ asti bhedaḥ tu pāramparyeṇa tad udayāt evam vyāpaka kāraṇa anupalabdhi ādiṣu akāraṇa vyāpaka ādeḥ dharmasya eva anupalambhāt abhāve siddhe tatas eva sāmarthyāt kārya ādeḥ abhāva avasāyaḥ iti idānīntanasya eva dṛśya anupalambhasya upayogaḥ na prāktanasya smṛti ādi viṣayīkṛtasya dṛśya anupalambhasya ca sākṣātkāraṇe vyāpārāt pāramparyeṇa ca viruddha ādi abhāve bhāve vyāpārāt dṛśya anupalabdheḥ bhedena kāraṇa anupalabdhi ādīnām prayogaḥ iti 
DhPr_149.1–149.3	 samprati adṛśya anupalabdhim adhikṛtya uktam vyācakṣāṇaḥ āha uktā iti nanu yadi pratyakṣā anumāna nivṛtti mātra rūpā adṛśya anupalabdhiḥ abhāve sādhye saṃśaya hetuḥ anaikāntikī tarhi sā tatas ca hetvābhāsa avasaraḥ eva vaktavyā tat kim iha uccayate iti ced na etat asti yatas na sā vacana vyaktyā anupalabdhi kṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ asat vyavahāre sādhye na pramāṇam aikāntika sat vyavahāra niṣedhe tu pramāṇam iti pradarśanāt na jñāna jñeya svabhāva iti yāvat itya artham nyāyam āśritya uktam na śābdam iti draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_149.4	 yadi pramāṇa nivṛttyā aprameya anivṛttiḥ tarhi tad sattayā api na prameya sattā siddhyet iti āśaṅkya tatra upapattim darśayan= āha yat punar iti nanu kāraṇam api avaśyam kārya vat bhavati tatas ca sati jñeye jñānena api avaśya bhāvyam tat ced na asti jñeyam api na asti eva tatas siddhyati evā adṛśyasya api abhāvaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha na tu iti tunā kārya dharmāt kāraṇa dharmasya vaidharmyam āha etat ca kāraṇa mātra abhiprāyeṇa uktam tathā cait tathā prāk eva nirṇītam tasmāt ityādinā asya eva prakṛtasya upasaṃhāraḥ iti 
DhPr_150.1–150.3	 trirūpam liṅgam jñātam api vaktum aviduṣaḥ bālasya vyutpādana artham trirūpa liṅga ākhyāna lakṣaṇam yat para artham anumānam uktam tat vyākhyātum sva artha ityādinā prastauti dvayoḥ rūpayoḥ abhidhānāt ekasya gamyamāna tvāt ākhyāyate prakāśyate anena iti trirūpam liṅgam iti vivṛtam na tu abhidhīyate anena iti abhidheyasya gamyamānasya ca prakāśya tvam tulyam iti prakāśyate iti anena dvayoḥ saṅgrahaḥ yena artha krameṇa ātmanaḥ parokṣa artha jñānam utpannam tena eva krameṇa para santāne liṅgi jñāna utpipādayiṣayā trirūpasya liṅgasya khyāpakam yat vacanam tad para artham anumānam iti draṣṭavyam kāraṇe vacane kāryasya jñānasya upacārāt samāropāt katham punarvacanasya anumāna hetu tvam iti āha trirūpā iti 
DhPr_151.1	 nanu ca trirūpa liṅga abhidhānāt avagate sati dharmiṇi liṅgam jñāyate tasya tu vyāptiḥ smaryate tat katham trirūpa liṅga vacanāt tad smṛtiḥ utpadyate iti ucyate iti ced ucyate gṛhyamāṇam api dhūma ādi vastu na tāvat liṅgam yāvat vahni ādi sādhyāvinābhūta tayā na jñāyate tathā tvam ca tasya na tadā grāhyam api tu pūrva gṛhītam eva smarttavyam iti sūktam trirūpa liṅga smṛtiḥ utpadyate iti smṛteḥ iti pakṣa dharma grahaṇa sahitāyāḥ iti draṣṭavyam 
DhPr_151.2–151.3	 ayam arthaḥ vacanam api trirūpam liṅgam smarayat parokṣa artha jñānasya paramparayā kāraṇam bhavat upacārāt anumānam ucyate iti atha ābādhita tva ādi api liṅgasya lakṣaṇam iti ācakṣate kecid iti vipratipatti darśanāt tad vyutpādanam yuktam na tu tad vacanam tasya vipratipatti abhāvāt iti ced na atra api avyāpti vyatirekābhyām nigadantaḥ vipratipannāḥ iti asya api vyutpādanam nyāyyam 
DhPr_151.4–151.5	 athā api syāt yadi paramparayā anumāna hetu tvena vacanam upacārāt anumānam iti vyutpādyate tarhi jijñāsā svāsthi ādikam api paramparayā anumāna hetu tvāt anumāna śabdena vaktum śakyam iti tat api kim na ucyate iti āha na yāvat iti nanu svāsthya ādikam api nimittam iti tad avasthaḥ doṣaḥ na nimittam vyākhpeyam iti avyahitam asādhāraṇam nimittam ākhyeyam iti arthaḥ 
DhPr_151.6	 nanu svayam pratītam liṅgam anumānasya nimittam tat kim tat vacanena vyākhyātena iti āha tat ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe vā śabdaḥ vikalpa arthaḥ yatas pareṇa pratipāditam api tad liṅgam anumānasya nimittam tatas tasmāt avaśyam vaktavyam pratipādakam liṅga pratipādakam vacanam darśayan= anumāna śabdena uktavān ācāryaḥ 
DhPr_152.1–152.3	 anena etat āha na svāsthya ādi pratipannam api parokṣa artha pratipādakam yena tat ucyeta tat vacanam avaśyam darśayitavyam anumāna śabdena abhilapyeta svayam aśaktam api tu hetu vacanam parokṣa prakāśana vastu sūcaka tvāt anumāna śabdena uktam iti iti parama arthaḥ evam asya upacārasya paramaḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ arthaḥ prayojanam vidha śabdena ca vigṛhṇataḥ abhiprāyaḥ prāk eva pradarśitaḥ abhidhānam artha prakāśanam 
DhPr_153.1	 kena kasya kim kṛtam ca sādharmyam vaidharmyam ca iti āha dṛṣṭānta iti sādṛśyam hetu kṛtam iti hetu sadbhāva dvārakam asādṛśyam ca hetu kṛtam iti hetu sadbhāva asadbhāva dvārakam draṣṭavyam vatu bartham prayojayitum āha tatra iti vākya upanyāse yasya vākyasya sādharmya sādṛśyam abhidheyam asti etat eva udāharaṇena darśayan= āha yathā iti yat kṛtakam iti yat yat kṛtakam iti vīpsā arthom vivakṣitaḥ tat iti atra api tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti pakṣa dharma tā kathanam idam na tu evam pakṣa dharmaḥ darśanīyaḥ kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti etāvatā eva gata artha tvena tathā aśabdasya vaiyarthyāt tatas kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti eva darśanīyaḥ itarathā pareṣām iva upanaya prayogaḥ syāt sa ca ayuktaḥ iti yat nityam iti sādhya abhāva anuvādaḥ tat akṛtakam iti sādhana abhāva vidhiḥ 
DhPr_153.2–153.3	 abhidheyam bhinnam iti bruvataḥ ayam āśayaḥ sādharmya vat prayogasya anvayaḥ pakṣa dharma tā ca abhidheyāḥ abhinnam sādhāraṇam prakāśyam dvayoḥ prayogayoḥ arthaḥ prayojana vāci ācāryeṇa uktaḥ na abhidheya vācī iti darśayati yat uddiśya iti spaṣṭayan prayujyate a nena iti prayojanam sādhana vākyasya pravarttakam liṅgavastu uktam na phalam prayojanam iti darśayati prakāśayitavyam rūpa traya yogi liṅgam tat ca abhinnam sādhāraṇam dvayoḥ api prayogayoḥ dvābhyām api tasya eva pratipādanāt anumāna hetu tvāt anumāne sādharmya vaidharmyavatī vākye kathite tatas iti prayojana samāna adhikaraṇam na hetu padam etat 
DhPr_153.4–153.5	 nanu abhidheyam eva prakāśyam tat katham prakāśya abhedaḥ iti āśaṅkya āha etat uktam bhavati iti anyat prakāśyam iti sāmarthya gamyam prakāśyam na tu tatra abhidhā vyāpāraḥ iti ākūtam tatra iti vākya upakṣepe yadi sādharmya vat vākye anvayaḥ abhidheyaḥ tarhi katham vyatirekaḥ prakāśyatām gataḥ baidharmya vākye ca yadi vyatirekaḥ abhidheyaḥ katham anvayaḥ prakāśyatām āpannaḥ iti āha anvayaḥ iti hiḥ yasmāt vakṣyamāṇena sādharmyeṇa api hī tyādinā pratipādayiṣyamāṇena nyāyena yuktāḥ 
DhPr_154.1–154.2	 syāt matam yayoḥ abhidheyam bhinnam tayoḥ sāmarthya gamyam api avaśyam bhidyate yathā gaṅgāyām ghoṣaḥ kūpe garga kulam iti āśaṅkya āha na ca iti caḥ yasmāt arthe arthaḥ prayojanam yat uddiśya pravṛttam vākyam upapattim āha yasmāt iti ekasya vākyasya divā bhojana abhāvaḥ abhidheyaḥ anyasya rātri bhojanam iti anayoḥ vākyayoḥ abhidheya bhedaḥ asti tasmin sati api yathā bhojana viśiṣṭam devadattasya pīna tvam pratipādyam na bhidyate tadvat atra abhidheyasya anvaya pakṣa dharma tā lakṣaṇasya vyatireka pakṣa dharma tā lakṣaṇasya bhede api gamyamānam ekam abhinnam 
DhPr_154.3	 atha gamyayānam sāmarthyāt pratīyamānam ucyate tat ca dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ bhidyate eva tathā hi divā bhojana niṣedha vākyasya gamyamānam rātri bhojanam rātri bhojana vidhāna vākyasya tu gamyamānam divā bhojana niṣedhanam tathā dārṣṭa antikepi sādharmya vat vākye vyatirekaḥ gamyamānaḥ vaidharmya vat vākye ca anvayaḥ gamyamānaḥ yat ekasya abhidheyam tat ekasya gamyamānam yat anyasya gamyamānam tad itarasya abhidheyam iti saṃkṣepaḥ tatas katham ucyate vākyayoḥ gamyamānam ekam iti kinnā ucyate gamyamāna śabdasya iha anya arthasya vivakṣita tvāt tathā hi gamyamāna śabdena atra abhidheyam sāmarthya prakāśyañca yat tu dvayam pratīyamāna tā mātreṇa upādhinā vivakṣitam tat ca dṛṣṭānta vākyayoḥ bhojana nimitta pīna tva lakṣaṇam dārṣṭa antika vākyayoḥ ca anvayatiḥ eka pakṣa dharmatā ātmaka rūpa traya yoga liṅga lakṣaṇam ekam abhinnam iti anavadyam etat 
DhPr_154.4	 sādharmyam abhidheyam yasya vidyate tad udāharaṇena darśayan= anupalabdhim āha tāvat śabdaḥ krame sa ca dvis āvṛttyā anupalabdhim iti atra api draṣṭavyaḥ tena ayam arthaḥ sādharmya vat tāvat udāharan= anupalabdhim āha paścāt vaidharmya vat udāharan vakṣyati tathā anupalabdhim tāvat āha paścāt svabhāva kārye vakṣyati iti 
DhPr_155.1	 nanu ācāryeṇa eva sādharmya vat vaidharmya vat ca udāhṛtam atra iti kim iti dharma uttareṇa yathā yat kṛtakam ityādinā sādharmya vat vaidharmya vat ca udāhṛtam prāk iti ced na eṣa doṣaḥ dṛṣṭānta sādhya dharmiṇoḥ sādṛśya ākhyam sādharmyam vaisadṛśya ākhyam vaidharmyam ca hetu dvārakam eva na tu sāmānyena anyathā pratiyogi apekṣayā api sādharmyam vaidharmyam ca kenacid ākāreṇa asti iti na tad nirākṛtam syāt iti darśayitum tat udāhṛtam na tu ācāryeṇa na udāhṛtam iti udāhṛtam iti tena atra api ācāryīye nidarśane hetu kṛtam eva tat pratyetavyam vyavasthitam
